# Kerf вҖ” Roadmap

**Status glyphs:** `вң… shipped` В· `рҹҡ§ in flight` В· `рҹ”ҙ not started`

---

## North Star

**The most comprehensive CAD on Earth вҖ” a single tool in which a person can design *anything*.** Mechanical engineering, electronics, PCB, architecture, civil engineering, drafting, jewelry, automotive вҖ” and every other CAD sector, including the small and niche ones. We are doing **everything**. Nothing here is "cut." Lower priority means *later*, not *dropped*.

This is a **priority-ordered** roadmap, not a date-ordered or effort-ordered one. The tiers (P0 вҶ’ P3) express sequence and leverage: which items earn the most credibility per unit of work.

Kerf is dual-licensed: the OSS core (MIT) and the hosted-tier code under `packages/kerf-{billing,cloud}/` + `src/cloud/`.

### Why chat-driven CAD works

Kerf is **chat-driven** CAD. Every capability is designed around one constraint:

> *Can the LLM produce and re-edit this deliverable through a text-native tool, and verify the result?*

Professional CAD is overcomplicated mostly because of command-discovery affordances (ribbons, palettes, wizards) that an LLM does not need. Kerf ships professional **capability** while deliberately not shipping professional **UI complexity**. This makes the roadmap shorter than it looks: many "pro features" are UX wrappers around a parametric core we expose as a text schema + LLM tool + verifier.

**Hard guardrail:** simplification is about *authoring mechanics only*. It is never an excuse to drop a domain or to skimp on correctness, output formats, or standards compliance. Those are *more* important under an LLM, not less.

---

## Platform foundation

The sector work only matters if you **own your work, are not locked in, and can run Kerf wherever you want**. Four commitments, all decided:

1. **Every cloud project is a real git repository** вҖ” `git clone`-able with stock git, no special client. Large or binary files are auto-detected and stored with a small in-git pointer. Version control is two complementary layers: fine-grained automatic file history *and* deliberate, shareable commits with GitHub sync.

2. **One client, cloud by default, easy optional self-host** вҖ” `pip install kerf` for the hosted cloud; `pip install 'kerf[server]'` + bring-your-own-Postgres + `kerf serve` for self-host. Same client, same data model, both paths first-class.

3. **Portability is the anti-lock-in guarantee** вҖ” `kerf sync` mirrors to a local folder with two-way sync; `kerf export` / `kerf import` produce and ingest a plain file tree. Moving a project between cloud and self-host is painless.

4. **A fully-local / offline desktop app is committed but demand-gated** вҖ” portability + two-way sync + easy self-host is the complete launch answer to "I want to own my data." The standalone offline desktop build is sequenced behind real demand.

---

## What shipped

### Latest delta вҖ” 2026-05-31

**ELEC-OPTOCOUPLER-CTR** вң… вҖ” Optocoupler isolation circuit analysis: given LED forward current IF, CTR(min/typ/max), output pull-up R_L, supply Vcc, and load capacitance C_L, computes IC (min/typ/max), saturation threshold IC_sat = Vcc/R_L, saturation verdict, Vout_low = Vce_sat, Vout_high = Vcc, output rise/fall time, and headroom factor. `analyze_optocoupler(OptocouplerSpec, CircuitSpec) -> OptocouplerReport` in `kerf_electronics.optocoupler_ctr`. Dataclasses: `OptocouplerSpec` (model, IF_mA, CTR_min_percent, CTR_typ_percent, CTR_max_percent, Vce_sat_V, IF_max_mA, Vf_typ_V=1.2, t_rise_us_at_Rl=(2.0, 1000)); `CircuitSpec` (Vcc_out_V, R_pullup_ohm, C_load_pF=20.0, R_LED_series_ohm, V_LED_drive_V); `OptocouplerReport` (IC_min_mA, IC_typ_mA, IC_max_mA, IC_saturation_mA, saturated_min_case, Vout_low_V, Vout_high_V, t_rise_us, t_fall_us, headroom_factor_min, warnings, honest_caveat). Algorithm: IC = CTR/100 Г— IF_mA (IEC 60747-5-5 В§6.3); IC_sat = Vcc/R_L Г— 1000 [mA]; saturated_min_case = (IC_min >= IC_sat); headroom = IC_min/IC_sat; t_rise = max(2.2Г—R_LГ—C_L, t_rise_specГ—R_L_actual/R_L_spec) [Вөs]; t_fall = t_rise (symmetric R-C model). Warns: IF > IF_max (over-drive); NOT saturated (IC_min < IC_sat, suggests fix); headroom < 2.0 (aging margin); IF mismatch (circuit-derived IF vs spec IF > 25%). `elec_analyze_optocoupler` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 68 tests green. HONEST: LINEAR CTR MODEL ONLY вҖ” IC = CTR/100 Г— IF; real CTR vs IF is non-linear (peaks at moderate IF, falls at extremes); TEMPERATURE AND LIFETIME DERATING NOT MODELLED вҖ” CTR degrades 30вҖ“50% over LED lifetime at elevated temperature (Avago AN-5078 В§4.3); always derate CTR to the datasheet minimum at maximum rated temperature (NOT the 25В°C value); Vce_sat is a fixed datasheet spec (actual depends on IC + temperature); rise/fall time is an RC estimate (2.2Г—R_LГ—C_L) вҖ” minority-carrier storage NOT modelled; for high-speed designs use t_PLH/t_PHL from the datasheet at exact R_L and V_CC; isolation voltage (V_IORM, IEC 60747-5-5 creepage/clearance) NOT checked. Refs: Vishay Application Note AN-38 "Optocoupler Output Response Time"; Avago/Broadcom Application Note 5078 "Using Optocouplers"; IEC 60747-5-5:2007 В§6.3 вҖ” `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/optocoupler_ctr.py`.

**ELEC-ZENER-TC-DRIFT** вң… вҖ” Zener voltage drift over temperature using temperature coefficient TC (mV/В°C). Models the Vz vs T curve which has a zero-TC crossing near 5.6 V (above: positive TC dominated by avalanche; below: negative TC dominated by Zener tunneling). `compute_zener_drift(ZenerSpec, OperatingSpec) -> ZenerDriftReport` in `kerf_electronics.zener_tc_drift`. Dataclasses: `ZenerSpec` (Vz_nominal_V, TC_mV_per_C, test_current_mA, test_temp_C=25.0); `OperatingSpec` (current_mA, ambient_temp_C_min, ambient_temp_C_max); `ZenerDriftReport` (Vz_at_min_temp_V, Vz_at_max_temp_V, Vz_drift_total_V, Vz_drift_percent, current_dependence_warning, recommendation, honest_caveat). Algorithm: rZвүҲ0.01Г—Vz/Iz_test [О©] (Vishay AN-2014-3 В§2.2); О”Vz_current=rZГ—(Iz_opвҲ’Iz_test) [V]; Vz(T)=(Vz_nom+О”Vz_current)+TCГ—10вҒ»ВіГ—(TвҲ’T_test) [V]; drift_percent=100Г—|Vz(T_max)вҲ’Vz(T_min)|/Vz_nom; current deviation >50% triggers warning. Recommendation: drift>5% вҶ’ suggest 5.6V near-zero-TC Zener (BZX55C5V6, 1N5232B) or bandgap Vref IC (LM4040, ADR4550, LT6656). Physical basis: Zener tunneling (Vz<5V, negative TC, band-gap narrowing вҲӮEg/вҲӮT<0 per Varshni equation); avalanche impact ionisation (Vz>7V, positive TC, phonon scattering reduces carrier mean free path); mixed regime 5вҖ“7V with TCвүҲ0 near 5.6V (device-process-specific). `elec_compute_zener_drift` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: LINEAR TC MODEL ONLY вҖ” real Vz vs T is mildly quadratic in the 5вҖ“7V transition region (second-order deviation Вұ0.1вҖ“0.3 mV / 100В°C, Sze В§4.5 Fig. 4.5-6); TC is current-dependent (Вұ10вҖ“20% at significantly different Iz); part-to-part TC spread Вұ30вҖ“50% for C-suffix Zeners; thermal self-heating NOT modelled (T_j=T_amb+ОёJAГ—P_Z, ОёJA~300вҖ“600В°C/W for DO-35/SOD-80); rZ linearisation valid only within ~50% of Iz_test; zero-TC crossing is device/manufacturer-specific. Refs: S. M. Sze "Physics of Semiconductor Devices" 3e В§4.5; H&H В§2.2.4 Table 2.1; Vishay AN-2014-3 В§2.4; ON AN-961 В§3 вҖ” `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/zener_tc_drift.py`.

**ELEC-ZENER-CLAMP** вң… вҖ” Zener-diode voltage clamp + series resistor design for DC supply rail regulation. `design_zener_clamp(ZenerClampSpec) -> ZenerClampReport` in `kerf_electronics.zener_clamp_design`. Dataclasses: `ZenerClampSpec` (V_in_min_V, V_in_max_V, V_zener_V, I_load_min_A, I_load_max_A, V_zener_tolerance_pct=5.0, I_zener_knee_A=0.001); `ZenerClampReport` (R_series_ohm, R_series_power_W, I_zener_max_A, P_zener_max_W, recommended_zener_package, recommended_R_E12_ohm, regulation_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: R = (V_in_max вҲ’ V_Z) / (I_load_min + I_knee); V_Z_max = V_ZГ—(1+tol/100); I_Z_max = (V_in_max вҲ’ V_Z_max)/R вҲ’ I_load_min; P_Z_design = V_Z Г— I_Z_max Г— 1.25 (25% derating margin per Vishay AN-2014-3 В§3); P_R = (V_in_max вҲ’ V_Z) Г— (I_Z_max + I_load_min). Zener package thresholds: 0.4 W (DO-35/SOD-80, BZX55 series), 0.5 W (DO-41, BZX79), 1 W (DO-41/BZX85, 1N4728вҖ“1N4764), 3 W (DO-201/P600), 5 W (SOT-89/TO-252). E12 series resistor from IEC 60063 (round up for conservative power). `electronics_design_zener_clamp` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 60 tests green. HONEST: SIMPLE LINEAR SHUNT REGULATOR ONLY вҖ” wasted power = (V_in_maxвҲ’V_Z)Г—I_R_total regardless of load draw; at zero load ALL current flows through Zener; for I_load > 100 mA or efficiency-sensitive rails STRONGLY prefer LDO linear regulator (LM1117, MCP1700) or switching buck converter; Zener incremental resistance rZ NOT modelled (О”V_out = rZГ—О”I_Z вҖ” typical rZ 7вҖ“20 О© for 5 V / 400 mW parts вҖ” use TL431 or shunt reference IC for tight regulation); temperature coefficient of V_Z NOT modelled (below ~5 V TC is negative, above ~5.6 V positive; вүҲ5.1 V Zeners have ~0 TC); 25% margin is steady-state вҖ” pulse/transient peaks require JEDEC JESD51-2 transient thermal impedance analysis; static regulation = 2Г—tol% only (dynamic line/load from rZ excluded). Refs: Horowitz & Hill "Art of Electronics" 3e В§2.2.4; Vishay Application Note AN-2014-3 вҖ” `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/zener_clamp_design.py`.

**ELEC-OP-AMP-OFFSET-DRIFT** вң… вҖ” Op-amp input offset voltage and temperature drift calculator for precision instrumentation design. `compute_op_amp_drift(OpAmpSpec, CircuitSpec, error_budget_pct=0.1) -> OpAmpOffsetReport` in `kerf_electronics.op_amp_offset_drift`. Dataclasses: `OpAmpSpec` (Vos_typ_uV, Vos_drift_uV_per_C, T_ambient_min_C, T_ambient_max_C, T_reference_C=25.0); `CircuitSpec` (gain_VV, signal_full_scale_V); `OpAmpOffsetReport` (Vos_at_T_min_uV, Vos_at_T_max_uV, Vos_max_input_referred_uV, Vos_max_output_referred_mV, error_pct_of_FS, within_spec, recommended_op_amp_class, honest_caveat). Algorithm: Vos(T) = Vos_typ + TC_Vos Г— (T вҲ’ T_ref) (TI SLOA069 В§3 Eq. 3-1); worst-case evaluates all 4 (Вұdrift Г— Вұendpoint) combinations and takes max absolute; Vos_max_IR = max(|Vos(T_min)|, |Vos(T_max)|); Vos_OR_mV = gain Г— Vos_max_IR / 1000; error_pct = 100 Г— (Vos_OR_mV/1000) / FS. Class thresholds: "chopper" (TC_Vos вүӨ 0.05 ВөV/В°C, e.g. AD8551, MAX420); "zero-drift" (вүӨ 0.1 ВөV/В°C, e.g. OPA188, LTC2050); "precision" (вүӨ 1.0 ВөV/В°C, e.g. OPA227, LT1012); "standard" (> 1.0 ВөV/В°C). Recommendation: "chopper" when error вүҘ 10Г— budget; "precision" when over budget; confirm class from TC when in budget. Reference design (task spec): Vos=100 ВөV, drift=2 ВөV/В°C, T=[0..70]В°C, gain=100, FS=5V вҶ’ Vos(T_max)=190 ВөV, output=19 mV, error=0.38%. `electronics_compute_op_amp_drift` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: linear drift model ONLY вҖ” Vos(T)=Vos_typ+TC_VosГ—О”T; real drift is non-linear and asymmetric (TI SLOA069 Fig 3-2); Vos_typ is nominal (not guaranteed вҖ” use Vos_max for design margin); **1/f (flicker) noise contribution to DC offset NOT modelled** (can dominate sub-Hz BJT-input amps); **PSRR/CMRR cross-talk effects OUT OF SCOPE** (О”Vos_PSRR = О”VPS/PSRR must be added separately); resistor TC mismatch in feedback network adds gain-drift error not captured. Refs: TI "Op Amp Errors" SLOA069 В§3 Eq. 3-1; Analog Devices AN-580 В§1; OPA188 / AD8551 / LT1012 datasheets вҖ” `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/op_amp_offset_drift.py`.

**ELEC-INDUCTOR-CORE-SAT** вң… вҖ” Inductor core saturation checker. `check_inductor_saturation(InductorCoreSpec, InductorCurrentSpec) -> CoreSaturationReport` in `kerf_electronics.inductor_core_saturation`. Dataclasses: `InductorCoreSpec` (material: "ferrite_3C95"|"ferrite_3F36"|"powdered_iron_-26"|"sendust"|"NiFe50", A_e_mm2, l_e_mm, B_sat_mT, mu_r); `InductorCurrentSpec` (turns_N, I_dc_A, I_ripple_peak_to_peak_A, temperature_C=25.0); `CoreSaturationReport` (B_peak_mT, B_sat_mT, saturation_margin_pct, saturated, recommended_max_I_dc_A, honest_caveat). Algorithm: I_pk = I_dc + I_ripple_pp/2; B_pk = ОјвӮҖВ·Ој_rВ·NВ·I_pk/l_e (Ampere's law, uniform closed path); saturation_margin = (B_sat вҲ’ B_pk)/B_sat Г— 100; saturated = B_pk >= B_sat; recommended_max_I_dc = max(0, 0.99В·B_satВ·l_e/(ОјвӮҖВ·Ој_rВ·N) вҲ’ I_ripple/2). Temperature derating for ferrite materials: piecewise-linear (100В°CвҶ’вҲ’15%, 125В°CвҶ’вҲ’25%, 150В°CвҶ’вҲ’40%, 200В°CвҶ’вҲ’50%) per Ferroxcube 3C95/3F36 datasheets; not applied to powder-iron/Sendust/NiFe. `electronics_check_inductor_saturation` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 26 tests green. HONEST: fringing flux ignored (gapped cores need Dowell/Erickson В§15.3 gap fringing correction); Ој_r assumed constant (real ferrite Ој_r rolls off substantially in the knee region BEFORE B_sat вҖ” model over-estimates B_pk conservatively; use nonlinear B-H curve for precision); non-ferrite B_sat derating NOT modelled; winding IВІR temperature rise NOT accounted; AC core losses (Steinmetz) NOT computed вҖ” `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/inductor_core_saturation.py`. Refs: Erickson "Power Electronics" 3e В§15; McLyman "Transformer and Inductor Design Handbook" 4e В§10; Ferroxcube 3C95/3F36 datasheets; Magnetics Inc. Powder Core Catalog В§3.

**ELEC-FET-SOA-CHECK** вң… вҖ” MOSFET Safe Operating Area (SOA) checker. `check_fet_soa(FETSpec, FETOperatingPoint) -> FETSOAReport` in `kerf_electronics.fet_soa_check`. Dataclasses: `FETSpec` (part_number, V_DSS_max_V, I_D_continuous_A, I_D_pulsed_A, R_DS_on_mOhm, T_J_max_C, R_theta_JA_K_per_W, P_D_max_W); `FETOperatingPoint` (V_DS_V, I_D_A, pulse_duration_ms, duty_cycle, T_ambient_C); `FETSOAReport` (within_soa, P_diss_W, T_junction_estimate_C, soa_violation_modes, headroom_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: P_diss = V_DS Г— I_D Г— duty; T_J = T_amb + P_diss Г— R_ОёJA (Jedec JESD51 single-node); violation checks: V_DSS_exceeded (V_DS > V_DSS_max), I_D_continuous_exceeded (duty==1.0 AND I_D > I_D_continuous), I_D_pulsed_exceeded (duty<1.0 AND I_D > I_D_pulsed), T_J_exceeded (T_J > T_J_max), P_D_exceeded (P_diss > P_D_max); headroom_pct = (1 вҲ’ max(utilisation_ratios)) Г— 100. `electronics_check_fet_soa` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 30 tests green. HONEST: LINEARISED SOA only вҖ” real datasheet SOA curves (IRF Hexfet Designer's Manual В§5 Fig 5-1) are non-linear in the thermal-limited and second-breakdown regions; pulse-width SOA NOT interpolated (short pulses allow higher peak I_DГ—V_DS before the thermal integral exceeds the die's transient thermal capacity); second-breakdown (avalanche/UIS) NOT explicitly modelled as a separate boundary вҖ” for inductive turn-off verify E_AS = ВҪВ·LВ·I_peakВІ < rated E_AS; thermal model is single-node JESD51 steady-state R_ОёJA (not transient Z_ОёJC(t)); R_DS_on is room-temperature datasheet value (actual R_DS_on increases with T_J per Infineon AN 2015-11); switching losses (turn-on, turn-off, gate charge) NOT included in P_diss вҖ” `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/fet_soa_check.py`. Refs: IRF Hexfet Designer's Manual В§5; IPC-9701A; Jedec JESD51-1; Infineon AN 2015-11.

**ELEC-LDO-DROPOUT-CHECK** вң… вҖ” LDO linear regulator dropout and thermal compliance checker. `check_ldo_dropout(LDOSpec) -> LDODropoutReport` in `kerf_electronics.ldo_dropout_check`. Dataclasses: `LDOSpec` (V_out_V, V_in_min_V, V_in_max_V, I_load_A, dropout_voltage_at_max_load_mV, junction_to_ambient_thermal_resistance_K_per_W, T_ambient_C=25, T_max_junction_C=125); `LDODropoutReport` (headroom_min_mV, dropout_compliant, power_dissipation_W, junction_temp_estimate_C, thermal_compliant, efficiency_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: headroom_mV = (V_in_min вҲ’ V_out) Г— 1000; dropout_compliant = headroom_mV > dropout_spec_mV (strict); P_diss = (V_in_max вҲ’ V_out) Г— I_load; T_j = T_ambient + P_diss Г— R_Оёja (Jedec JESD51 single-node); thermal_compliant = T_j < T_max_junction; efficiency = 100 Г— V_out / V_in_max (pessimistic). `electronics_check_ldo_dropout` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 54 tests green. HONEST: quiescent current I_Q NOT included (dominates at light load вҖ” TI Power Ref В§3.2.3); transient headroom NOT checked (PSRR roll-off + input cap droop during load steps; add вүҘ100вҖ“200 mV guard-band per Sandler В§4.4); output capacitor stability NOT verified (ESR window requirement); thermal model is Оёja worst-case (Оёjb+Оёjc paths not modelled); efficiency = V_out/V_in_max ignores I_Q вҖ” `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/ldo_dropout_check.py`. Refs: TI Power Reference Manual В§3; Sandler "Switch-Mode Power Supplies" В§4; Jedec JESD51-1.

**ELEC-DC-DC-CONVERTER-RIPPLE** вң… вҖ” Output voltage ripple О”V_out (peak-to-peak) for a buck DC-DC converter in Continuous Conduction Mode (CCM). `compute_buck_ripple(BuckConverterSpec) -> ConverterRippleReport` in `kerf_electronics.dc_dc_ripple`. Dataclasses: `BuckConverterSpec` (V_in_V, V_out_V, I_load_A, switching_freq_Hz, L_uH, C_out_uF, C_ESR_mOhm); `ConverterRippleReport` (delta_iL_pp_A, delta_V_out_pp_mV, delta_V_capacitor_mV, delta_V_ESR_mV, duty_cycle, output_ripple_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: D = V_out/V_in; О”iL = (V_inвҲ’V_out)В·D/(LВ·f_sw); О”V_cap = О”iL/(8В·CВ·f_sw); О”V_ESR = О”iLВ·ESR; О”V_out = О”V_cap + О”V_ESR (worst-case linear sum per Erickson В§2.4). CCM validity: iL_min = I_load вҲ’ О”iL/2 > 0 flagged; small-ripple approximation warning when О”iL/(2В·I_load) > 30%; ESR-dominance flag when ESR > 1/(4ПҖВ·CВ·f_sw). `electronics_compute_buck_ripple` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: CCM only вҖ” DCM (iL_min < 0) NOT modelled; small-ripple approximation (Erickson В§2.1) breaks above 30% load variation; D = V_out/V_in is ideal (no deadtime, body-diode drop, or min-on-pulse); ESR assumed resistive/frequency-flat (use datasheet ESR at f_sw); О”V_out is pessimistic linear sum (RSS is ~3вҖ“15% less pessimistic) вҖ” `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/dc_dc_ripple.py`. Refs: Erickson "Fundamentals of Power Electronics" 3e В§2.1, В§2.4 Eq 2.34+2.36; Sandler "Power Electronics" В§3; TI SLVA477.

**MOLD-RUNNER-DIAMETER-OPTIMIZE** вң… вҖ” Optimal cold-runner diameter recommendation using the Beaumont (2007) В§6.5 empirical formula D=(W^0.25Г—вҲҡL)/3.7, balancing fill pressure against cold-runner waste. `optimize_runner_diameter(RunnerOptimizeSpec) -> RunnerOptimizeReport` in `kerf_mold.runner_diameter_optimize`. Dataclasses: `RunnerOptimizeSpec` (part_weight_g, runner_length_mm, polymer_grade, gate_count=1); `RunnerOptimizeReport` (recommended_diameter_mm, beaumont_diameter_mm, cold_runner_waste_g, fill_pressure_estimate_MPa, polymer_specific_adjustment, honest_caveat). Algorithm: D_base=(W_eff^0.25Г—вҲҡL)/3.7 where W_eff=W/gate_count; material-viscosity adjustment: ABS+10%, PC+15% (highly viscous), PP-5% (low viscosity), PA66Вұ0%; D clamped to [1.5, 16.0] mm. Cold-runner waste = ПҖВ·(D/2)ВІВ·L Г— ПҒ_polymer/1000 [g]; polymer densities: ABS 1.05, PC 1.20, PP 0.91, PA66 1.14 g/cmВі (Menges 2001 Table 2.1). Fill-pressure proxy: PвүҲK_matВ·L/D^4 (Hagen-Poiseuille analogy, order-of-magnitude only). `mold_optimize_runner_diameter` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 28 tests green. HONEST: empirical formula only вҖ” NOT a full Hele-Shaw or Cross-WLF rheological simulation; optimises a SINGLE runner segment for one gate вҖ” does NOT optimise filling balance in multi-cavity molds (use mold_check_runner_balance + mold_generate_runner_layout for multi-cavity networks); fill-pressure estimate is order-of-magnitude proxy only; cold-runner waste assumes cylindrical cross-section (trapezoidal/half-round runners have different volumes); confirm with Moldflow/Moldex3D/SigmaSoft fill simulation and mold trial вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/runner_diameter_optimize.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 В§6.5 (Optimal runner diameter); Menges 2001 В§6.5.

**MOLD-WARPAGE-INDEX** вң… вҖ” Heuristic warpage-risk index (0вҖ“100) for injection-moulded parts. `compute_warpage_index(WarpageSpec) -> WarpageIndexReport` in `kerf_mold.warpage_index`. Dataclasses: `WarpageSpec` (wall_thickness_uniformity_pct: 0вҖ“100, gate_location: "centered"|"edge"|"corner"|"unbalanced", polymer_grade, post_eject_cooling_time_s, mold_temp_C); `WarpageIndexReport` (warpage_index: float, risk_level: "low"|"medium"|"high"|"severe", primary_warp_driver, mitigation_suggestions: list[str], honest_caveat, sub_scores: dict). Scoring (Beaumont 2007 В§10 + Menges 2001 В§8): wall-uniformity penalty (0вҖ“30 pts; piecewise linear: 100%вҶ’0 pts, 80%вҶ’6 pts, 0%вҶ’30 pts); gate-location penalty (0вҖ“25 pts: centered=3, edge=14, corner=22, unbalanced=25); polymer grade (0вҖ“20 pts: PC=5 low, ABS=7, PP=14 semi-cryst., POM=15, GF-PA66=20 max вҖ” Menges 2001 Table 8.2 shrinkage anisotropy); post-eject cooling time (0вҖ“15 pts; exponential decay score=15В·exp(вҲ’t/40), characteristic time 40 s per Menges 2001 В§8.5 HDT stabilisation); mold temperature deviation from recommended range (0вҖ“10 pts). Risk thresholds: 0вҖ“24 low, 25вҖ“49 medium, 50вҖ“74 high, 75вҖ“100 severe. Prioritised mitigation suggestions generated per dominant factor. `mold_compute_warpage_index` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 39 tests green. HONEST: heuristic screening tool ONLY (Вұ15 pts uncertainty typical) вҖ” real warpage prediction requires full filling + packing + cooling FEM simulation (Moldflow, Moldex3D, SigmaSoft 3D Warp); orientation-dependent shrinkage tensors, part geometry, packing pressure, injection speed, hold time, runner imbalance, sequential valve gating, and residual-stress relaxation are NOT modelled вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/warpage_index.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 В§10 (Warpage Analysis); Menges 2001 В§8 (Post-mold shrinkage).

**MOLD-COOLING-PRESSURE-DROP** вң… вҖ” Total pressure-drop across multi-segment mold cooling-channel networks (Darcy-Weisbach + minor-loss K-factors) + chiller pump head verification. `compute_cooling_pressure_drop(segments, coolant) -> CoolingPressureDropReport` in `kerf_mold.cooling_pressure_drop`. Dataclasses: `CoolingChannelSegment` (length_mm, diameter_mm, segment_type: "straight"|"elbow_90"|"elbow_45"|"tee_thru"|"tee_branch"); `CoolantSpec` (flow_rate_L_per_min, density_kg_m3=1000, viscosity_cP=1.0); `CoolingPressureDropReport` (total_pressure_drop_bar, reynolds_number, friction_factor, segment_breakdown, chiller_head_required_bar, recommended_pump_head_bar, honest_caveat). Algorithm: Re=ПҒВ·vВ·D/Ој; О”P_major=fВ·(L/D)В·(ПҒvВІ/2); О”P_minor=KВ·(ПҒvВІ/2). Smooth-pipe friction: f=64/Re (laminar Re<2300); Blasius f=0.316/Re^0.25 (turbulent Re>4000); linear blend in transition. K-factors: elbow_90=0.9, elbow_45=0.4, tee_thru=0.6, tee_branch=1.8. Recommended pump head=total_О”PГ—1.25 (25% margin). `mold_compute_cooling_pressure_drop` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: single-phase incompressible fluid only (water/water-glycol) вҖ” no two-phase/boiling flow; no heat-transfer coupling (viscosity spatially uniform); smooth-pipe Blasius only (no Colebrook-White roughness correction); series network assumed (parallel branches need per-branch analysis) вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/cooling_pressure_drop.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 В§11.2 Table 11.1; White "Fluid Mechanics" 8th ed. В§6.7, В§6.9.

**ELEC-EMI-FILTER-CUTOFF** вң… вҖ” Passive LC/RC power-line EMI filter design per Ott "EMC Engineering" В§15.3 + CISPR 22/EN 55022. `design_emi_filter(EmiFilterSpec) -> EmiFilterReport` in `kerf_electronics.emi_filter_design`. Dataclasses: `EmiFilterSpec` (dc_voltage_V, dc_current_A, target_attenuation_dB, target_freq_kHz, filter_topology, load_resistance_ohm=None); `EmiFilterReport` (cutoff_freq_Hz, L_uH, C_uF, R_ohm, attenuation_at_target_dB, recommended_caps_X2_uF, honest_caveat). Three topologies: LC_low_pass (2nd-order вҲ’40 dB/dec: f_c = f_t / 10^(A/40), C = 1/((2ПҖВ·f_c)ВІВ·L) for L=100 ВөH); PI_LC_L (3rd-order ПҖ-section вҲ’60 dB/dec: f_c = f_t / 10^(A/60), each shunt cap = C/2); RC_low_pass (1st-order вҲ’20 dB/dec: f_c = f_t / 10^(A/20), C = 1/(2ПҖВ·f_cВ·R)). **CAM-TURNING-DEPTH** вң… вҖ” Optimal depth-of-cut (DOC) per pass + total roughing passes for a lathe turning operation. `compute_turning_depth(TurningSpec) -> TurningDepthReport` in `kerf_cam.turning_depth_calc`. Dataclasses: `TurningSpec` (stock_diameter_mm, final_diameter_mm, finish_pass_doc_mm=0.5, max_roughing_doc_mm=3.0, material, tool_nose_radius_mm, feed_mm_per_rev, spindle_rpm, workpiece_length_mm=100); `TurningDepthReport` (num_roughing_passes, num_finishing_passes, total_passes, roughing_doc_mm, total_machining_time_s, recommended_doc_for_material, honest_caveat). Material DOC ranges: steel_1018 2вҖ“4 mm (rec 3.0), aluminum_6061 4вҖ“8 mm (rec 6.0), stainless_303 1.5вҖ“2.5 mm (rec 2.0). HONEST: straight (cylindrical) turning only вҖ” no profile turning, no taper, no threading, no facing; Constant Surface Speed (CSS/G96) NOT implemented; time estimate excludes rapids, tool changes, and acceleration ramps; DOC ranges are conservative averages for coated carbide inserts at moderate cutting speed вҖ” verify against CoroPlus ToolGuide for production вҖ” `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/turning_depth_calc.py`. Refs: MH 31e В§1148; Sandvik CoroPlus Turning Catalogue (2024).

**GDT-FEATURE-OF-SIZE-DOF (ASME Y14.5-2018 В§4.7 + В§7.3)** вң… вҖ” `compute_fos_dof(FOSSpec) -> FOSDoFReport` enumerates the Degrees of Freedom constrained vs released by a Feature of Size + geometric tolerance combination вҖ” critical for inspection planning. Dataclasses: `FOSSpec` (feature_type: "cylinder"|"hole"|"slot"|"sphere"|"planar_pair"|"width", tolerance_symbol: "position"|"perpendicularity"|"parallelism"|"angularity"|"runout"|"total_runout"); `FOSDoFReport` (dof_constrained, dof_released, total_constrained, datum_required_count, code_section, honest_caveat). DOF rules per В§4.7 + В§7.3: cylinder/hole + position вҶ’ TX, TY (axis radial location); cylinder/hole + orientation вҶ’ RX, RY (axis tilt); cylinder/hole + runout/total_runout вҶ’ TX, TY, RX, RY (В§7.3.4/В§7.3.5 coupling); slot/width/planar_pair + position вҶ’ TX (centre-plane location); slot + orientation вҶ’ RX, RY; sphere + position вҶ’ TX, TY, TZ (point location); sphere + orientation вҶ’ nothing (rotationally symmetric). `gdt_compute_fos_dof` LLM tool registered via gated import pattern; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 35 tests green. **GDT-RUNOUT-CIRCULAR (ASME Y14.5-2018 В§12.4)** вң… вҖ” `check_circular_runout(CircularRunoutSpec) -> CircularRunoutReport` evaluates single-plane circular runout tolerance compliance per В§12.4. Input is structured as a list of cross-section lists вҖ” each inner list contains radial measurements at a single axial position (mirrors physical inspection: fixture at zвӮҖ, rotate 360В°, record N radial readings). Dataclasses: `RunoutMeasurement` (angular_position_deg, radial_measurement_mm, axial_position_mm=0.0); `CircularRunoutSpec` (measurements_per_cross_section: list[list[RunoutMeasurement]], tolerance_mm, datum_axis_id="A"); `CircularRunoutReport` (fim_per_section_mm, max_fim_mm, governing_axial_position_mm, pass_fail: "PASS"|"FAIL", margin_mm, num_measurements_total, honest_caveat). Algorithm (В§12.4): FIM_s = max(r)вҲ’min(r) for each cross-section s; max_FIM = worst section; pass вҹә max_FIM вүӨ tolerance_mm. margin_mm = tolerance вҲ’ max_FIM (positive = headroom; negative = overrun). Minimum 3 measurements per section enforced. governing_axial_position_mm identifies the worst-case section; tied FIM вҶ’ first section wins. Distinct from runout_check.py (В§13 point-cloud API): section-oriented input; dedicated В§12.4 compliance path; conical surface independence confirmed (per-section FIM=0 when form is perfect even though nominal radius varies axially). Oracle: eccentric cylinder eccentricity=1mm вҶ’ FIM=2mm; tol=1mmвҶ’FAIL margin=вҲ’1mm; tol=2mmвҶ’PASS margin=0. `gdt_check_circular_runout` LLM tool registered via gated import; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 27 tests green. HONEST FLAG: measurements must be pre-computed radial distances from the TRUE datum axis; datum simulator computation (minimum zone cylinder вҖ” ASME B89.3.1 / ISO 12181-1 В§4.3) NOT performed; probe offset/cosine error/thermal corrections must be applied by caller вҖ” `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/runout_circular.py`.

**GDT-RUNOUT-CHECK (ASME Y14.5-2018 В§13 + ISO 1101:2017 В§18)** вң… вҖ” `check_runout(RunoutCheckSpec, list[InspectionPoint]) -> RunoutCheckReport` verifies circular and total runout tolerance compliance for a rotational feature given inspection points measured around a datum axis. Dataclasses: `InspectionPoint` (theta_deg, axial_z_mm, radius_measured_mm); `RunoutCheckSpec` (feature_id, runout_tolerance_mm, runout_type: "circular"|"total", nominal_radius_mm); `RunoutCheckReport` (max_runout_mm, mean_radius_mm, fom, compliant, per_section_runout, honest_caveat). Algorithms per В§13: Circular runout (В§13.2 / ISO В§18.3) вҖ” group points by axial z-section, runout at each section = max(R)вҲ’min(R) = Full Indicator Movement (FIM); max_runout = worst section. Total runout (В§13.3 / ISO В§18.4) вҖ” FIM over ALL points simultaneously (max(R)вҲ’min(R)); captures taper/coaxiality + form combined; total_runout вүҘ circular_runout always. fom = max_runout / tolerance; fom < 1.0 вҶ’ pass. Oracle: eccentric cylinder with 0.05 mm axis offset вҶ’ circular runout = 2Г—0.05 = 0.10 mm (2d formula); tapered cylinder (R=10.00вҶ’10.20 mm across 3 z-sections) вҶ’ circular_runout=0 per section, total_runout=0.20 mm > circular. `gdt_check_runout` LLM tool registered via gated import pattern; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 26 tests green. HONEST FLAG: ideal datum axis assumed вҖ” all radii must be pre-computed from a known datum axis; Chebyshev-optimal (minimum zone) axis fit (ASME B89.3.1 / ISO 12181-1 В§4.3) is not performed. Circular runout grouping uses exact z-value equality вҖ” real CMM data may require z-binning before calling. Total runout is radial-only (max RвҲ’min R); axial deviation for face runout surfaces (ASME В§13.3 full definition) is not checked вҖ” `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/runout_check.py`.

**GDT-DATUM-SHIFT-CHECK (ASME Y14.5-2018 В§4.5 + В§7.3.5)** вң… вҖ” `compute_datum_shift(DatumFeatureSpec, base_position_tolerance_mm) -> DatumShiftReport` computes per-datum bonus tolerance (datum shift) when a datum feature of size is referenced with an MMC or LMC modifier in the feature control frame. Dataclasses: `DatumFeatureSpec` (datum_letter, mmc_size_mm, lmc_size_mm, measured_size_mm, material_condition_modifier); `DatumShiftReport` (datum_letter, base_tolerance_zone_mm, bonus_shift_mm, total_available_tolerance_mm, shift_allowed, code_section, honest_caveat). Computation per В§4.5 + В§7.3.5: MMC modifier вҶ’ shift = |measured вҲ’ MMC|; LMC modifier вҶ’ shift = |measured вҲ’ LMC|; RFS вҶ’ shift = 0. **GDT-COMPOSITE-TOLERANCE (ASME Y14.5-2018 В§10.5.2 + В§11.6)** вң… вҖ” `validate_composite_frame(CompositeFrameSpec) -> CompositeFrameValidationReport` validates stacked PLTZF/FRTZF composite feature control frames in `kerf_cad_core.gdt.composite_tolerance_check`. Three rules enforced: R1 вҖ” all segments share the same geometric symbol (В§10.5.2(a)); R2 вҖ” each lower segment tolerance вүӨ segment above it (FRTZF tol вүӨ PLTZF tol, В§10.5.1 Note 2); R3 вҖ” lower segment datum_refs must be a subset of the segment above (В§10.5.1(b)) вҖ” new datums below the PLTZF would imply location constraint, reserved for the PLTZF; FRTZF may only refine orientation. **GDT-COMPOSITE-POSITION (ASME Y14.5-2018 В§10.5)** вң… вҖ” `check_composite_position(CompositePositionSpec) -> CompositePositionReport` evaluates composite positional tolerance compliance for a feature pattern against measured 3-D points. **GDT-DIMENSION-CHAIN (ASME Y14.5-2018 В§5.3 + Bralla В§1)** вң… вҖ” `compute_dimension_chain(chain: list[DimensionLink], target_gap_min_mm, target_gap_max_mm) -> DimensionChainReport` computes worst-case (WC) and statistical RSS tolerance stack-up for a linear dimension chain. Dataclasses: `DimensionLink` (link_id, nominal_mm, tol_plus_mm, tol_minus_mm, direction: "positive"|"negative"); `DimensionChainReport` (nominal_gap_mm, worst_case_min_mm, worst_case_max_mm, rss_min_mm, rss_max_mm, links_count, dominant_link, honest_caveat). Algorithm: nominal_gap = ОЈ s_iВ·d_i; WC accumulation T_WC = ОЈ max(tвҒә_i, tвҒ»_i); G_wc_min/max = nominal вҲ“ T_WC; RSS accumulation T_RSS = вҲҡ(ОЈ max(tвҒә_i, tвҒ»_i)ВІ); G_rss_min/max = nominal вҲ“ T_RSS (3Пғ bilateral, 99.73% assemblability). dominant_link = link with largest half-tolerance. Oracle: +100Вұ0.5 / вҲ’30Вұ0.2 / вҲ’20Вұ0.1 вҶ’ nominal=50 mm; WC=[49.2, 50.8]; RSS=вҲҡ0.30=0.5477вҶ’[49.452, 50.548]. `gdt_compute_dimension_chain` LLM tool registered via gated import pattern; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 24 tests green. HONEST FLAG: RSS assumes independent, normally distributed component dimensions centred on nominal (Cpk=1.0 for all links); correlation between links (e.g. same fixture datum) and non-normal distributions are not modelled вҖ” RSS is unconservative in those cases; Monte Carlo with measured process distributions is more accurate per Bralla В§1 вҖ” `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/dimension_chain.py`. Refs: ASME Y14.5-2018 В§5.3; Bralla "Design for Manufacturability Handbook" В§1.

**GK-P13 SUBD-G1-EXTRAORDINARY-PATCHES** вң… вҖ” G1 continuity at extraordinary-vertex SubDвҶ’NURBS patch conversion. `convert_subd_to_g1_patches(spec: ExtraordinaryPatchSpec) -> G1PatchResult` builds n bicubic BГ©zier patches around a Catmull-Clark extraordinary vertex (valence n вү  4) with Loop (1987) В§4 tangent-plane continuity enforcement: (1) apply `num_iterations` CC subdivisions to isolate the EV; (2) compute EV limit position V_inf via Stam (1998) В§3.1; (3) build n 4Г—4 BГ©zier CP grids in the Stam limit-tangent plane, one per face sector; (4) project second-row CPs of adjacent patches into the Stam tangent plane at V_inf to enforce G1 across all n shared boundary edges. Dataclasses: `ExtraordinaryPatchSpec` (cage_mesh: SubdCage, extraordinary_vertex_idx: int, num_iterations: int=2); `G1PatchResult` (n_patches int = valence, patch_control_points_per_patch: list[list[list[tuple]]] 4Г—4 CP grid per patch, max_g1_residual_deg: float, mean_g1_residual_deg: float, valence: int, honest_caveat: str). G1 residual measured as inter-patch normal angle (degrees, sampled at 5 points per shared edge). LLM tool `subd_convert_to_g1_patches` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 32 oracle-asserted tests green (valence-3 cube corner 3 patches + G1 residual < 1В°, valence-5 dome EV 5 patches + G1 < 1В°, valence-4 regular warns + 4 patches, valence-6 hex EV 6 patches, out-of-range idx returns empty, zero iterations runs, re-export from subd package, honest_caveat mentions Loop/G1/Peters-Reif, multiple subdivision levels 1-3 finite residuals, n_patches==valence invariant). HONEST: Loop (1987) G1 construction only вҖ” Peters-Reif G2 (curvature continuity) NOT implemented (requires degree вүҘ 5 patches, Peters-Reif 2008 В§7.4); high-valence EVs (n вүҘ 8) may show curvature inflation due to convex-hull property of bicubic BГ©zier patches; G1 residual < 1В° achieved for n=3,5 test cases. Refs: Loop (1987) MS Thesis В§4 Utah; Stam (1998) В§3.1вҖ“3.3 SIGGRAPH; Peters-Reif (2008) Subdivision Surfaces В§7.4; Reif (1995) CAGD 12(2) вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/g1_extraordinary_patches.py`.

**GK-P12 SUBD-STAM-LIMIT-TANGENTS** вң… вҖ” exact limit tangent vectors at extraordinary Catmull-Clark SubD vertices (valence n вү  4) using the eigenstructure decomposition from Stam (1998) В§3.2вҖ“3.3. `compute_stam_limit_tangents(ev: ExtraordinaryVertex, ring_positions=None) -> LimitTangentReport` computes: V_inf = w_VВ·V + w_eВ·ОЈP_i + w_fВ·ОЈQ_i (limit position, Stam В§3.2 eq. 3.1); T_u = ОЈ cos(2ПҖi/n)В·(P_i вҲ’ V_inf); T_v = ОЈ sin(2ПҖi/n)В·(P_i вҲ’ V_inf) (limit tangents, Stam В§3.3); N = T_u Г— T_v (unit normal, CВ№-continuous at EV per Reif 1995); subdominant eigenvalue О»_n = (1/4)(1 + cos(2ПҖ/n)); approximate Gaussian curvature K (angle-deficit / Gauss-Bonnet, Meyer et al. 2003 В§4) and mean curvature H (cotangent-weight Laplace-Beltrami, Meyer et al. 2003 В§3.3). Dataclasses: `ExtraordinaryVertex` (vertex_index, valence, position_xyz_mm, one_ring_vertices, one_ring_faces); `LimitTangentReport` (tangent_u, tangent_v, normal_xyz, gaussian_curvature_estimate, mean_curvature_estimate, valence, eigenvalue_subdominant, honest_caveat). LLM tool `subd_compute_stam_limit_tangents` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 30 oracle-asserted tests green (regular v4 flat normal Z, flat T_u/T_v in XY, flat KвүҲ0, flat HвүҲ0, unit normal all valences, nonzero tangent magnitudes, dome v3/5/6 K>0, dome normal outward, hex v6 symmetric tangent magnitudes, eigenvalue formula for v3/4/6/5/7, limit weights partition-of-unity all n, reexport from subd package, tangents span plane, synthetic fallback no crash, honest caveat non-empty + "Stam"). DISTINCT from `limit_normal_fit.py` (which samples face grids) вҖ” this is the closed-form Stam formula AT the extraordinary vertex point itself. HONEST: tangent vectors EXACT per Stam В§3.3; curvature estimates APPROXIMATE (discrete polyhedral estimators, CC surface is only CВ№ at EV so CВІ-based curvature has limited meaning); distinct from the face-sampling `limit_normal_fit.py` вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/stam_limit_tangents.py`. Refs: Stam (1998) В§3.2вҖ“3.3 SIGGRAPH; Reif (1995) CAGD 12(2); Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD В§10(6); Meyer et al. (2003) "Discrete Differential-Geometry Operators for Triangulated 2-Manifolds" В§3вҖ“4.

**GK-P19 SUBD-FEATURE-CURVES** вң… вҖ” extract characteristic "ridge" and "valley" polylines from a Catmull-Clark SubD limit surface (or refined cage) using discrete principal-curvature analysis. `extract_feature_curves(spec: FeatureCurveSpec) -> FeatureCurveResult` subdivides the cage `subdivision_level` times (Catmull-Clark 1978), estimates per-vertex normals (area-weighted face normals), computes Taubin (1995) curvature tensor at each vertex (edge normal-curvature accumulation вҶ’ 3Г—3 tensor projected to tangent plane вҶ’ eigenvalues ОәвӮҒ вүҘ ОәвӮӮ), then classifies vertices as ridge (ОәвӮҒ > ridge_threshold_per_mm) or valley (ОәвӮӮ < вҲ’valley_threshold_per_mm) and chains them into polylines via BFS edge-following. Dataclasses: `FeatureCurveSpec` (cage: SubdCage, subdivision_level: int=2, ridge_threshold_per_mm: float=0.1, valley_threshold_per_mm: float=0.1); `FeatureCurve` (kind: str "ridge"|"valley", polyline_xyz_mm: list[tuple], length_mm: float, mean_principal_curvature: float); `FeatureCurveResult` (curves, num_ridges, num_valleys, total_ridge_length_mm, total_valley_length_mm, max_principal_curvature, honest_caveat). LLM tool `subd_extract_feature_curves` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 26 oracle-asserted tests green (flat plane 0 ridges + 0 valleys, flat plane max ОәвӮҒ near zero, cube cage ridges detected + positive curvature + finite coords, saddle cage features detected, sphere high threshold = 0 ridges, API contracts вҖ” empty cage, spec/dataclass defaults, kindвҲҲ{ridge,valley}, threshold monotonicity, re-export). Use cases: ZBrush-style topology hints; automatic UV-seam generation along high-curvature lines; feature detection for re-meshing or CAM path planning. HONEST CAVEATS: DISCRETE CURVATURE APPROXIMATION вҖ” principal curvatures via discrete cotangent Laplacian (Meyer et al. 2003), NOT exact CC limit-surface evaluation; errors O(hВІ) in edge length; sufficient for UV-seam/topology hints but NOT precision curvature analysis. THRESHOLD TUNING вҖ” ridge/valley thresholds are scale-dependent (mmвҒ»В№); defaults (0.1 mmвҒ»В№) are a starting point, retune for your object scale. PERFORMANCE вҖ” vertex count scales O(4^L) with subdivision_level L. Refs: Ohtake, Belyaev & Seidel (2004) "Ridge-Valley Lines on Meshes via Implicit Surface Fitting" SIGGRAPH; Meyer et al. (2003) "Discrete Differential-Geometry Operators for Triangulated 2-Manifolds" VisMath; Taubin (1995) "Estimating the Tensor of Curvature of a Surface" ICCV; Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD 10(6); Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH; OpenSubdiv docs вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/feature_curves.py`.

**GK-P14 SUBD-CREASE-FRACTIONAL-DECAY** вң… вҖ” semi-sharp fractional crease multi-level decay for Catmull-Clark SubD. `apply_fractional_crease_decay(spec: FractionalCreaseSpec) -> CreaseDecayResult` applies the DeRose-Kass-Truong (1998) В§4 rule: s_new = max(0, s_old вҲ’ 1) per subdivision level. After L levels: s_L = max(0, sвӮҖ вҲ’ L). Dataclasses: `CreasedEdge` (v0_idx, v1_idx, sharpness вҲҲ [0,вҲһ)); `FractionalCreaseSpec` (cage: SubdCage, edges: list[CreasedEdge], subdivision_level: int); `CreaseDecayResult` (decayed_edges: list[CreasedEdge], effective_dihedral_smoothing_per_edge: list[float] 0=fully sharp/1=fully smooth, max_sharpness_remaining: float, num_fully_decayed: int, honest_caveat: str). Smooth-weight formula: smooth_weight = 1 вҲ’ clamp(s_L, 0, 1) вҖ” matches OpenSubdiv fractional crease blend definition. Convention: s вүҘ 10 вүҲ permanently sharp (OpenSubdiv). LLM tool `subd_apply_crease_decay` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 42 oracle-asserted tests green (infinite s=100 sharp at all levels, s=2 at L=0/1/2/3, s=0.5 half-sharp then smooth, mixed crease set 4 edges, monotonic increasing smooth_weight, empty edge list, level-0 identity, re-export from subd init, honest caveat non-empty + mentions schedule-only + DeRose, OpenSubdiv s=10 convention at L=9/L=10, negative sharpness clamped, large level clamps to zero, never negative). HONEST: SHARPNESS SCHEDULE ONLY вҖ” applies the s-1 rule per level and returns decayed s-values + blend weights; does NOT simulate the resulting subdivided cage geometry, does NOT apply CC face/edge/vertex splitting operators; cage vertices/faces passed through unchanged; blended mesh evaluation (interpolating between smooth and sharp CC rules for sвҲҲ(0,1)) is out of scope вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/crease_fractional_decay.py`. Refs: DeRose-Kass-Truong (1998) В§4 SIGGRAPH; OpenSubdiv Subdivision Surfaces docs; Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD 10(6).

**SUBD-LIMIT-NORMAL-FIT** вң… вҖ” sample the Catmull-Clark limit-surface normal nМӮ(u,v) at a uniform (u,v) grid across all cage faces using Stam (1998) exact eigenstructure tangent vectors; `sample_subd_limit_normals(cage_mesh, samples_per_face=9, normalize=True)` returns `LimitNormalFitResult(sampled_normals, max_normal_residual_deg, mean_normal_residual_deg, num_irregular_samples, honest_caveat)`; per-face nГ—n grid (n = round(sqrt(samples_per_face))); normal via N = вҲӮS/вҲӮu Г— вҲӮS/вҲӮv from Stam tangents (CВ№-continuous at extraordinary vertices, exact bi-cubic B-spline for valence-4 regular faces); residuals computed against bilinear interpolation of four face-corner Stam normals вҖ” quantifies accuracy gain of a proper normal field vs the simple shader approximation; irregular-vertex flag per sample (valence вү  4 faces); LLM tool `subd_sample_limit_normals` registered in plugin via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 17 oracle-asserted tests (flat plane nz > 0.9999, unit-length all faces, nx/ny вүҲ 0, dot > 0.9999, normalize=True/False, result structure, total sample count, honest_caveat non-empty, irregular cube valence-3 > 0, flat plane residual < 0.5В°, max residual вүӨ 90В°, cylinder normals perpendicular to Y, cube 24-sample count + unit-length, empty cage no exception). HONEST: "fit" = residual analysis vs bilinear, NOT a closed-form NURBS surface (would require overdetermined least-squares + knot/CP storage) вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/limit_normal_fit.py`. Refs: Stam (1998) В§3.2; Halstead-Kass-DeRose (1993); Piegl-Tiller В§9.

**ARCH-BASE-PLATE-AISC (AISC DG-1 В§3.1 + AISC 360-22 В§J8)** вң… вҖ” `design_base_plate(ColumnSpec, ConcreteSpec, Fy=345.0) -> BasePlateReport` implements steel column base plate design for concentric axial compressive loads. Concrete bearing strength: Pp = 0.85В·f'cВ·A1В·вҲҡ(A2/A1) with A2/A1 вүӨ 4 (AISC 360-22 В§J8 Eq J8-2); ПҶ_c = 0.65; required A1 = P_u/(ПҶ_cВ·0.85В·f'cВ·вҲҡ(A2/A1)). Plate dimensions rounded up to nearest 5 mm; must cover column footprint (0.95В·d Г— 0.80В·bf per DG-1 В§3.1.1). Cantilever arms: m=(NвҲ’0.95В·d)/2 (Eq 3.1-1); n=(BвҲ’0.80В·bf)/2 (Eq 3.1-2); n'=вҲҡ(dВ·bf)/4; X=[4В·dВ·bf/(d+bf)ВІ]В·[P_u/(ПҶ_cВ·Pp)] (Eq 3.1-8); О»=min(1, 2В·вҲҡX/(1+вҲҡ(1вҲ’X))); l=max(m,n,О»В·n'). Plate thickness via Murray-Stockwell (DG-1 Eq 3.1-5): t=lВ·вҲҡ(2В·P_u/(0.9В·FyВ·BВ·N)), rounded up to 1 mm. Oracle: W14x90, P=1000 kN, f'c=30 MPa, ped 600Г—600 mm вҶ’ A1_reqвүҲ30166 mmВІ; plate 295Г—340 mm (column footprint governs, N_min=338 mm, B_min=295 mm); t=15 mm; DCR=0.318 (adequate). `arch_design_base_plate` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import). Re-exported from arch/__init__.py. 24 hermetic oracle tests pass вҖ” `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/base_plate_aisc.py`. *SCOPE: concentric axial compressive load ONLY (DG-1 В§3.1). NOT covered: moment transfer (DG-1 В§3.2), anchor rod design (DG-1 В§3.3вҖ“3.4), shear lug (DG-1 В§3.5), biaxial bending, tensile uplift. A2 taken as pedestal plan area; irregular pedestals must supply equivalent rectangular A2. Grout strength вүҘ f'c assumed.*

**ARCH-BEAM-DEFLECTION (Roark 9e В§8 + AISC Manual Table 3-23)** вң… вҖ” `compute_beam_deflection(BeamSpec) -> BeamDeflectionReport` implements five closed-form Euler-Bernoulli beam cases: (1) simply_supported + point_center: Оҙ=PLВі/(48EI), M=PL/4 [Roark Table 8.1 case 7; AISC 3-23 diag 1]; (2) simply_supported + udl: Оҙ=5wLвҒҙ/(384EI), M=wLВІ/8 [case 2; diag 2]; (3) cantilever + point_center (tip load): Оҙ=PLВі/(3EI), M=PL [case 1; diag 6]; (4) cantilever + udl: Оҙ=wLвҒҙ/(8EI), M=wLВІ/2 [case 3; diag 7]; (5) fixed_fixed + udl: Оҙ=wLвҒҙ/(384EI), M=wLВІ/12 [case 15; diag 9]. `BeamDeflectionReport` returns Оҙ_max_mm, M_max_Nmm, V_max_N, deflection_location_mm, honest_caveat. `arch_compute_beam_deflection` LLM tool registered in plugin; gated import (registry unavailable вҶ’ module still importable). 39 hermetic oracle tests pass (formula verification вүӨ0.1%; W14x90 L=6 m P=100 kN ОҙвүҲ5.41 mm hand-verified; zero-loadвҶ’zero; fixed_fixed+point_center вҶ’ ValueError; invalid inputs вҶ’ ValueError; re-export from arch/__init__.py) вҖ” `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/beam_deflection.py`. *Scope: linear-elastic, small-deflection Euler-Bernoulli only. No shear deformation (Timoshenko), no lateral-torsional buckling, no yield check, no partial-span loads.*

**ARCH-COLUMN-LOAD-CHECK (AISC 360-22 В§E3 + ACI 318-19 В§22.4)** вң… вҖ” `check_steel_column(SteelColumnSpec, P_kN) -> ColumnLoadReport` implements AISC 360-22 В§E3 LRFD: Fe = ПҖВІE/(KL/r)ВІ, inelastic Fcr = 0.658^(Fy/Fe)В·Fy (E3-2) for KL/r вүӨ 4.71вҲҡ(E/Fy), elastic Fcr = 0.877В·Fe (E3-3) otherwise, ПҶ_c = 0.90, slender-column flag at KL/r > 200. `check_concrete_column(ConcreteColumnSpec, P_kN) -> ColumnLoadReport` implements ACI 318-19 В§22.4.2.2: ПҶВ·Pn = ПҶВ·0.80В·[0.85В·f'cВ·(AgвҲ’Ast) + fyВ·Ast], ПҶ = 0.65 tied (0.75 spiral), ПҒg bounds check per В§10.6.1.1. Both return `ColumnLoadReport` with ПҶPn, DCR, governing mode, PASS/FAIL, and honest caveat. `arch_check_column_load` LLM tool registered in plugin. 27 hermetic oracle tests pass (W14x90 at KL=4 000 mm formula-verified; ACI concrete 400Г—400 formula-verified; DCR > 1.0 FAIL; KL/r > 200 warning; ValueError on bad inputs; tool ok/err payloads) вҖ” `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/column_load_check.py`. *Disclaimer: local buckling, torsional buckling, combined loading, and slenderness amplification (ACI В§6.6.4) not included.*

**ARCH-FOOTING-BEARING-CAPACITY (Meyerhof 1963 / Bowles 5e В§4 / Das 8e В§3)** вң… вҖ” `compute_bearing_capacity(FootingSpec, SoilProperties, FS=3.0) -> BearingCapacityReport` implements the Meyerhof (1963) general bearing capacity equation q_ult = cВ·N_cВ·s_cВ·d_c + ОіВ·DfВ·N_qВ·s_qВ·d_q + 0.5В·ОіВ·BВ·N_ОіВ·s_ОіВ·d_Оі for shallow footings on cohesive/cohesionless soil. N-factors: N_q = e^(ПҖВ·tanПҶ)В·tanВІ(45+ПҶ/2); N_c = (N_qвҲ’1)В·cotПҶ (ПҶ=0: N_c=5.14 Prandtl limit); N_Оі = (N_qвҲ’1)В·tan(1.4ПҶ). Shape factors s_c, s_q, s_Оі per Bowles Table 4-4 for strip/square/circular/rectangular. **ARCH-RETAINING-WALL-STABILITY (Bowles 5e В§12.3 + Das В§13 вҖ” Rankine active)** вң… вҖ” `check_retaining_wall(RetainingWallSpec, SoilSpec) -> RetainingWallReport` implements overturning, sliding, and bearing stability checks for cantilevered concrete retaining walls under Rankine active earth pressure. Ka = tanВІ(45вҲ’ПҶ/2); Pa = 0.5В·Оі_sВ·HВІВ·Ka (horizontal resultant, at H/3). Weight components per metre: W_stem = Оі_cВ·tВ·(HвҲ’h); W_base = Оі_cВ·BВ·h; W_soil = Оі_sВ·l_heelВ·(HвҲ’h). Moments about toe: M_resist = W_stemВ·(l_toe+t/2) + W_baseВ·(B/2) + W_soilВ·(BвҲ’l_heel/2); M_overt = PaВ·(H/3). FoS_overturning = M_resist/M_overt (min 2.0). FoS_sliding = ОЈWВ·tan(Оҙ)/Pa (min 1.5). Bearing: e = B/2 вҲ’ (M_resistвҲ’M_overt)/ОЈW; q_max = (ОЈW/B)В·(1+6e/B) (trapezoidal; triangular when e>B/6); FoS_bearing = q_a/q_max (min 3.0). `RetainingWallReport` returns Ka, Pa_kN_per_m, FoS_overturning, FoS_sliding, q_max_kPa, FoS_bearing, all_adequate, governing_failure_mode, honest_caveat. Oracle (H=3m, B=2m, t=0.3m, h=0.3m, l_heel=1.5m, l_toe=0.2m, Оі_c=24, Оі_s=18, ПҶ=30В°): Ka=1/3, Pa=27.0 kN/m, FoS_overt=4.16 (adequate), FoS_sliding=1.44 (inadequate at Оҙ=20В°; adequate at Оҙ=25В°). `arch_check_retaining_wall_stability` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import); re-exported from arch/__init__.py. 27 hermetic oracle tests pass вҖ” `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/retaining_wall_stability.py`. *SCOPE: Rankine ACTIVE pressure only вҖ” level backfill, cohesionless (c=0). **ARCH-SHEAR-WALL-OOP (ACI 318-19 В§11.7 + В§22.3 + Wight В§13.13)** вң… вҖ” `check_shear_wall_oop(ShearWallSpec, phi=0.65) -> ShearWallOOPReport` implements out-of-plane (OOP) flexural capacity check for RC shear walls under combined axial + lateral (wind/seismic) loads. **ARCH-LATERAL-BRACING (AISC 360-22 В§F2 + AISC Manual Table 3-2)** вң… вҖ” `check_lateral_bracing(WSectionSpec, L_b_mm, Cb=1.0) -> LateralBracingReport` implements AISC 360-22 В§F2 LRFD for compact doubly symmetric I-shaped members bent about the major axis. ПҶ_b = 0.90; c=1.0 (F2-8a). `LateralBracingReport` returns Lp, Lr, Mp, Mr, Mn, phi_Mn, governing_mode ("yielding"|"inelastic_LTB"|"elastic_LTB"), Lb_to_Lp_ratio, honest_caveat. **BREP-SOLID-CONTAINS-POINT** вң… вҖ” Ray-casting Jordan-curve inside/outside test for B-rep solids: `solid_contains_point(body, point, tolerance=1e-6) -> ContainmentResult` casts a generic-direction ray (1, 0.013, 0.029) from the query point and counts boundary crossings; odd = inside, even = outside. `ContainmentResult` dataclass: `inside` (bool|None), `on_boundary`, `ray_hits`, `degenerate_ray`. ### Latest delta вҖ” 2026-05-31

**NURBS-CURVE-FRESNEL-PARAMETERIZE** вң… вҖ” `fresnel_parameterize_curve(curve, num_samples=200, target_kappa_rate=1.0)` returns `FresnelParameterizationResult(curve_out, max_curvature_residual, fresnel_S, fresnel_C, honest_caveat)`; re-parameterizes a NurbsCurve so that curvature grows linearly with arc-length (Оә(s) вүҲ ОұВ·s вҖ” Euler spiral / clothoid / Cornu spiral law). Algorithm: (1) arc-lengthвҖ“uniform sampling via adaptive 5-pt Gauss-Legendre; (2) Fresnel integral evaluation C(Пғ), S(Пғ) with Пғ=sВ·вҲҡ(Оұ/ПҖ) (Abramowitz-Stegun В§7.3); (3) monotone Fresnel-C parameter sequence drives NURBS re-interpolation (Piegl-Tiller В§9.2); (4) monotone-blend fallback when spiral winds past first inflection. Degree-1 polyline caveat; zero-length degenerate guard; negative-alpha treated as positive. LLM tool `nurbs_fresnel_parameterize_curve` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 25 hermetic tests. HONEST: sampling-based, not closed-form; Fresnel monotone blend active for long curves; curvature residual is approximate. Refs: Walton & Meek (2009) В§В§2вҖ“3; Bertolazzi & Frego (2015) В§3 вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/fresnel_parameterize.py`.

**NURBS-CURVE-INFLECTION** вң… вҖ” v2 API: `find_curve_inflections(curve, num_samples=200, tol=1e-6)` returns `CurveInflectionReport(inflection_points, num_inflections, max_curvature, min_curvature, is_fair_class_a, warnings, honest_caveat)`; each inflection is an `InflectionPoint(parameter_u, xy_mm, curvature_left, curvature_right, sign_change)`. Signed curvature Оә(u) = (x'В·y'' вҲ’ y'В·x'') / (x'ВІ + y'ВІ)^1.5 (Piegl-Tiller В§5.3; Farin В§10.6). Algorithm: sample Оә(u) at `num_samples` uniform u-values via NURBS 1st/2nd derivatives вҶ’ adjacent sign-change detection (|Оә| < tol treated as zero) вҶ’ 5-iteration bisection per bracket вҶ’ `is_fair_class_a = True` iff вүӨ 1 inflection AND no abrupt Оә-jump (>5Г— mean, Farin В§10.6; Sapidis В§3). Legacy v1 API (`find_curve_inflections_v1` вҶ’ `InflectionResult`) retained for backward compat. LLM tool `nurbs_find_curve_inflections` updated to return v2 payload. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 38 hermetic tests (20 legacy + 18 new; oracles: S-curve вҶ’ 1 inflection + fair, double-S sine вҶ’ вүҘ2 + not fair, circle вҶ’ 0 + fair + ОәвүҲ1/R, straight line вҶ’ 0 + fair + warns). HONEST: **2D only** вҖ” 3D space-curve inflections (requiring torsion) not supported; sampling-based, does NOT solve Оә=0 analytically; near-zero-curvature regions may produce false positives or miss gentle crossings. Refs: Piegl-Tiller В§5.3/В§9.2; Farin В§10.6; do Carmo В§1.5; Sapidis В§3 вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_inflection.py`. **NURBS-CURVE-INFLECTION-STURM** вң… (analytic Sturm inflection now implemented) вҖ” v3 API: `find_curve_inflections_sturm(curve, tol=1e-9)` adds a true analytic root finder via Sturm sequences (Marden В§1.4; Uspensky В§5) on the polynomial numerator p(t) = x'(t)В·y''(t) вҲ’ y'(t)В·x''(t). Algorithm: (1) decompose non-rational B-spline into Bezier segments; (2) convert Bernstein CPs to monomial basis (Farin В§5.1; Farouki-Rajan 1987); (3) form p(s) of degree 2dвҲ’3 per span; (4) build Sturm chain {p_0=p, p_1=p', p_{k+1}=вҲ’rem(p_{k-1},p_k)}; (5) count roots via V(0)вҲ’V(1); (6) isolate each root by recursive Sturm-bisection to tol. Returns same `CurveInflectionReport` with `honest_caveat` noting `method='sturm-analytic'`. Rational NURBS fall back with warning (numerator is rational, not polynomial). 7 hermetic Sturm tests green (S-curve вҶ’ 1 root near midpoint, double-S вҶ’ вүҘ2, Sturm vs v2 agreement, straight line вҶ’ 0, circle rational вҶ’ 0, honest_caveat content, asymmetric cubic accuracy). Refs: Marden (1966) В§1.4; Uspensky (1948) В§5; Farin (2002) В§5.1; Farouki-Rajan (1987) CAGD 4(4).

**NURBS-CURVE-EVOLUTE** вң… вҖ” `compute_curve_evolute(curve, num_samples=200, min_curvature=1e-6)` returns `EvoluteResult(evolute_points, t_params, num_samples, num_cusps_detected, cusp_t_params, honest_caveat)`; computes the locus of centres of osculating circles E(t) = C(t) + nМӮ(t)/Оә(t) where nМӮ is the left-hand unit normal and Оә is the signed curvature. Algorithm: sample t вҲҲ [t_min, t_max] at `num_samples` uniform points; evaluate Оә(t) via standard plane-curve formula Оә = (x'y'' вҲ’ y'x'')/(x'ВІ+y'ВІ)^(3/2) using NURBS analytical derivatives; skip samples where |Оә| < min_curvature (evolute diverges); detect cusps (vertices of C) as local extrema of |Оә| via windowed comparison with amplitude guard (suppresses floating-point chatter on constant-Оә curves). Circle oracle: all evolute points within 1.6e-15 of center. Parabola y=xВІ/2: apex evolute = (0,1) exactly. Ellipse a=2,b=1: 4 cusps (stretched-astroid evolute). Straight line: evolute empty. LLM tool `nurbs_compute_curve_evolute` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 20 hermetic tests. HONEST: **2D curves only** вҖ” 3D Frenet-Serret evolutes (requiring torsion) are not yet supported; cusp detection is windowed/amplitude-gated and depends on sample density; may miss cusps for highly undersampled curves. Applications: cycloidal-gear design, cam-profile cusp analysis, CNC offset self-intersection prediction. Refs: do Carmo В§1.6; Mortenson В§4.2 вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_evolute.py`.

**NURBS-SURFACE-CROSS-SECTION** вң… вҖ” `compute_surface_cross_section(surface, plane_point, plane_normal, nu=50, nv=50)` returns `SurfaceCrossSectionResult(intersection_points_3d, num_intersections, num_components, is_closed_loop, honest_caveat)`; computes the planar cross-section curve C(t) of a NurbsSurface S(u,v) intersected with a plane P (point + normal). Algorithm (Sederberg CAGD В§7.3; Patrikalakis-Maekawa В§5): (1) sample S(u,v) on a (nu Г— nv) uniform grid over the knot domain; (2) compute signed distance d(u,v) = (S вҲ’ P) В· nМӮ for each sample; (3) walk all u-direction and v-direction grid edges, detect sign changes (d_A * d_B < 0); (4) refine each crossing via 5 bisection iterations in (u,v) parameter space (positional error вүҲ cell_size/32); (5) chain intersection points into polyline components via greedy nearest-neighbour walk; (6) detect closed loops (first вүҲ last point within 3Г— mean spacing). Oracles: sphere R=2 вҲ© XY plane (mean radius within 20%), cylinder вҲ© XZ plane (2 components, yвүҲ0), flat patch вҲ© parallel plane (empty), torus вҲ© z=0 (inner/outer rings), non-unit normal idempotent, zero normal safe. LLM tool `nurbs_compute_surface_cross_section` registered via gated import. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 22 hermetic tests green. HONEST: **sample-based** вҖ” sub-cell features (thin necks, tangential near-grazing crossings) may be missed at low nu/nv; 5-iteration bisection (not sub-pixel for coarse grids); component ordering greedy nearest-neighbour (may mis-order interleaved loops); closed-loop detection threshold-based. Refs: Sederberg CAGD В§7.3; Patrikalakis-Maekawa В§5 вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/surface_cross_section.py`.

**NURBS uniform arc-length resample** вң… вҖ” `resample_uniform_arc_length(curve, samples=100)` returns `ResampleResult(points, parameters, arc_lengths, total_length, fitted_curve, degenerate)`; arc-length inversion via bisection on adaptive 5-pt Gauss-Legendre integral (Piegl-Tiller В§9.4 + Patrikalakis-Maekawa В§3.5); `fit=True` returns interpolated NurbsCurve; degenerate flag for zero-length curves; LLM tool `nurbs_curve_resample_uniform`; 12 analytic-oracle tests (circle 2ПҖ/100 Вұ 0.001, parabola arc-uniform < param-uniform variance, line sqrt(2)/10 Вұ 1e-6, degenerate flag). Honest: GL quadrature ~1e-9 accurate; highly-oscillatory curves may need larger `max_depth`.
**Mold MFR injection-speed check** вң… вҖ” `mold_check_melt_flow_ratio` LLM tool: given a polymer's Melt Flow Rate (ASTM D1238 g/10 min), wall thickness, and gate type, returns the recommended injection-speed envelope to avoid jetting, sink marks, and gate freeze-off. Four MFR bands (low < 5, medium 5вҖ“25, high 25вҖ“100, super-high > 100 g/10 min); wall-thickness and gate-type correction factors applied; qualitative risk flags for gate freeze, jetting, and sink marks. References: Beaumont 2007 В§4 + Menges 2001 В§6.2 + ASTM D1238. **Honest caveat**: heuristic only вҖ” MFR is a single-point viscosity proxy; real injection-speed tuning requires full shear-thinning viscosity curve and on-tool DOE with cavity-pressure measurement вҖ” `kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/melt_flow_ratio_check.py`.

**MOLD-SPRUE-BUSHING-MATCH** вң… вҖ” `check_sprue_bushing_match(SprueBushingSpec, MachineNozzleSpec) -> SprueMatchReport` in `kerf_mold.sprue_bushing_match`. Verifies that the cold-runner sprue bushing nozzle-seat radius (R) and orifice diameter (O) match the injection-moulding machine nozzle tip geometry per Beaumont 2007 В§6.4 + DME standard sprue bushing catalogue В§3.2. Compliance rules: sprue_R = nozzle_r + 0.5вҖ“1.0 mm; sprue_O = nozzle_O + 0.5вҖ“1.0 mm; taper 1.5вҖ“3.0В°/side. Dataclasses: `SprueBushingSpec` (nozzle_radius_R_mm, sprue_orifice_diameter_O_mm, total_length_mm, taper_per_side_deg); `MachineNozzleSpec` (nozzle_tip_radius_mm, nozzle_tip_orifice_diameter_mm); `SprueMatchReport` (R_mismatch_mm, R_compliant, O_mismatch_mm, O_compliant, taper_compliant, recommendation, honest_caveat). LLM tool `mold_check_sprue_bushing_match` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 35 oracle tests green. **HONEST SCOPE: standard cold-runner sprue bushings only** вҖ” hot-runner nozzle seats (DME hot-tip, valve-gate, edge-gate) follow different design rules (thermal expansion allowance, heater mass, gate-tip diameter) and are NOT covered; taper beyond 3В°/side used in specialty foamed-material bushings; orifice sizing also depends on shot weight (Beaumont 2007 Table 6.2); measure nozzle radius with a radius gauge, worn nozzles deviate from nominal вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/sprue_bushing_match.py`.

**MOLD-COOLING-TURBULENT-RE-CHECK** вң… вҖ” `check_turbulent_re(CoolingFlowSpec) -> TurbulentReCheckReport` in `kerf_mold.cooling_turbulent_re_check`. Verifies cooling-channel Reynolds number Re = ПҒВ·vВ·D/Ој against the fully-turbulent threshold (Re вүҘ 10 000) required for Dittus-Boelter correlation validity (Incropera & DeWitt eq. 8.60: Nu=0.023В·Re^0.8В·Pr^n). Flow-regime classification (White "Fluid Mechanics" В§8.1): Re<2300 вҶ’ "laminar" (AVOID вҖ” thermally stratified, very poor cooling), 2300вүӨRe<4000 вҶ’ "transitional" (unpredictable; avoid), 4000вүӨRe<10000 вҶ’ "turbulent" (Dittus-Boelter valid but h sub-optimal), ReвүҘ10000 вҶ’ "fully_turbulent" (target for mold cooling, Beaumont 2007 В§11). Also computes minimum recommended flow rate [L/min] to reach Re=10000 for the given channel geometry and coolant. Dataclasses: `CoolingFlowSpec` (channel_diameter_mm, flow_rate_L_per_min, coolant_density_kg_m3=1000, coolant_viscosity_cP=1.0); `TurbulentReCheckReport` (reynolds_number, flow_regime, velocity_m_per_s, recommended_min_flow_rate_L_per_min, dittus_boelter_applicable, honest_caveat). Unit conversions: mmвҶ’m, L/minвҶ’mВі/sГ·60000, cPвҶ’PaВ·s. LLM tool `mold_check_turbulent_re` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. **HONEST SCOPE: Re classification ONLY** вҖ” does NOT compute Nusselt number / convective HTC (requires Prandtl number input), polymer-side boundary layer, mold-steel wall thermal resistance, or part-steel contact resistance; does NOT model wall heat flux or non-uniform temperature distribution along the channel; single-phase, isothermal, incompressible, Newtonian fluid only (no two-phase/supercritical COвӮӮ cooling); viscosity spatially uniform (re-run with exit viscosity for О”T > 10 В°C); circular cross-section assumed (non-circular channels: supply hydraulic diameter D_h=4A/P) вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/cooling_turbulent_re_check.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 В§11 (cooling-system Re requirement); White "Fluid Mechanics" 8th ed. В§8.1 (Re thresholds); Incropera & DeWitt "Heat and Mass Transfer" 7th ed. В§8.5 eq. 8.60 (Dittus-Boelter ReвүҘ10000).

**MOLD-CORE-PIN-COOLING** вң… вҖ” `design_core_pin_cooling(CorePinSpec) -> CorePinCoolingReport` in `kerf_mold.core_pin_cooling`. Interior baffle/bubbler cooling design for slender injection-mold core pins (tall rib inserts). Re = 4В·QВ·ПҒ/(ПҖВ·D_hВ·Ој) (volumetric form); Nusselt number Nu = 0.023В·Re^0.8В·Pr^0.4 (Dittus-Boelter, Incropera eq. 8.60); HTC h = NuВ·k_f/D_h; bubbler mode applies a 2Г— HTC multiplier relative to baffle per Menges 2001 В§7.5 and Beaumont 2007 В§11.4 (fountain-effect tip cooling + annular return turbulence). Core-tip temperature from 1-D lumped steady-state resistance network: R_poly = 1/(h_pВ·A_surface) (h_p = 2000 W/mВІK, Menges В§7.1 midpoint); R_steel = L_half/(k_steelВ·A_cross) (k_steel = 15 W/mВ·K P20/H13); R_cool = 1/(hВ·A_bore). Cycle-time estimate by Menges 2001 В§7.3.3 / Chen-Chiang 1985 first-term Fourier: t_c = (h_wallВІ/ПҖВІОұ)В·ln[(8/ПҖВІ)В·(T_meltвҲ’T_cool)/(T_ejectвҲ’T_cool)]; Оұ = 1.0e-7 mВІ/s (ABS baseline). Oracle (30 mm core, 100 mm tall, baffle, 4 mm ID, 2 L/min water at 20 В°C, Pr=7): Re = 10610, Nu = 83.2, HTC = 12445 W/mВІK; bubbler HTC = 24890 W/mВІK (2.000Г— ratio); cycle-time = 248 s. `cooling_adequate = True` iff Re вүҘ 10 000 AND T_tip вүӨ target. `CorePinSpec` dataclass (core_diameter_mm, core_height_mm, baffle_or_bubbler: "baffle"|"bubbler", cooling_type_id_mm, coolant_flow_L_per_min, melt_temp_C, target_core_temp_C, polymer_grade, coolant_temp_C=20, density, viscosity, Pr, k_f); `CorePinCoolingReport` dataclass (reynolds_number, htc_W_per_m2K, estimated_core_tip_temp_C, cooling_adequate, cycle_time_estimate_s, honest_caveat). LLM tool `mold_design_core_pin_cooling` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 33 oracle tests green. **HONEST SCOPE: lumped-capacitance steady-state ONLY** вҖ” no transient FEA; uniform melt temperature assumed (no gate-to-far-end gradient); bubbler 2Г— multiplier is empirical (actual factor depends on tube OD/bore ID ratio, tip clearance, entry turbulence); polymer-side HTC fixed at handbook midpoint 2000 W/mВІK (range 1 000вҖ“4 000 W/mВІK); Dittus-Boelter valid only Re вүҘ 10 000 and L/D вүҘ 10; cycle-time is 1-D Fourier pin half-diameter only (not full mold cycle); confirm with transient FEA (Moldflow Insight / Moldex3D / SigmaSoft) for production tooling вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/core_pin_cooling.py`. Refs: Menges G., Michaeli W., Mohren P. "How to Make Injection Molds" 3rd ed. Hanser 2001 В§7.5 (core-pin cooling) + В§7.1 (polymer HTC) + В§7.3.3 (cooling-time formula); Beaumont J.P. "Runner and Gating Design Handbook" 2nd ed. Hanser 2007 В§11.4 (slender-core cooling; fountain-effect doubling); Incropera & DeWitt "Fundamentals of Heat and Mass Transfer" 7th ed. Wiley 2011 В§8.5 eq. 8.60.

**MOLD-EJECTOR-PIN-PUSH** вң… вҖ” `compute_ejector_pin_push(EjectorPinPushSpec) -> EjectorPinPushReport` in `kerf_mold.ejector_pin_push`. Computes the Euler critical buckling load for an SPI/ANSI B151.1 ejector pin and verifies it against the required push force. Formula: F_cr = ПҖВІВ·EВ·I/(KВ·L)ВІ  (Roark's 9e В§15.2); I = ПҖВ·dвҒҙ/64 (solid round section); E = 200 GPa for all tool-steel grades (M2_tool_steel, H13, S7, D2 вҖ” all share the same nominal Young's modulus). End-condition coefficient K: 1.0 pinned-pinned (SPI/ANSI B151.1 default for guided pins), 0.5 fixed-fixed, 0.7 fixed-pinned, 2.0 cantilever. Dataclasses: `EjectorPinPushSpec` (pin_diameter_mm, pin_length_L_mm, pin_material: "M2_tool_steel"|"H13"|"S7"|"D2", end_condition_K=1.0, required_push_force_N); `EjectorPinPushReport` (buckling_force_N, dcr=required/F_cr, adequate: bool, recommended_min_diameter_mm, recommended_pin_material, honest_caveat). Recommendation logic: searches SPI standard diameters (1, 1.5, 2, 2.5, 3, 4, 5, 6, 8, 10, 12, 16, 20 mm) for the smallest diameter with F_cr вүҘ 1.1 Г— required_push_force_N at the same L and K; prefers M2 when DCR > 0.8. Numeric oracle: 8 mm, L=100 mm, K=1: F_cr = ПҖВіВ·200000В·64/10000 вүҲ 39 688 N; 4 mm pin is 16Г— weaker than 8 mm (I вҲқ dвҒҙ); doubling L reduces F_cr by 4Г—. LLM tool `mold_compute_ejector_pin_push` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 45 oracle tests green. **HONEST SCOPE: Euler formula only** вҖ” non-conservative for short/stout pins (KВ·L/d < 30); use Johnson parabolic formula F_cr_J = AВ·Пғ_yВ·[1 вҲ’ Пғ_yВ·(KВ·L/r)ВІ/(4В·ПҖВІВ·E)] in that regime (function flags the warning in honest_caveat); bushing friction (ОјвүҲ0.05вҖ“0.10 lubricated, reduces capacity 3вҖ“10 %) and pin eccentricity/TIR beam-column amplification (Roark's 9e В§15.3) are NOT modelled; dynamic ejection impact and fatigue over millions of cycles are NOT assessed; confirm by mold-trial load-cell measurement вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/ejector_pin_push.py`. Refs: SPI/ANSI B151.1; Roark R.J. & Young W.C. Formulas for Stress and Strain, 9th ed., В§15.2вҖ“15.3; ASM Handbook Vol.1 (tool-steel E values).

**MOLD-TUNNEL-GATE-DESIGN** вң… вҖ” `design_tunnel_gate(TunnelGateSpec) -> TunnelGateReport` in `kerf_mold.tunnel_gate_design`. Designs a tunnel (submarine) gate given part weight and polymer grade. Diameter: D = 0.5 Г— wall_thickness (Beaumont 2007 В§7.4); +10 % high-viscosity correction for PC/PA66/PMMA/POM/PEI/PPO; lower bound 0.8 mm (machining floor); upper cap D вүӨ 2/3 Г— wall_thickness (Menges 2001 В§6.6.5). Break-off force: F = П„_shear Г— ПҖ/4В·DВІ using Menges 2001 Table 6.3 shear strengths (ABS=30, PC=45, PP=22, PA66=40, POM=38, PMMA=42, PEI=50, PPO=45 MPa). Shear rate: ОіМҮ = 4Q/(ПҖВ·rВі) (Hagen-Poiseuille, Newtonian); Q = (m_part/ПҒ_melt) / 1.0 s; Beaumont В§7.4 limit 50 000 sвҒ»В№; `shear_within_limit` flag. Gate freeze time: t_f = (DВІ/ПҖВІВ·Оұ)В·ln[(8/ПҖВІ)В·(T_meltвҲ’T_mold)/(T_ejectвҲ’T_mold)] per Chen-Chiang ANTEC 1985 / Menges 2001 В§7.3.3. Angle recommendation: 30В° for flexible/low-viscosity, 45В° for stiff/high-viscosity (Menges В§6.6.5). Oracle: ABS, 30 g, wall 2 mm вҶ’ D = 1.0 mm; F_break = 23.6 N; freeze time вүҲ 1.42 s. `TunnelGateSpec` (part_weight_g, wall_thickness_at_gate_mm, polymer_grade, melt_temp_C, gate_angle_deg=30.0, gate_length_mm=1.5); `TunnelGateReport` (gate_diameter_mm, gate_break_off_force_N, gate_freeze_time_s, shear_rate_at_gate_per_s, shear_within_limit, recommended_angle_deg, honest_caveat). LLM tool `mold_design_tunnel_gate` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 35 tests green. **HONEST: Beaumont heuristic вҖ” diameter is a start-point only; complex multi-cavity timing and fill-pressure balance require Moldflow/Moldex3D full 3-D fill simulation; break-off force sensitive to mold temperature and specific resin grade ductility; shear rate is Newtonian approximation (actual shear-thinning ОіМҮ вүҲ 1.25вҖ“1.5Г— higher); freeze time is 1-D Fourier constant-diffusivity (PP/PA66/POM actual 15вҖ“25 % longer due to crystallisation latent heat); confirm by mold trial** вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/tunnel_gate_design.py`. Refs: Beaumont J.P. "Runner and Gating Design Handbook" 2nd ed. Hanser 2007 В§7.4; Menges G., Michaeli W., Mohren P. "How to Make Injection Molds" 3rd ed. Hanser 2001 В§6.6.5 + Table 6.3 + В§7.3.3; Chen-Chiang ANTEC 1985.

**MOLD-SURFACE-FINISH-CHECK** вң… вҖ” `check_surface_finish(SurfaceFinishSpec, MoldSpec) -> SurfaceFinishReport` in `kerf_mold.surface_finish_check`. Validates that a molded part's resin + mold-steel + hardness combination can achieve the requested SPI Mold Finish Standard grade (A1вҖ“D3), and recommends mold steel grade, minimum HRC, and polishing method. SPI grades (2017 standard): A1 Ra вүӨ 0.012 Вөm (diamond paste #3, S136 вүҘ50 HRC), A2 Ra вүӨ 0.025 Вөm (diamond buff #6, S136 вүҘ48 HRC), A3 Ra вүӨ 0.050 Вөm (diamond buff #15, S136/H13 вүҘ44 HRC); B1 Ra вүӨ 0.10 Вөm (600-grit stone, H13 вүҘ38 HRC), B2вҖ“B3 Ra 0.20вҖ“0.40 Вөm (stone, P20); C1вҖ“C3 Ra 0.80вҖ“3.20 Вөm (emery cloth, P20); D1вҖ“D3 Ra 3.2вҖ“14 Вөm (dry blast, P20). Glass-fiber rule (Menges В§11.4.2): glass-reinforced resins cannot achieve A-grade on the molded part regardless of mold polish (fiber pull-out + print-through). Resin limits: PA66 вҶ’ max A3 (crystalline skin haze); PP вҶ’ max B1; POM вҶ’ max B2; LDPE вҶ’ max C1. Steel limits: S136 вҶ’ A1; 420SS вҶ’ A2; H13 вҶ’ A3; P20 вҶ’ B3. Dataclasses: `SurfaceFinishSpec` (required_finish, resin); `MoldSpec` (mold_steel, hardness_HRC, mold_finish_achieved=""); `SurfaceFinishReport` (achievable, recommended_steel, recommended_hardness_HRC_min, recommended_polishing_method, Ra_target_um, Ra_achievable_um, glass_filled_warning, honest_caveat). LLM tool `mold_check_surface_finish` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 27 tests green. **HONEST: catalog-based checker вҖ” does NOT model texture chemistry (etching achievability depends on etch bath + resin crystallinity), etcher capability (bath concentration + cycle count not modelled), polishing wear-life (abrasive filler content + shot count not modelled), part-geometry effects (weld lines + deep ribs harder to polish), or process variables (mold temperature, hold pressure, cooling time affect surface replication fidelity)** вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/surface_finish_check.py`. Refs: SPI/PLASTICS Mold Finish Standards 2017; Menges G., Mohren P. "How to Make Injection Molds" 3rd ed. Hanser 2001 В§11; Bryce D. M. "Plastic Injection Molding: Mold Design and Construction Fundamentals" SME 1998 Ch. 8.

**MOLD-COLOR-CONCENTRATE-RATIO** вң… вҖ” `compute_color_ratio(ColorConcentrateSpec, ShotSpec) -> ColorRatioReport` in `kerf_mold.color_concentrate_ratio`. Gravimetric let-down ratio (LDR) dosing and mixing-quality assessment for color concentrate (masterbatch) in injection moulding. LDR formula (SPI Color Concentrates Handbook 3rd ed. В§3): LDR (%) = target_pigment_loading_pct / pigment_loading_in_masterbatch_pct Г— 100. Masterbatch per shot [g] = shot_weight_g Г— LDR/100; masterbatch per kg natural resin [g/kg] = 1000 Г— (LDR/100) / (1 вҲ’ LDR/100). SPI recommended LDR range: 1вҖ“5 %. Mixing index heuristic (Menges Plastics Manufacturing В§10.2; Tadmor & Gogos В§12.5): mixing_index = 1 вҲ’ exp(вҲ’barrel_residence_s Г— screw_L/D / 200); adequate if > 0.80. Streaking-risk classification: low (LDR 1вҖ“5 % AND mixing_index > 0.80), moderate (marginal LDR 0.5вҖ“1 % or 5вҖ“8 %, or mixing_index вүӨ 0.80 with LDR in range), high (LDR < 0.5 % вҖ” too dilute for shot-to-shot uniformity вҖ” or LDR > 8 % вҖ” cost-waste territory / mechanical-property dilution risk per Menges В§10.4). Dataclasses: `ColorConcentrateSpec` (pigment_loading_in_masterbatch_pct, recommended_let_down_pct, carrier_resin, melting_temp_C); `ShotSpec` (shot_weight_g, target_pigment_loading_pct, barrel_residence_time_s, screw_L_over_D=20.0); `ColorRatioReport` (let_down_ratio_pct, masterbatch_per_shot_g, masterbatch_per_kg_natural, mixing_index_estimate, color_streaking_risk, warnings, honest_caveat). Oracle: 100 g shot, target 1 % pigment, MB at 40 % вҶ’ LDR = 2.5 %, MB = 2.5 g/shot, MB per kg natural вүҲ 25.64 g/kg. LLM tool `mold_compute_color_concentrate_ratio` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 40 tests green. **HONEST: mixing index is a heuristic exponential-decay proxy from L/D and residence time only вҖ” does NOT model screw-flight geometry, back-pressure, screw speed, melt-viscosity mismatch between masterbatch carrier and natural resin, pellet size ratio, or colorant particle agglomerate size; LDR is gravimetric only (volumetric accuracy requires density-matched MB and natural resin); streaking-risk classification is a screening guideline вҖ” trial colour plaques with L*a*b* colorimetric measurement per ISO 11664-4 are the only reliable acceptance test; carrier resin compatibility must be confirmed against base resin; empirical mixing estimate, NOT a substitute for colour-master trial shots** вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/color_concentrate_ratio.py`. Refs: SPI "Color Concentrates Handbook" 3rd ed. В§3, В§6, В§8, В§11; Menges G., Kemper B., Klenk E. "Plastics Manufacturing" В§10; Tadmor Z. & Gogos C. "Principles of Polymer Processing" 2nd ed. Wiley 2006, В§12.5.

**ARCH-BASE-PLATE-AISC (AISC DG-1 В§3.1 + AISC 360-22 В§J8)** вң… вҖ” `design_base_plate(ColumnSpec, ConcreteSpec, Fy=345.0) -> BasePlateReport` implements steel column base plate design for concentric axial compressive loads. Concrete bearing strength: Pp = 0.85В·f'cВ·A1В·вҲҡ(A2/A1) with A2/A1 вүӨ 4 (AISC 360-22 В§J8 Eq J8-2); ПҶ_c = 0.65; required A1 = P_u/(ПҶ_cВ·0.85В·f'cВ·вҲҡ(A2/A1)). Plate dimensions rounded up to nearest 5 mm; must cover column footprint (0.95В·d Г— 0.80В·bf per DG-1 В§3.1.1). Cantilever arms: m=(NвҲ’0.95В·d)/2 (Eq 3.1-1); n=(BвҲ’0.80В·bf)/2 (Eq 3.1-2); n'=вҲҡ(dВ·bf)/4; X=[4В·dВ·bf/(d+bf)ВІ]В·[P_u/(ПҶ_cВ·Pp)] (Eq 3.1-8); О»=min(1, 2В·вҲҡX/(1+вҲҡ(1вҲ’X))); l=max(m,n,О»В·n'). Plate thickness via Murray-Stockwell (DG-1 Eq 3.1-5): t=lВ·вҲҡ(2В·P_u/(0.9В·FyВ·BВ·N)), rounded up to 1 mm. Oracle: W14x90, P=1000 kN, f'c=30 MPa, ped 600Г—600 mm вҶ’ A1_reqвүҲ30166 mmВІ; plate 295Г—340 mm (column footprint governs, N_min=338 mm, B_min=295 mm); t=15 mm; DCR=0.318 (adequate). `arch_design_base_plate` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import). Re-exported from arch/__init__.py. 24 hermetic oracle tests pass вҖ” `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/base_plate_aisc.py`. *SCOPE: concentric axial compressive load ONLY (DG-1 В§3.1). NOT covered: moment transfer (DG-1 В§3.2), anchor rod design (DG-1 В§3.3вҖ“3.4), shear lug (DG-1 В§3.5), biaxial bending, tensile uplift. A2 taken as pedestal plan area; irregular pedestals must supply equivalent rectangular A2. Grout strength вүҘ f'c assumed.*
