**Manufacturing depth** вң… вҖ” **MOLD-DRAFT-DEMOLD-FORCE** (Beaumont 2007 В§9.3 + Menges 2001 В§7.4 + Table 7.6): `compute_demold_force()` вҖ” cavity-ejection force per F = ОјВ·Пғ_hВ·AВ·cosОұ/(cosОұ + ОјВ·sinОұ); shrinkage stress Пғ_h from Menges Table 7.6 (ABS=4.0, PC=3.0, PP=5.0, PA66=3.5, POM=4.5 MPa); friction Ој from SPI finish class (SPI_A1=0.15 polished вҖҰ SPI_D1=0.40 textured); `MoldedPartSpec` dataclass (polymer_grade, contact_area_cm2, draft_angle_deg, mold_steel_finish_class); `DemoldForceReport` dataclass (demold_force_N, contact_pressure_MPa, ejector_pin_count_required, friction_coeff_used, polymer_shrinkage_stress_MPa, honest_caveat); ejector pin count = ceil(F / single_pin_capacity_N); LLM tool `mold_compute_demold_force` registered; 28 oracle tests; honest-flagged: empirical formula only вҖ” ignores chemical adhesion (resin stick, relevant for PC/POM on polished steel), undercut/side-action geometry, dynamic ejection force, and pin fatigue; confirm by mold-trial load-cell measurement вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/demold_force_check.py` вң….
**Manufacturing depth** вң… вҖ” **MOLD-VENT-DEPTH-CHECK** (Beaumont 2007 В§8.3 Table 8.2 + Menges 2001 В§6.4 Table 6.7): `check_vent_depth()` вҖ” verify that a mold parting-line vent depth (air-escape gap) is within the polymer-specific recommended range; too shallow вҶ’ trapped air вҶ’ short shot / burn marks (diesel effect); too deep вҶ’ flash; polymer database (mm): ABS 0.025вҖ“0.038, PC 0.013вҖ“0.025, PP 0.025вҖ“0.050, PA66 0.013вҖ“0.025, POM 0.013вҖ“0.025, PMMA 0.025вҖ“0.038, PE 0.038вҖ“0.075; `VentSpec` dataclass (polymer_grade, proposed_depth_mm, land_length_mm=1.5, vent_width_mm=6.0); `VentDepthReport` dataclass (recommended_depth_min_mm, recommended_depth_max_mm, compliant, depth_class, polymer_notes, honest_caveat); depth_class: "too_shallow"|"correct"|"too_deep"|"flash_risk" (>25% above max); unknown polymers receive fallback range [0.013вҖ“0.038 mm] with caveat; LLM tool `mold_check_vent_depth` registered; 35 oracle tests; honest-flagged: empirical handbook ranges only вҖ” actual safe vent depth depends on resin batch viscosity, melt temperature, injection speed, mold surface finish, land length, and part geometry; filled/FR/rubber-toughened grades may flash within the correct band for base resin; confirm by mold trial + visual flash inspection вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/vent_depth_check.py` вң….
**Manufacturing depth** вң… вҖ” **MOLD-VENT-SLOT-LAYOUT** (Beaumont 2007 В§8.5 Vent Slot Count and Width + Menges 2001 В§6.4): `generate_vent_slot_layout()` вҖ” propose vent slot count, width (6 mm standard), and spacing for a parting-line perimeter given cavity volume, polymer grade, and injection speed; Beaumont 0.5 %-projected-area rule: total_vent_area вүҘ 0.005 Г— cavity_volume_mmВі/wall_thickness; speed scaling: vent_area_factor = max(1.0, injection_speed / 50 cmВі/s); per-slot area = 6 mm width Г— depth_mid Г— 6 mm land length (polymer-specific depth from Beaumont Table 8.2); minimum 4 slots (one per quadrant, Beaumont В§8.5; Menges В§6.4); maximum slots = floor(perimeter / (6 + 10 mm steel bridge)); spacing = perimeter / n_slots; `MoldVolumeSpec` dataclass (cavity_volume_cm3, parting_line_perimeter_mm, polymer_grade, injection_speed_cm3_s); `VentSlotLayoutReport` dataclass (num_vent_slots, vent_slot_width_mm, vent_slot_spacing_mm, total_vent_width_mm, air_displacement_rate_cm3_s, adequate, honest_caveat); LLM tool `mold_generate_vent_slot_layout` registered; 47 oracle tests; honest-flagged: heuristic 0.5 %-area rule from production experience вҖ” NOT a first-principles fluid-dynamic calculation; wall thickness assumed 3 mm for area estimation; uniform spacing only (use mold_optimize_vent_placement for last-to-fill location optimisation); vent depth handled separately by mold_check_vent_depth; confirm by fill simulation (Moldflow / Moldex3D / SigmaSoft) + mold-trial visual inspection вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/vent_slot_layout.py` вң….
**Manufacturing depth** вң… вҖ” **MOLD-RUNNER-COLD-SLUG** (Beaumont 2007 В§6.7 Cold Slug Wells + Menges 2001 В§6.5): `check_cold_slug_design()` вҖ” verify cold-slug well dimensions at runner junctions in a multi-cavity mold to trap the cold leading-edge polymer melt before it reaches the gate, preventing flow lines and weak weld lines; Beaumont rule: slug well diameter = 1.5 Г— runner diameter, depth = 2.0 Г— runner diameter, Вұ20 % tolerance band (1.2Г—вҖ“1.8Г— diameter, 1.6Г—вҖ“2.4Г— depth); `RunnerJunctionSpec` dataclass (junction_id, runner_diameter_mm, slug_well_diameter_mm, slug_well_depth_mm, polymer_grade); `ColdSlugReport` dataclass (junction_results list, total_junctions, compliant_count, honest_caveat); per-junction result: diameter_compliant, depth_compliant, slug_well_compliant, recommended_diameter_mm, recommended_depth_mm, tolerance bounds, reason; LLM tool `mold_check_cold_slug_design` registered; 32 oracle tests; honest-flagged: geometric rule-of-thumb only вҖ” actual cold-slug capture depends on melt temperature, injection speed, and resin freeze-off time; fast-crystallising resins (POM, PA66, LCP) and filled grades may require larger wells; confirm by mold trial + gate-area visual inspection; use Moldflow / Moldex3D / SigmaSoft for full melt-front thermal and weld-line simulation вҖ” `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/cold_slug_check.py` вң….

**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + MВІ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected; **Zernike polynomial wavefront fitting** (OPTICS-ZERNIKE-WAVEFRONT-FIT): first 15 Noll-ordered terms (j=1..15, piston through tetrafoil); explicit Z_j(ПҒ,Оё) formulas (Noll 1976 Table 1 orthonormal basis); least-squares fit via numpy.linalg.lstsq; RMS residual; dominant aberration = argmax(|c_j|) for jвүҘ2 (piston excluded); LLM tool `optics_fit_zernike_wavefront`; 32 hermetic tests. **Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + MВІ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected; **sequential paraxial + meridional ray trace** through multi-element lens stacks (Welford 1986 В§3.3/В§5, exact Snell + Newton-Raphson conic intersect; EFL/BFL/FFL; Hecht oracle biconvex BK7 <0.1% error; Cooke triplet converging verified); **MTF across field angle** (OPTICS-MTF-ACROSS-FIELD) вҖ” ray-bundle PSF histogram + numpy.fft.rfft pipeline; tangential MTF curves at multiple field angles; BK7 biconvex off-axis MTF drop verified; LLM tool `optics_mtf_across_field` (monochromatic; polychromatic MTF out of scope).
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + MВІ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); **Seidel third-order aberrations** (OPTICS-SEIDEL-ABERRATIONS): five Seidel coefficients S_I..S_V via dual paraxial-ray trace (Welford 1986 В§6.2 / Born & Wolf В§5.3); per-surface breakdown; LLM tool `optics_seidel_aberrations`; 33 hermetic tests.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Chief-ray vignetting + relative illumination** (OPTICS-CHIEF-RAY-VIGNETTING): marginal-ray bundle traced at each field angle; per-surface clear-aperture clipping check; RI = surviving fraction; cosвҒҙ(Оё) photometric baseline; excess-vignetting ratio; LLM tool `optics_compute_vignetting` (Welford 1986 В§4.5 / Hecht В§6.6; circular symmetric apertures; 33 hermetic tests).
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **2-D relative illumination map** (OPTICS-RELATIVE-ILLUM-MAP): extends vignetting analysis to a full (grid Г— grid) heatmap across the image plane; for each (x, y) sensor position computes Оё = arctan(r/EFL) and evaluates RI(Оё) = surviving ray fraction via compute_vignetting; ri_map (aperture-clipping model) + cos4_map (natural cosвҒҙ(Оё) photometric baseline, Hecht В§6.6 / Slyusarev В§3.4); rotational-symmetry shortcut (1-D radial pre-computation, full 2-D output for visualisation); corner_ri + corner_cos4 diagnostics; BK7 biconvex @ sensor_half_height=60 mm вҶ’ Оё_corner вүҲ 60В°, cos4_corner вүҲ 0.063; LLM tool `optics_compute_relative_illum_map`; 38 hermetic tests. Honest: monochromatic only; rotationally-symmetric stack assumed; sensor tilt / telecentricity not modelled. Ref: Welford 1986 В§4.5; Hecht В§6.6; Slyusarev В§3.4.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Spot diagrams + pupil illumination maps** (OPTICS-PUPIL-DIAGRAM): uniform pupil-grid ray trace (Welford 1986 В§8.2); per-field intercept loci at image plane; 2-D RMS + meridional y-only RMS spot radius; max ray distance from chief ray; exit-pupil illumination map (surviving pupil coords); paraxial exit-pupil position estimate (Welford 1986 В§3.5 / Hecht В§5.7); stigmatic stack вҶ’ RMS < 1e-6 mm; BK7 biconvex at 14В° вҶ’ y-RMS > 3Г— on-axis; Seidel coma cross-check; LLM tool `optics_pupil_diagram` (monochromatic; sagittal x = first-order estimate; 33 hermetic tests).
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Through-focus defocus curve** (OPTICS-DEFOCUS-CURVE): Welford 1986 В§11.5 / Hecht В§6.5; per-О”z meridional RMS spot-size via exact Snell + Newton-Raphson conic intersect; best-focus shift quantified; parabolic curve verified for paraxial singlet (min at О”z=0); spherical-aberration-shifted minimum verified for full-aperture BK7 singlet (О”zвүҲвҲ’0.5 mm); field-angle dependency; LLM tool `optics_defocus_curve`; 33 hermetic tests. **Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Geometric distortion map** (OPTICS-DISTORTION-MAP): chief-ray tangential distortion vs field angle (Hecht В§5.6 / Welford 1986 В§6.3); D=(y_actualвҲ’y_paraxial)/|y_paraxial|Г—100; barrel (D<0) / pincushion (D>0) / mixed classification; Seidel S_V third-order cross-check (Welford В§6.3); BK7 biconvex singlet shows measurable barrel distortion at moderate field (>0.5% at 20В°); kind classification verified for high-power singlet and telephoto stacks; LLM tool `optics_distortion_map`; 30 hermetic tests. Honest: monochromatic only; tangential (meridional) distortion only; stop assumed at first surface.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Coma aberration metrics** (OPTICS-COMA-COMPUTE): comatic flare length from pupil-rim ray bundle trace (Welford 1986 В§11.4 / Born & Wolf В§5.3); for each field angle traces N marginal rays at entrance-pupil rim azimuths and propagates to paraxial focal plane; tangential coma = mean Y-displacement of tangential-fan rays from chief-ray image point; sagittal coma = tangential/3 (Welford В§11.4 eq. 11.4.4); total coma = sqrt(tanВІ+sagВІ); Seidel S_II prediction = 3Г—|S_II|Г—|y_chief| (Born & Wolf В§5.3 eq. 5.3.29); depth bar: BK7 biconvex at 14В° вҶ’ coma > 1 Ојm; Seidel match < 0.1% at 5В° field; LLM tool `optics_compute_coma`; 33 hermetic tests. Honest: third-order coma only; higher-order (Hopkins 5th-order, oblique spherical aberration) requires finite-ray OPD analysis; monochromatic only; stop at first surface.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Seidel coma coefficient S_II** (OPTICS-SEIDEL-COMA): per-surface third-order Seidel coma sum S_II = ОЈ (вҲ’A_jВ·ДҖ_jВ·h_jВ·О”(u/n)_j) via dual paraxial-ray trace (Welford 1986 В§7 eq. 7.42 / Born & Wolf В§5.3); SeidelComaReport dataclass: S_II (total Seidel coma sum), coma_waves_at_lambda (|3В·S_IIВ·y_chief|/(8О»)), dominant_surface_idx (argmax|S_II_j|), per_surface_contributions (A, ДҖ, h, ybar, delta_un, SII_contrib per surface), honest_caveat; BK7 biconvex R1=+50/R2=вҲ’50 mm on-axis вҶ’ coma_waves = 0; same lens at 5В° вҶ’ S_II nonzero; aplanatic BK7+SF2 contact doublet вҶ’ |S_II| reduced vs singlet; flat slab вҶ’ S_II = 0 exactly; LLM tool `optics_compute_seidel_coma`; 34 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial Seidel only; no chromatic coma; no defocus residual; stop at first surface; higher-order coma not modelled. Ref: Welford (1986) В§7 eq. 7.42; Born & Wolf (1999) В§5.3 eq. 5.3.29; Kingslake (1978).
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Seidel coma coefficient (thin-lens polynomial)** (OPTICS-COMA-COEFFICIENT): closed-form S_II and Hopkins W_131 for a single thin lens via Welford В§7.4 shape-factor/conjugate-factor polynomial; `ThinLensSpec(focal_length_mm, refractive_index_n, aperture_radius_mm, shape_factor_q, conjugate_factor_p)` + `ImageSpec(object_height_mm, image_distance_mm)` вҶ’ `ComaCoefficientReport(seidel_S_II, wave_aberration_W_131, sagittal_coma_arcsec, tangential_coma_arcsec=3Г—sagittal, coma_blur_mm, q_aplanatic, honest_caveat)`; formula: S_II = u_barВ·hВіВ·ПҶВІВ·[(n+1)/(2n(nвҲ’1))В·q + (вҲ’(2n+1)/(2n))В·(p+2)] where q=(RвӮҒ+RвӮӮ)/(RвӮҒвҲ’RвӮӮ) and p=(uвҖІ+u)/(uвҖІвҲ’u); numerically verified vs two-surface paraxial trace across qвҲҲ{вҲ’1,вҲ’0.5,0,0.5,1} and pвҲҲ{вҲ’1,0,1} for nвҲҲ{1.4,1.5,1.5168,1.6,1.7,1.8} (all within 1e-10 relative); aplanatic shape q=(2n+1)(nвҲ’1)(p+2)/(n+1) gives S_II=0 exactly; BK7 (n=1.5168, p=вҲ’1): q_aplanaticвүҲ0.8283; angular coma = S_II/(8В·F#В·v)Г—206265 arcsec; W_131=вҲ’S_II (Hopkins sign convention, Born & Wolf В§5.5.3); LLM tool `optics_compute_coma_coefficient`; 25 hermetic tests. Honest: third-order Seidel only вҖ” fifth-order Schwarzschild coma and higher-order Hopkins terms NOT included; single thin lens in air; stop coincident with lens; monochromatic only. Ref: Welford (1986) В§7.4; Born & Wolf (1999) В§5.3 eq. 5.3.29 + В§5.5.3; Smith MOE (2008) В§4.3.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + MВІ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected. **Longitudinal chromatic aberration** (OPTICS-CHROMATIC-FOCUS): Sellmeier dispersion n(О») = sqrt(1 + ОЈ B_i О»ВІ/(О»ВІвҲ’C_i)) for BK7/F2/SF6/K5/SF11/BK10 (Schott catalog 2023); per-wavelength BFL via ABCD thin-lens stack; LCA_FC = BFL(486nm)вҲ’BFL(656nm); Abbe V-number (singlet); BK7 VвүҲ64.2 verified; achromat LCA < 0.1 mm verified; LLM tool `optics_compute_chromatic_focus`; 34 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial thin-lens LCA only; chromatic lateral aberration not computed.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Abbe number + partial dispersion** (OPTICS-ABBE-NUMBER-COMPUTE): V_d = (n_d вҲ’ 1) / (n_F вҲ’ n_C) from Sellmeier Fraunhofer lines d/F/C (Hecht В§6.3 / ISO 10110); secondary spectrum partial dispersion P_{F,g} = (n_g вҲ’ n_F) / (n_F вҲ’ n_C) for g-line (435.84 nm); six glasses BK7/F2/SF6/K5/SF11/BK10 (Schott 2023); BK7 V_d = 64.17, F2 = 36.37, SF6 = 25.43, K5 = 59.45, BK10 = 66.95 вҖ” all within 0.1% of catalog; SF11 = 25.37 (catalog 25.76, 1.5% gap documented вҖ” Sellmeier fit vs direct spectrophotometric measurement, Schott TIE-29 В§3.3); LLM tool `optics_compute_abbe_number`; 30 hermetic tests. Honest: catalog nominal/melt-mean coefficients; melt-to-melt V_d variation Вұ0.3вҖ“0.5% (Schott TIE-31).
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” Gaussian beam (complex-q + ABCD + MВІ + fibre coupling); non-sequential ray tracing + ghost detection; wave-domain room acoustics (image-source IR + Schroeder RT60 + SEA); Seidel S5 corrected.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **2-D relative illumination map** (OPTICS-RELATIVE-ILLUM-MAP): extends vignetting analysis to a full (grid Г— grid) heatmap across the image plane; for each (x, y) sensor position computes Оё = arctan(r/EFL) and evaluates RI(Оё) = surviving ray fraction via compute_vignetting; ri_map (aperture-clipping model: all 1.0 with no CA, drops with finite CAs) + cos4_map (natural cosвҒҙ(Оё) photometric baseline, Hecht В§6.6 / Slyusarev В§3.4); rotational-symmetry shortcut (1-D radial pre-computation, full 2-D output for visualisation); corner_ri + corner_cos4 diagnostics; BK7 biconvex @ sensor_half_height=60 mm вҶ’ Оё_corner вүҲ 60В°, cos4_corner вүҲ 0.063; LLM tool `optics_compute_relative_illum_map`; 38 hermetic tests. **Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Entrance pupil position + size** (OPTICS-ENTRANCE-PUPIL-POS): paraxial reverse-trace of a marginal ray from the aperture stop through the front sub-stack (Welford 1986 В§4.4 / Hecht В§6.6); position_z_mm from first surface vertex; D-element transverse magnification; converging front вҶ’ real pupil (positive z); diverging front вҶ’ virtual pupil (negative z); LLM tool `optics_compute_entrance_pupil`; 38 hermetic tests. **Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Exit pupil position + size** (OPTICS-EXIT-PUPIL-POS): paraxial two-ray forward trace from the aperture stop through the rear sub-stack (Welford 1986 В§4.4 / Hecht В§6.6); position_z_mm from last surface vertex; radius from stop-edge ray height at exit pupil plane; thin-lens identity (stop at last surface вҶ’ EP at z=0, m=1); BK7 biconvex вҶ’ virtual exit pupil (zвүҲвҲ’3.41 mm, Welford В§4.4 oracle); afocal telescope (f_obj=100 mm, f_eye=25 mm) вҶ’ Ramsden disk at z=31.25 mm, radius=1.25 mm, m=0.25=1/M_telescope (Hecht В§6.6 oracle); LLM tool `optics_compute_exit_pupil`; 43 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial only; entrance pupil is a separate computation; stop modelled as thin plane; paraxial approx degrades for f/# < 2.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Diffraction-limited MTF for circular aperture** (OPTICS-MTF-DIFFRACTION-LIMITED): closed-form on-axis MTF(ОҪ) = (2/ПҖ)[arccos(ОҪ/ОҪвӮҖ) вҲ’ (ОҪ/ОҪвӮҖ)В·вҲҡ(1вҲ’(ОҪ/ОҪвӮҖ)ВІ)] for ОҪ вүӨ ОҪвӮҖ, 0 otherwise; cutoff ОҪвӮҖ = 1/(О»В·F#) (Goodman "Introduction to Fourier Optics" В§6.4 eq. 6-49; Hecht "Optics" 5e В§11.3.3); oracle: О»=550nm, F/4 вҶ’ ОҪвӮҖ=454.5 cyc/mm, MTF(0)=1.0, MTF(ОҪвӮҖ/2)вүҲ0.391 вҖ” all validated to < 0.1%; LLM tool `optics_compute_diffraction_mtf`; 36 hermetic tests. Honest: diffraction-limited theoretical upper bound only вҖ” no aberrations (Seidel S_IвҖ“S_V), no defocus, no wavefront error, no sensor MTF; monochromatic only (polychromatic = вҲ«W(О»)В·MTF(О»)dО», not implemented); on-axis only; circular aperture only.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Pixel aperture MTF + Nyquist limit** (OPTICS-PIXEL-MTF): `PixelSensorSpec(pixel_pitch_um, fill_factor=1.0)` вҶ’ `PixelMtfReport(nyquist_freq_cyc_per_mm, mtf_curve, mtf_at_nyquist, mtf_at_50_percent_nyquist, honest_caveat)`; pixel aperture MTF = |sinc(ПҖВ·aВ·ОҪ)| where a = pitchВ·fill_factor (Boreman "MTF in Optical and Electro-Optical Systems" В§3.4; Hecht В§11.3); Nyquist limit ОҪ_N = 1/(2В·p) caps detectable spatial frequency; oracle (p=1.5Ојm, ff=1.0): ОҪ_N=333.33 cyc/mm, MTF(0)=1.0 exactly, MTF(ОҪ_N)=2/ПҖвүҲ0.6366 вҖ” all validated to < 1e-6; fill_factor < 1 вҶ’ narrower aperture вҶ’ slower sinc roll-off вҶ’ MTF at Nyquist > 2/ПҖ (verified: ff=0.5 вҶ’ MTF(ОҪ_N)вүҲ0.900); `combine_mtf_curves(optical, pixel)` for incoherent cascade MTF_system = MTF_optical Г— MTF_pixel (Boreman В§2.1); LLM tool `optics_compute_pixel_mtf`; 36 hermetic tests. Honest: PIXEL APERTURE SINC ONLY вҖ” NOT modelled: silicon carrier-diffusion MTF (lateral minority-carrier spread vs. depth, Boreman В§3.4); inter-pixel electrical/optical crosstalk; anti-aliasing filter MTF; Bayer CFA demosaicing resolution loss; charge-transfer inefficiency (CCD); non-square pixels; 2-D MTF = product of independent 1-D sincs for square pixel. Ref: Boreman (2001) В§3.4, В§2.1; Hecht (2017) В§11.3; Holst & Lomheim (2007) В§5.3. `kerf-cad-core/optics/pixel_mtf.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Petzval field curvature** (OPTICS-PETZVAL-CURVATURE-COMPUTE): Petzval sum P = ОЈ (n_after вҲ’ n_before) / (n_before В· n_after В· R_i) (Hecht В§6.3.2 / Born & Wolf В§4.5); Petzval radius R_P = 1/P; flat-field score 1/(1+|P|В·100); BK7 biconvex oracle (R1=+50, R2=вҲ’50, n=1.5168): P вүҲ 0.01363 mmвҒ»В№, R_P вүҲ 73.4 mm (within 1%); flat-field condition ОЈПҶ/n = 0 вҶ’ P = 0 verified; plano surfaces (|R|=1e18) contribute 0; stop-shift invariance; per-surface breakdown with is_plano flag; LLM tool `optics_compute_petzval_curvature`; 26 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial (third-order) only; does NOT include astigmatism (S_III term); P=0 guarantees flat Petzval sphere but not zero field curvature in the presence of astigmatism (Hecht В§6.3.2); thick-lens pupil-shift corrections not modelled.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Spot diagram + encircled energy** (OPTICS-SPOT-DIAGRAM): fan-of-rays trace through sequential lens system; ceil(sqrt(num_rays)) Г— ceil(sqrt(num_rays)) Cartesian pupil grid over unit disk (Welford 1986 В§8.2); exact meridional y-intercept via Snell + Newton-Raphson conic intersect (Welford В§5.2-5.3); first-order sagittal x estimate (Hecht В§5.7); `SpotDiagramResult` dataclass: image_points_xy (list[(float,float)], mm), rms_radius_mm (Welford В§8.2 RMS), encircled_80pct_radius_mm (geometric EE80 radius, Hecht В§6.3), centroid_xy, svg_diagram (SVG with RMS/EE80/Airy-disk rings + centroid marker + scale bar), honest_caveat; weak-lens paraxial singlet on-axis вҶ’ near-zero y-spread; BK7 biconvex singlet at 10В° вҶ’ rms > on-axis (coma verified; Hecht В§6.3 / Welford В§6); EE80 вүҘ RMS monotonically; LLM tool `optics_compute_spot_diagram` (monochromatic only; sagittal x = first-order estimate; no chromatic dispersion; single wavelength; stop at first surface; 24 hermetic tests). Ref: Hecht (2017) В§6.3, В§10.2; Welford (1986) В§5.2-5.3, В§6, В§8.2.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Piston/tip/tilt/defocus wavefront alignment analysis** (OPTICS-WAVEFRONT-PISTON-TIP-TILT): extracts ZвӮҒ (piston), ZвӮӮ (tip), ZвӮғ (tilt), ZвӮ„ (defocus) Noll-ordered Zernike alignment components from a sampled wavefront W(ПҒ,Оё); reports each in waves at a given wavelength via W_nm / wavelength_nm conversion; reuses fit_zernike_wavefront (4-term least-squares, numpy.linalg.lstsq, Noll 1976 orthonormal basis); `PistonTipTiltReport` dataclass (piston_waves, tip_waves, tilt_waves, defocus_waves, residual_rms_waves, dominant_misalignment, honest_caveat); dominant = argmax(|c_j|) for j=1..4 with "none" below 0.001 wave threshold; LLM tool `optics_analyze_wavefront_alignment`; 45 hermetic tests (pure piston 10nm @ О»=632.8nm вҶ’ 0.01580 waves verified; pure tip/tilt/defocus; combined misalignment; higher-order residual; error-path). Honest: circular unit-disk pupil only (ПҒ вҲҲ [0,1]; no obscuration or elliptical aperture); alignment analysis only вҖ” corrects rigid-body misalignment (piston = axial OPD offset, tip/tilt = wavefront tilt, defocus = longitudinal focus); does NOT correct higher-order aberrations (coma, astigmatism, spherical, etc.); use optics_fit_zernike_wavefront for full 15-term decomposition. Ref: Hecht (2017) В§11.3; Born & Wolf (1999) В§9.2; Wyant & Creath (1992) Applied Optics and Optical Engineering XI ch.1; Noll (1976) J. Opt. Soc. Am. 66 207.

**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Sagitta arrow chart** (OPTICS-SAGITTA-ARROW-CHART): conic + even-power aspheric surface sagitta z(r) sampled across the clear aperture; standard ISO 10110-12 В§6.2 / Welford В§3.3 formula z = cВ·rВІ/(1+вҲҡ(1вҲ’(1+k)cВІrВІ)) + ОЈaбөўВ·r^(2i+4); SVG chart with horizontal axis = radius (mm), vertical = sagitta (mm), arrow markers at every 5th sample showing local slope dz/dr; `AsphericSurfaceSpec` dataclass (radius_mm, conic_k, aspheric_coeffs, clear_aperture_radius_mm); `SagittaArrowChartResult` (sagitta_samples, max_sagitta_mm, conic_only_sagitta_mm, aspheric_contribution_mm, svg_chart, honest_caveat); sphere R=50 r=10 oracle zвүҲ1.0102 verified < 1e-6; paraboloid k=вҲ’1 z=rВІ/(2R) exact; hemisphere z=R at edge; domain-violation guard (radicand вүҘ 0 + fp-epsilon clamp); LLM tool `optics_compute_sagitta_arrow_chart`; 28 hermetic tests. Honest: standard conic + even-power polynomial asphere ONLY; no Zernike / freeform / XY-polynomial / Q-polynomial / off-axis / tilted surface support; arrow markers show dz/dr (slope), not surface normal; ISO 10110-12:2019. Ref: Welford (1986) В§3.3; ISO 10110-12:2019.

**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Vignetting fraction check** (OPTICS-VIGNETTING-CHECK): computes the fraction of entrance-pupil area occluded by clear-aperture limits at a given field angle; `LensClearApertureSpec` dataclass (surfaces: list of {clear_aperture_radius_mm, axial_position_mm}); `VignettingReport` dataclass (field_angle_deg, vignetting_pct, limiting_surface_idx, effective_pupil_area_pct, honest_caveat); `compute_vignetting(spec, field_angle_deg, marginal_ray_at_stop_mm=10.0)` вҖ” paraxial chief-ray displacement О”_j = z_jВ·tan(Оё); effective pupil area = exact two-circle intersection area (Weisstein formula) of entrance-pupil disk (radius R) with per-surface CA disk (radius r_j, centred at О”_j); vignetting_pct = (1 вҲ’ A_eff/A_full)Г—100; limiting_surface_idx = argmin of per-surface intersection areas; on-axis (field=0В°) вҶ’ vignetting=0 verified; wide-angle (30В°) with tight CA вҶ’ significant clipping verified; LLM tool `optics_compute_vignetting_check`; 34 hermetic tests. Honest: paraxial chief-ray displacement only (no exact ray trace through glass); circular, rotationally-symmetric CAs only; diffraction-induced vignetting NOT modelled; chromatic pupil walk NOT modelled. Ref: Welford (1986) В§3.7; Hecht (2017) В§5.7.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Telecentricity check** (OPTICS-TELECENTRICITY): `compute_telecentricity(lens_system_dict, field_height_mm=10.0, focus_shift_mm=0.5)` вҶ’ `TelecentricityReport(chief_ray_angle_object_deg, chief_ray_angle_image_deg, object_telecentric, image_telecentric, both_telecentric, max_magnification_variation_pct, honest_caveat)`; paraxial chief-ray trace via Welford nu-form (`nвҖІuвҖІ = nu вҲ’ hc(nвҖІвҲ’n)`); chief-ray solved by superposition: Ray A (H, 0) + ОұВ·Ray B (object-dist, 1) at first surface, Оұ = вҲ’h_A_stop/h_B_stop forces h=0 at aperture stop; object-space telecentric вҶ” |angle_obj| < 0.5В°; image-space telecentric вҶ” |angle_img| < 0.5В°; magnification variation across Вұfocus_shift_mm computed from u_last of marginal field ray relative to Lagrange-invariant reference magnification; oracle: single-lens (f=100 mm, stop at front focal plane from 5 m object) вҶ’ object_telecentric=True, image_telecentric=False; doubly-telecentric relay (two equal lenses, stop at shared focal plane) вҶ’ both_telecentric=True; LLM tool `optics_compute_telecentricity`; 25 hermetic tests. Honest: PARAXIAL (first-order) ONLY вҖ” chief ray forced through h=0 at stop surface; aspheric surface terms do not affect first-order angle; stop modelled as thin plane; infinite-conjugate objects approximated by large finite distance; magnification variation uses thin-lens paraxial formula (nu-form). Telecentric threshold: |angle| < 0.5В° (conventional machine-vision). Ref: Welford "Aberrations of Optical Systems" (1986) В§3, В§4.4; Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" В§5.4; Hecht "Optics" В§6.6. `kerf-cad-core/optics/telecentricity_check.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Depth-of-field + hyperfocal distance** (OPTICS-FOCAL-DISTANCE-DEPTH): `LensFocusSpec(focal_length_mm, f_number, focus_distance_mm, circle_of_confusion_mm=0.03)` вҶ’ `DepthOfFieldReport(hyperfocal_distance_mm, near_limit_mm, far_limit_mm, depth_of_field_mm, behind_focus_fraction, infinity_focus_at_hyperfocal, honest_caveat)`; standard photographic thin-lens DoF formulae (Greenleaf "Photographic Optics" В§3 / Hecht "Optics" В§6.4): H = fВІ/(NВ·c) + f; D_near = DВ·(HвҲ’f)/(H+DвҲ’2f); D_far = DВ·(HвҲ’f)/(HвҲ’D) [вҲһ when D вүҘ H]; oracle 50mm f/2.8 @ 5 m c=0.03 mm вҶ’ H вүҲ 29811.9 mm (вүҲ29.81 m); near вүҲ 4286 mm; far вүҲ 5993 mm; DoF вүҲ 1707 mm вҖ” all verified to < 0.01%; at focus=H: D_near = H/2 exactly, D_far = вҲһ verified; D вүҘ H вҶ’ DoF infinite; larger f/# вҶ’ wider DoF; LLM tool `optics_compute_depth_of_field`; 25 hermetic tests. Default CoC 0.03 mm = 35mm full-frame standard (Greenleaf В§3 / 1/1400 diagonal). HONEST: geometric thin-lens model only вҖ” does NOT add diffraction-limited Airy-disk blur to geometric CoC; at small apertures (f/# вүі f/16 for visible light) Airy disk 1.22В·О»В·N approaches 0.03 mm CoC, so geometric DoF is slightly optimistic; for combined blur circle use c_eff = sqrt(c_geomВІ + c_airyВІ). Ref: Hecht (2017) В§6.4; Greenleaf (1950) В§3; Kingslake (1978) В§4.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Working f-number (finite-conjugate)** (OPTICS-FNO-WORKING): `FnoWorkingSpec(nominal_f_number, magnification)` вҶ’ `FnoWorkingReport(nominal_f_number, working_f_number, exposure_loss_stops, image_irradiance_factor, honest_caveat)`; thin-lens working f-number formula N_w = NВ·(1+|m|) (Hecht "Optics" В§6.4 / Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" В§4.5); magnification convention m = вҲ’s_i/s_o (negative for real inverted images); oracle f/4 at 1:1 macro (m=вҲ’1) вҶ’ N_w=8.0, loss=2.0 stops exactly; f/2.8 at 1:2 (m=вҲ’0.5) вҶ’ N_w=4.2, lossвүҲ1.17 stops; image irradiance factor = (N/N_w)ВІ = 1/(1+|m|)ВІ; exposure_loss_stops = 2В·logвӮӮ(1+|m|); m=0 (infinity focus) вҶ’ N_w=N, loss=0, factor=1.0 (no penalty); absolute value of m used so positive (virtual-image) magnifications are handled; LLM tool `optics_compute_working_fno`; 28 hermetic tests. HONEST: thin-lens (symmetric-pupil) approximation ONLY вҖ” real asymmetric lenses (retrofocus, telephoto, macro with floating elements) have pupil magnification p = D_exit/D_entrance вү  1; exact formula N_w = (1/p)В·NВ·(1+|m|/p) (Smith MOE В§4.5) can differ by 0.5вҖ“1 stop for extreme retrofocus designs; pupil-position measurement requires an aperture-stop trace not in scope here. Ref: Hecht (2017) В§6.4; Smith (2008) В§4.5; Ray (2002) В§2. `kerf-cad-core/optics/fno_working.py`.

**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Iris (aperture stop) diameter map** (OPTICS-IRIS-DIAMETER-MAP): `IrisMapSpec(lens_system_dict, target_f_number, target_efl_mm=None)` вҶ’ `IrisDiameterReport(iris_diameter_mm, effective_f_number, efl_mm, surface_clearance_check, clipped, honest_caveat)`; paraxial formula D = EFL/f# (Welford "Aberrations" В§3.4 / Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" В§6); EFL computed via canonical marginal-ray trace (h=1, u=0) or supplied via `target_efl_mm`; marginal ray h=D/2 at stop (u=0) traced forward through surfaces after the stop and backward through a reversed sub-system for surfaces before the stop; per-surface clearance_ratio = CA_radius / |h| (>1 = clears; <1 = clips); clipping flag when h > 0.95 Г— CA_radius; oracle: EFL=50 mm, f/4 вҶ’ D=12.5 mm exactly; f/1.4 fast lens вҶ’ DвүҲ35.7 mm; stop_surface_index configurable; LLM tool `optics_compute_iris_diameter_map`; 25 hermetic tests. HONEST: paraxial (first-order) marginal-ray trace only вҖ” aspheric higher-order sag terms ignored; D=EFL/f# is infinity-conjugate formula only (finite-conjugate requires working f-number N_w=NВ·(1+|m|), Smith MOE В§4.5); clear apertures are caller-supplied; production design requires exact skew-ray analysis (Zemax OpticStudio / CODE V / Welford В§5). Ref: Welford (1986) В§3.4; Smith (2008) В§6; Hecht (2017) В§6.4. `kerf-cad-core/optics/iris_diameter_map.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Airy-disk diffraction-limited PSF** (OPTICS-DIFFRACTION-PSF): `DiffractionPSFSpec(wavelength_nm, aperture_diameter_mm, focal_length_mm)` вҶ’ `DiffractionPSFReport(airy_disk_radius_um, rayleigh_resolution_um, fwhm_um, psf_profile, honest_caveat)`; radial intensity I(r) = [2В·JвӮҒ(x)/x]ВІ where x = ПҖВ·DВ·r/(О»В·f) (Hecht "Optics" 5e В§10.2, eq. 10.22; Born & Wolf "Principles of Optics" 7e В§8.5.2, eq. 8.41); Airy disk radius r_Airy = 1.22В·О»В·F# (first zero of JвӮҒ, Born & Wolf В§8.5.2); Rayleigh resolution criterion О”r = r_Airy (Hecht В§10.2.7, eq. 10.28); FWHM вүҲ 1.03В·О»В·F# (Hecht eq. 10.59); uses scipy.special.j1 when available with pure-Python ascending-series fallback (Abramowitz & Stegun В§9.1.10); oracle О»=550nm, D=10mm, f=50mm (F#=5): r_Airy=3.355 Ојm, FWHM=2.833 Ојm, I(0)=1.0, I(r_Airy)вүҲ0 вҖ” all validated to <1e-6; LLM tool `optics_compute_diffraction_psf`; 32 hermetic tests. HONEST: SCALAR DIFFRACTION ONLY вҖ” no vector/polarisation effects (Richards-Wolf high-NA integral, Born & Wolf В§8.7); circular aperture only (non-circular/annular not modelled); aberration-free (Airy pattern = diffraction-limited ideal; Seidel/Zernike wavefront error вҶ’ Strehl < 1 not modelled); monochromatic (polychromatic PSF = вҲ«W(О»)В·I(r,О»)dО» not implemented); on-axis and paraxial (NA = D/(2f) вүӘ 1 assumed). Ref: Hecht (2017) В§10.2; Born & Wolf (1999) В§8.5; Goodman (2005) В§4.4. `kerf-cad-core/optics/diffraction_psf.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Singlet lens glass volume and weight** (OPTICS-LENS-VOLUME): `SingletLensSpec(radius_R1_mm, radius_R2_mm, center_thickness_mm, clear_aperture_radius_mm, glass_density_g_cm3=2.51)` вҶ’ `LensVolumeReport(volume_mm3, weight_g, edge_thickness_mm, sag1_mm, sag2_mm, lens_form, honest_caveat)`; sag h = |R| вҲ’ вҲҡ(|R|ВІ вҲ’ rВІ) (Smith "Modern Optical Engineering" В§13.3 eq. 13.6 / Mahajan "Optical Imaging and Aberrations" В§1.2); cap volume V_cap = ПҖВ·hВІВ·(3|R|вҲ’h)/3 (Smith В§13.3 eq. 13.7); lens volume V = ПҖВ·rВІВ·t_c Вұ V_cap1 Вұ V_cap2 with sign from Cartesian-sign surface convention (convex вҶ’ subtract, concave вҶ’ add); oracle: BK7 plano-convex R1=+100 mm, R2=вҲһ, ct=5 mm, CA_r=12.5 mm, ПҒ=2.51 g/cmВі вҶ’ sag1=0.7843 mm, V=2261.6 mmВі, weight=5.677 g (analytically verified); biconvex symmetric V = cylinder вҲ’ 2В·cap (both surfaces subtract); biconcave V = cylinder + 2В·cap (both surfaces add; edge > center thickness); meniscus R1=+100/R2=+200 classified correctly; lens_form вҲҲ {biconvex, biconcave, plano_convex, plano_concave, meniscus, plano_plano}; LLM tool `optics_compute_lens_volume`; 35 hermetic tests. HONEST: SPHERICAL SURFACES ONLY вҖ” aspheric sag h=RcВ·rВІ/(1+вҲҡ(1вҲ’(1+k)cВІrВІ))+ОЈ A_iВ·r^(2i) requires numerical integration (out of scope); no anti-reflection coating thickness (AR layers 100вҖ“500 nm, negligible mass); homogeneous density assumed (GRIN / melt-gradient glass differs вүӨ0.3%, Schott TIE-31 В§3); clear_aperture_radius вү  physical blank radius вҖ” blank is always larger, giving higher actual weight. Ref: Smith (2008) В§13.3; Mahajan (2011) В§1.2; Schott TIE-31 (2023). `kerf-cad-core/optics/lens_volume.py`.
**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Paraxial chief-ray height trace** (OPTICS-CHIEF-RAY-HEIGHT): `trace_chief_ray(lens_system_dict, field_angle_deg, stop_surface_idx)` вҶ’ `ChiefRayHeightReport(per_surface_heights, image_height_mm, magnification, stop_surface_idx, chief_ray_at_stop_mm, object_angle_deg, image_angle_deg, honest_caveat)`; paraxial chief-ray (principal ray from off-axis object through stop centre) traced via nu-form superposition (Welford "Aberrations" В§3 / Mahajan "Optical Imaging" В§2): two auxiliary rays (Ray A: object height H, slope 0; Ray B: height obj_dist, slope 1) solve h_stop=0 вҶ’ u_obj=вҲ’h_A_stop/h_B_stop; oracle: f=50mm plano-convex thin lens, Оё=5В° вҶ’ image_height=fВ·tan(5В°)=4.374mm (verified to <1e-3mm); chief-ray height at stop = 0 exactly; image-space telecentric condition (stop at front focal plane вҶ’ u_img=0) verified; per-surface {surface_idx, ray_height_mm, ray_angle_deg}; LLM tool `optics_trace_chief_ray`; 30 hermetic tests. HONEST: PARAXIAL ONLY вҖ” first-order heights differ from exact at large field/fast optics; APERTURE STOP POSITION MUST BE SUPPLIED (no auto-detect); rotationally symmetric systems only; image height = fВ·tan(Оё) (no distortion correction). Ref: Welford (1986) В§3, В§3.7; Mahajan (2011) В§2; Smith (2008) В§5. `kerf-cad-core/optics/chief_ray_height.py`.

**Optics / acoustics** вң… вҖ” **Schmidt corrector plate aspheric profile** (OPTICS-SCHMIDT-CORRECTOR-PLATE): `SchmidtSpec(primary_radius_R_mm, aperture_diameter_D_mm, glass_index_n=1.5168, neutral_zone_factor_kappa=1.5)` вҶ’ `SchmidtReport(aspheric_profile, max_sag_mm, neutral_zone_radius_mm, schwarzschild_constant_k, honest_caveat)`; classical Schmidt (1932) corrector sag z(r) = rВІВ·(rВІвҲ’2В·ПҒ_nВІ)/[8В·(nвҲ’1)В·RВі] where ПҒ_n = (D/2)/вҲҡОә is the neutral zone radius (Born & Wolf В§6.3); kappa=1.5 places neutral zone at rвүҲ0.8165В·D/2 (classic Schmidt optimum that minimises peak-to-valley sag); max_sag = |z(ПҒ_n)| = ПҒ_nвҒҙ/[8В·(nвҲ’1)В·RВі]; neutral-zone slope check (dz/dr=0 at r=ПҒ_n); Schwarzschild constant k=вҲ’1 (paraboloid equivalent); oracle: 200mm f/2 BK7 corrector вҶ’ neutral zone 81.65mm, max_sagвүҲ0.168mm; sag scales as (nвҲ’1)вҒ»В№ verified; LLM tool `optics_design_schmidt_corrector`; 28 hermetic tests. HONEST: classical Schmidt (1932) ONLY вҖ” modern SchmidtвҖ“Cassegrain and SchmidtвҖ“Newtonian designs add a secondary mirror, field-flattener, and refined aspherics for a flat corrected field; these are NOT modelled; monochromatic (chromatic residual is second-order, Wilkins 1950, not computed); on-axis only (off-axis coma requires corrector at exact centre-of-curvature position); field curvature R_PetzvalвүҲвҲ’R/2 not corrected; thin-plate approximation. Ref: Schmidt (1932) Zentralzeitung fГјr Optik und Mechanik 52, 25-26; Born & Wolf (1999) В§6.3; Rutten & van Venrooij "Telescope Optics" (1988) В§6.3. `kerf-cad-core/optics/schmidt_corrector.py`.

**Implicit geometry** вң… вҖ” F-rep CSG (union/intersect/subtract/blend/shell) + domain warps (twist/taper/wave) in `kerf_cad_core.frep.csg`.

**Materials + LCA** вң… вҖ” Ashby database to ~200 materials (14 families) with Pareto-frontier multi-objective selection; full ISO 14040/44 LCA (4 phases, 6 impact categories, Monte-Carlo uncertainty). **Embodied-carbon DB (ICE v3 lookups)** вң… вҖ” `kerf_lca.database` module with 30-material `MATERIAL_DATABASE` (steel, aluminium, copper, composites, concrete, timber, plastics, elastomers, glass, ceramics); `lca_lookup_material` + `lca_compute_embodied_carbon` LLM tools; EN 15978 Module D EoL credits. Data: ICE v3.0, Hammond & Jones, University of Bath, 2019 вҖ” NOT Ecoinvent (license-restricted).
**Materials + LCA** вң… вҖ” Ashby database to ~200 materials (14 families) with Pareto-frontier multi-objective selection; full ISO 14040/44 LCA (4 phases, 6 impact categories, Monte-Carlo uncertainty); EoL circularity (EN 15978 Module D + Ellen MacArthur MCI) вң….

**Compare matrices** вң… вҖ” feature-matrix YAML for 14 reference CADs: Fusion 360, SolidWorks, Onshape, FreeCAD, Rhino, KiCad, CATIA, Creo, NX, Inventor, AutoCAD, Altium, Revit, Blender вҖ” 741 grounded rows total.

**Security hardening** вң… вҖ” `/run-topo` auth gate; NFP `grid_step` clamped; PVT `n_mc` clamped; Yosys module-name injection blocked; shared `_guard_*` helpers extracted across 68 files (вҲ’2009/+129 lines net).

**SUBD-LIMIT-WALK-CROSS-CURVE** вң… вҖ” walk a parametric path on the Catmull-Clark subdivision-surface limit and intersect with a planar cut to produce a cross-section curve: `walk_subd_limit_cross_plane(cage_mesh, plane_point, plane_normal, num_walk_samples=400)` returns `CrossCurveResult(points, face_indices_crossed, num_intersections, honest_caveat)`; samples a uniform (u,v) grid on each cage face using the Stam (1998) closed-form limit-position evaluator (`stam_limit_position` вҖ” bi-cubic B-spline for regular valence-4 patches, eigenstructure for extraordinary vertices); sign changes in signed plane distance are detected between adjacent grid samples (u-adjacent + v-adjacent separately); each crossing refined by 5 bisection iterations (positional error вүҲ cell_size/32 вүҲ face_size/32); honest caveats: discrete sample walk (coarse grid can miss sub-cell features), 5-iter bisection (not sub-pixel), boundary edge duplicates possible, extraordinary vertices use Stam eigenstructure approximation; LLM tool `subd_walk_limit_cross_plane`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 20 oracle-asserted tests (cube XY/XZ/diagonal cuts, parallel planes вҶ’ empty, flat patch, grid cage, extraordinary vertex cage, degenerate cage, non-unit normal, sample-count monotonicity) вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/limit_walk_cross_curve.py`. Refs: Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH В§3вҖ“4; Schaefer-Warren (2004).

**SUBD-LIMIT-WALK-ALONG-EDGES** вң… вҖ” sample the Catmull-Clark limit-surface curve corresponding to a chain of cage edges: `walk_along_cage_edges(cage, vertex_sequence, samples_per_edge=8)` returns `SubDEdgeWalk(points, arc_length)`; boundary edges вҶ’ limit = cage (crease rule); creased interior edges вҶ’ limit on sharp crease curve; smooth interior edges вҶ’ smooth arc through CC limit positions; intermediate points via index-tracked CC subdivision (k = ceil(log2(spe)) levels, max 6) + per-vertex limit stencil; honest ValueError for non-adjacent vertices or out-of-range indices; LLM tool `subd_walk_edge_chain`; 14 oracle-asserted tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_edge_walk.py`.

**SUBD-CAGE-RING-FROM-EDGE** вң… вҖ” edge ring traversal on Catmull-Clark quad cages: `compute_edge_ring(cage, start_edge)` returns `EdgeRingResult(edge_indices, is_closed, is_degenerate, transition_face_indices)`; follows opposite edges across each quad face (Maya/Blender Bridge pattern); closed on cube (4-ring) and torus (ring length = opposite-axis count); open at mesh boundary; honest degenerate flag at non-quad faces; start_edge accepts `(v0, v1)` pair or integer edge index; LLM tool `subd_compute_edge_ring`; 25 oracle-asserted tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_edge_ring.py`.

**SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-LOOP-SELECT** вң… вҖ” directional edge-loop walk on a quad cage mesh: `select_edge_loop(cage_mesh, start_edge_idx, max_steps=1000)` returns `EdgeLoopResult(edge_indices, vertex_indices, closed, terminated_at_irregular, irregular_vertex_valences, honest_caveat)`; walks the opposite-edge chain (Bommes-LГ©vy-Pietroni 2013 В§3.2 'skip-2' rule): at each step crosses the current quad face to its opposite edge; terminates at irregular vertex (valenceвү 4), boundary edge, non-quad face, or loop closure; oracles: 4Г—4 torus (all valence-4) вҶ’ closed loops length 4; 6Г—8 torus вҶ’ lengths {6, 8}; cube (all valence-3) вҶ’ terminates at first irregular vertex, valence=3 reported; cylinder axial-interior edge вҶ’ closed ring length nu; mixed tri/quad вҶ’ terminates; ValueError on out-of-range start_edge_idx; honest caveats: quads only, no tris; assumes manifold mesh; boundary vertices treated as irregular; traversal direction fixed by first adjacent face winding; LLM tool `subd_select_edge_loop`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 25 oracle-asserted tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_loop_select.py`. Refs: Bommes-LГ©vy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F В§3.2; LГ©vy-Liu (2010) SIGGRAPH В§4.

**SUBD-CAGE-FACE-LOOP** вң… вҖ” walk a face loop on a quad cage mesh by hopping through opposite-edge adjacent quads: `select_face_loop(cage_mesh, start_face_idx, walk_direction=0, max_steps=1000)` returns `FaceLoopResult(face_indices, closed, terminated_at_irregular, irregular_face_indices, honest_caveat)`; dual of the edge-loop walk вҖ” tracks faces rather than edges, useful for ring-cut planning and subdivision sweep selection; `walk_direction` 0/1 selects which opposite-edge pair to traverse: dir=0 crosses (v0,v1)вҶ”(v2,v3) edges, dir=1 crosses (v1,v2)вҶ”(v3,v0) edges; on a regular torus the two directions produce orthogonal face rings; terminates at non-quad face, boundary edge, or loop closure; oracles: 4Г—4 torus dir=0 вҶ’ closed ring length 4; 4Г—6 torus dir=0вҶ’length 4, dir=1вҶ’length 6; cylinder (nu=12) dir=1 вҶ’ circumferential closed ring length 12; cube вҶ’ closed 4-ring; mixed tri/quad вҶ’ terminated; single-quad cage вҶ’ terminated; non-quad start face вҶ’ immediate termination; ValueError on out-of-range start_face_idx or walk_direction not in {0,1}; honest caveats: quads only вҖ” non-quad face terminates immediately; boundary edges terminate walk; walk_direction relative to start face winding; one-directional (no back-propagation); manifold mesh assumed; LLM tool `subd_select_face_loop`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 20 oracle-asserted tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/face_loop_select.py`. Refs: Bommes-LГ©vy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F В§3.2; Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes В§3.2.

**SUBD-CAGE-SUBDIVIDE-EDGE** вң… вҖ” localized single-edge refinement on a SubD control cage (not a full Catmull-Clark pass): `subdivide_edge(cage, edge_index, position_t=0.5, split_strategy='quad') -> SubdivideEdgeResult`; inserts midpoint vertex v_m = lerp(v_a, v_b, t) on the target edge; each of the 1вҖ“2 adjacent faces split into face_a [p0, v_m, p_{n-1}] (triangle) + face_b [v_m, p1, ..., p_{n-1}] (quad for n=4); cube oracle: V=8вҶ’9, F=6вҶ’8, E=12вҶ’15, Euler 9вҲ’15+8=2 вң“; boundary-edge split: 1 adjacent face only; invalid edge_index вҶ’ ValueError; position_t clamp [1e-9, 1вҲ’1e-9]; honest flag `has_non_quad_input` for non-quad input faces; sharpness/bevel-weight not preserved across edge-index remapping; LLM tool `subd_subdivide_edge`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 24 oracle-asserted tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_subdivide_edge.py`. Ref: Catmull & Clark 1978; Stam 1998 В§4 local refinement; Maya polySplit API.

**SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-COLLAPSE** вң… вҖ” collapse a SubD cage edge (merge two endpoints into one vertex) while maintaining mesh validity; used for mesh decimation and cage simplification: `collapse_edge(cage: SubdCage, v_keep, v_remove, midpoint=True) -> EdgeCollapseResult`; `EdgeCollapseResult(new_cage: SubdCage, num_vertices_removed, num_faces_removed, collapsed_position_xyz_mm, degenerate_faces_removed, became_invalid, honest_caveat)`; midpoint=True (default): v_new = (V[v_keep] + V[v_remove]) / 2; midpoint=False: v_new = V[v_keep]; all face refs to v_remove rewritten to v_keep; degenerate faces (containing both endpoints вҶ’ repeated vertex) removed; vertex list compacted; adjacency check вҖ” if v_keep and v_remove do not share a face (not a valid edge), became_invalid=True and input cage returned unchanged; cube oracle: collapse top-front edge (v_keep=4, v_remove=5) вҶ’ 7 verts, 2 degenerate faces removed вң“; pyramid base edge: 5вҶ’4 verts, вүҘ1 degenerate face вң“; non-adjacent pair вҶ’ became_invalid=True, cage unchanged вң“; midpoint position oracle вң“; endpoint position (midpoint=False) oracle вң“; all face indices valid post-collapse вң“; v_keep/v_remove out-of-range вҶ’ ValueError вң“; honest caveats: TOPOLOGY ONLY вҖ” no QEM cost function (Garland-Heckbert 1997); caller chooses which edge to collapse; midpoint placement can deviate from CC limit surface; crease annotations not preserved; all indices invalidated; non-manifold edges handled conservatively; LLM tool `subd_collapse_edge`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in `plugin.py _TOOL_MODULES`; 14 oracle-asserted tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_collapse.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1993) Mesh Optimization; Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes В§3.2; Garland-Heckbert (1997) QEM В§3; Bommes-LГ©vy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F В§4.

**SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-FLIP** вң… вҖ” topological edge flip for two adjacent triangles sharing an edge: `flip_edge(cage_mesh, edge_idx) -> EdgeFlipResult`; finds the two triangles T1=(v_a, v_b, v_c) and T2=(v_a, v_b, v_d) sharing edge (v_a, v_b); replaces them with T1'=(v_a, v_c, v_d) and T2'=(v_b, v_d, v_c) connecting the opposite vertices; winding order of T1 is preserved in both output triangles; vertex list unchanged (no vertices added or removed); face count unchanged (2 in вҶ’ 2 out); canonical oracle: triangles ABC+BCD (share BC) вҶ’ flip gives {A,B,D}+{A,C,D} (share AD); new shared edge is AD, old shared edge BC no longer present вң“; double flip restores original topology (flip is its own inverse) вң“; only non-incident faces unchanged вң“; out-of-range edge_idx вҶ’ ValueError; boundary edge (1 incident face) вҶ’ ValueError; non-manifold edge (> 2 incident faces) вҶ’ ValueError; quad or n-gon face вҶ’ ValueError; honest caveats: TOPOLOGICAL FLIP ONLY вҖ” no Delaunay in-circle test; callers must test in-circle criterion themselves if Delaunay quality is required; triangles only (quad faces raise ValueError); no crease/UV/colour attribute preservation on flipped edge; vertex positions unchanged; LLM tool `subd_flip_edge`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 14 oracle-asserted tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_flip.py`. Refs: Bommes-LГ©vy-Pietroni (2013) CG&F В§3; Edelsbrunner (2001) Geometry and Topology for Mesh Generation В§2; de Berg et al. (2008) Computational Geometry В§9.3.

**SUBD-CAGE-AREA** вң… вҖ” compute total surface area of a subdivision control cage (control polygon) and estimate the asymptotic Catmull-Clark limit-surface area: `compute_cage_area(cage) -> CageAreaReport`; `SubdCage(vertices_xyz_mm, faces)` accepts tris, quads, and n-gons; triangle area = 0.5В·|cross(v1-v0, v2-v0)|; quad area = 0.5В·|cross(d1, d2)| (diagonal cross-product, exact for planar quads); n-gon area = centroid fan triangulation (exact for planar n-gons); limit-surface estimate = cage_area Г— 0.94 (empirical Catmull-Clark shrinkage ratio); `CageAreaReport` fields: `total_cage_area_mm2`, `estimated_limit_surface_area_mm2`, `per_face_areas`, `min_face_area_mm2`, `max_face_area_mm2`, `degenerate_face_indices`, `num_quads`, `num_tris`, `num_ngons`, `honest_caveat`; unit cube oracle: 6 mmВІ cage, 5.64 mmВІ estimate вң“; degenerate triangle (collinear) flagged вң“; pyramid (1 quad + 4 tris) area oracle вң“; pentagon n-gon area = exact formula within 1e-9 вң“; hexagon n-gon вң“; area scales by kВІ on vertex rescaling вң“; limit estimate = cage Г— 0.94 exactly вң“; LLM tool `subd_compute_cage_area`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 23 oracle-asserted tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/cage_area.py`. HONEST: LIMIT-SURFACE AREA IS AN EMPIRICAL ESTIMATE ONLY вҖ” exact value requires Stam (1998) eigenanalysis at each extraordinary vertex or GL integration over Stam B-spline patches; empirical 0.92вҖ“0.95 range applies to typical organic closed all-quad cages; error vs exact limit area can exceed 5% for cages with many extraordinary vertices or high non-planarity; non-planar quad/n-gon face areas are first-order approximations only. Refs: Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD 10(6); Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH В§2; Warren-Weimer (2001) В§5; Zorin-SchrГ¶der (2000) SIGGRAPH Course В§3.

**SUBD-CAGE-VERTEX-MERGE** вң… вҖ” merge a list of N cage vertices (by index) into their centroid, updating all adjacent face indices and removing degenerate faces: `merge_vertices(cage_mesh, vertex_indices) -> VertexMergeResult`; computes v_c = mean of all named vertex positions; replaces every face reference to any named vertex with v_c; faces containing вүҘ 2 named vertices become degenerate (repeated vertex) and are removed; vertex list compacted (net -(|S|-1) vertices); special cases: empty or single-vertex list вҶ’ no-op; duplicate indices вҶ’ deduplicated; non-adjacent vertices (no shared edge) вҶ’ no faces removed, vertex count drops by |S|-1; cube oracle: merge all 4 corners of isolated quad вҶ’ 3 verts removed, 1 face removed, 0 faces survive; 2-vertex merge on plane вҶ’ equivalent to edge_collapse (same vertex count, same faces removed, centroid=midpoint); 3-vertex centroid oracle вң“; all face indices valid post-merge вң“; out-of-range index вҶ’ ValueError; honest caveats: centroid placement only вҖ” NO quadric error metric (Garland-Heckbert 1997 В§3); CC limit surface shape changes; crease annotations on incident edges not preserved; vertex/face indices invalidated after merge; LLM tool `subd_merge_vertices`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 20 oracle-asserted tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/vertex_merge.py`. Refs: Hoppe (1996) Progressive Meshes В§3.2; Garland-Heckbert (1997) QEM В§3.

**SUBD-LIMIT-CRITICAL-POINTS** вң… вҖ” discrete Morse critical points (вҲҮf = 0) on Catmull-Clark SubD limit surfaces: `find_critical_points(cage, scalar_field, sample_density=4) -> CriticalPointsReport`; classifies interior vertices using lower/upper link under Simulation-of-Simplicity total order (Edelsbrunner-MГјcke 1990) вҖ” minima (LkвҒ» empty), maxima (LkвҒә empty), saddles (#components(LkвҒ») + #components(LkвҒә) > 2); Morse-Euler verification #max вҲ’ #sad + #min = ПҮ(VвҲ’E+F); scalar fields: height_z/height_x/height_y/radius; oracle depth bar: sphere from cube cage вҶ’ 1 max + 1 min + 0 sad (ПҮ=2, Euler passes); torus (axis along Y, Morse generic) вҶ’ 1 max + 1 min + 2 sad (ПҮ=0); flat/tilted-plane open mesh вҶ’ 0 critical points; honest caveat: Bott-Samelson degenerate fields (axis-symmetric height on upright torus) not handled вҖ” euler_check flags violations; LLM tool `subd_find_critical_points`; 16 oracle-asserted tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_critical_points.py` (Edelsbrunner-Harer 2010 В§1).

**BREP-SHELL-WALL-CHECK** вң… вҖ” post-shell wall-thickness verification against manufacturing process requirements: `check_shell_walls(body, process, material) -> ShellWallReport`; injection moulding spec from Menges 2001 В§3.3 Table 3.3 (t_min/t_max per material, flow-length correction +0.5 mm/100 mm); sheet metal from Boothroyd-Dewhurst В§5 (constant-wall + В§5.4 bend-radius multiplier); FDM/SLA/SLS/DLP/MJF nozzle-diameter minimum wall; per-face `FaceWallResult` with violation text; `violations_thin`/`violations_thick` lists; honest caveat: static rule-based only, no CFD or mould-fill simulation; LLM tool `brep_check_shell_walls`; 20 oracle-asserted tests (2mm ABS вҶ’ pass; 0.5mm ABS вҶ’ thin; 0.5mm FDM вҶ’ pass; 0.2mm FDM вҶ’ thin; 6mm ABS вҶ’ thick; Menges Table 3.3 oracle for PP/PC/LCP/PVC/POM/PEEK; flow-length correction; sheet-metal Al; SLA; nozzle override) вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/shell_wall_check.py`.

### Core platform

- **Auth + projects + files + chat (CRUD)** вң… вҖ” Postgres, JWT, Google OAuth.
- **Plugin monorepo (`packages/kerf-*`)** вң… вҖ” `kerf-core` app factory + entry-point loader; ~25 plugin packages; 864+ tests.
- **Single-binary build + brew/curl install** вң… вҖ” embedded Vite SPA (~32 MB).
- **Auth-optional local mode** вң… вҖ” `POST /auth/bootstrap-local` singleton user.
- **Cloud: workshop sharing, billing, LLM pricing, free/paid buckets + wallet** вң… вҖ” USD-display, credits at cost, BYO-key plumbing.
- **Cloud: git (commits/branches/merge/GitHub sync) + git Storer** вң….
- **Large-file git handling** вң… вҖ” pointer kind, Phase 1.
- **Diff-based + compressed revisions** вң… вҖ” 82Г— shrink.
- **Workspaces (orgs), activity timeline, avatars/CDN, collapsible chat** вң….
- **E2E Playwright + per-plugin pytest suites** вң….
- **Billing-ledger schema on fresh databases** вң….

### Scripting / SDK

- **`.script.py` via `kerf-sdk`** вң… вҖ” `/v1/rpc` JSON-RPC over the LLM tool registry; API tokens; PyPI publish.
- **SDKs: Python В· TypeScript В· Rust В· Go В· Lua** вң… вҖ” same `/v1/rpc` wire format.

### Parametric core

- **Equations / global parameters** вң… вҖ” `.equations`, mathjs.
- **Configurations / variants** вң… вҖ” per-file param overrides, BOM rollup.
- **Materials database** вң… вҖ” `.material` kind, 200 seeded materials.
- **Two coexisting kernels** вң… вҖ” `.jscad` (mesh) + `.feature` (OCCT BRep), shared `.sketch`/`.assembly`/`.drawing`.
- **Pure-Python B-rep + NURBS kernel** вң… вҖ” validated `Body` topology, tolerant booleans, G1/G2 fillets, closest-point, hardened SSI, parametric history DAG with persistent face naming. 620 hermetic analytic-oracle-asserted tests.

### Geometry kernel вҖ” depth

The pure-Python kernel (`packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/geom/`) now matches Rhino/Blender-class construction depth with an analytic foundation:

| Module | Description | Status |
|---|---|---|
| **`brep.py`** | B-rep topology: radial-edge `BodyвҶ’SolidвҶ’ShellвҶ’FaceвҶ’LoopвҶ’CoedgeвҶ’EdgeвҶ’Vertex`, nine Euler operators, EulerвҖ“PoincarГ© invariant enforced | вң… shipped |
| **`geom/topology_euler_check.py`** | **BREP-TOPOLOGY-EULER-CHECK**: full generalised Euler-PoincarГ© verifier V-E+F = 2(S-G)+H (Mantyla 1988 В§6; Hoffmann 1989 В§5); `verify_euler_topology(Body)` + `verify_euler_topology_from_dict(faces, ...)` + `EulerCheckReport` dataclass; union-find shell count; oracle helpers for cube/torus/disjoint cubes; LLM tool `brep_verify_euler_topology`; 16 hermetic tests (cube ПҮ=2, torus ПҮ=0, disjoint cubes S=2/ПҮ=4, inner loops, violation flags). Pure-Python. CAVEATS: genus/inner-loops require caller hints in dict mode; vertex dedup after sew/heal may cause spurious failure (degenerate_vertices_hint flag). | вң… shipped |
| **`brep_build.py`** | Analytic verbs (box/cylinder/sphere/Coons patch) вҶ’ `validate_body`-clean `Body` | вң… shipped |
| **`geom/brep_connect_inspector.py`** | **BREP-CONNECT-INSPECTOR**: radial-edge connectivity classification (Weiler 1985 В§3 + Mantyla 1988 В§6); counts dangling / boundary / manifold / non-manifold edges; isolated vertices; degenerate (zero-length) edges; union-find shell connectivity components; EulerвҖ“PoincarГ© V-E+F residual; `inspect_connectivity` + `is_manifold_closed`; LLM tools `brep_inspect_connectivity` + `brep_is_manifold`; 11 hermetic oracle tests (closed cube вҶ’ manifold=12/boundary=0/components=1; open box вҶ’ boundary=4/manifold=8; T-shape вҶ’ nonmanifoldвүҘ1; two disconnected cubes вҶ’ components=2). Pure-Python, no OCCT. | вң… shipped |
| **`geom/brep_connect_inspector.py`** | **BREP-CONNECT-INSPECTOR**: radial-edge connectivity classification (Weiler 1985 В§3 + Mantyla 1988 В§6); manifold/boundary/nonmanifold/dangling counts; isolated vertices; degenerate edges; union-find shell components; EulerвҖ“PoincarГ© V-E+F; `inspect_connectivity` + `is_manifold_closed`; LLM tools `brep_inspect_connectivity` + `brep_is_manifold` | вң… shipped |
| **`geom/vertex_degree_check.py`** | **BREP-VERTEX-DEGREE-CHECK**: count incident edges per vertex; flag boundary (degree < expected_degree) and non-manifold (degree > expected_degree + 2); `VertexDegreeReport` dataclass with `num_vertices`, `degree_histogram` (dict[int,int]), `num_boundary_vertices`, `num_non_manifold_vertices`, `max_degree`, `irregular_vertex_indices`, `honest_caveat`; `check_vertex_degrees(brep_or_mesh, expected_degree=4)`; oracle helpers for cube + tetrahedron; LLM tool `brep_check_vertex_degrees`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 20 hermetic tests. Pure-Python. CAVEATS: edge-based degree only вҖ” does NOT analyse face-fan angular order or non-manifold edges at high-degree vertices. Refs: Mantyla 1988 В§3.4; Hoffmann 1989 В§4. | вң… shipped |
| **`geom/brep_edge_metrics.py`** | **BREP-SUM-EDGE-LENGTHS**: total edge length + kind/curve-type breakdowns for cutting-cost estimation; `total_edge_length` / `edge_length_by_kind` / `edges_by_curve_type` / `compute_edge_metrics`; linearвҶ’Euclidean, circularвҶ’radiusГ—angle, freeformвҶ’adaptive 5-pt Gauss-Legendre (Stoer-Bulirsch В§3 + Piegl-Tiller В§5.4); oracles: 100Г—50 rect=300, unit cube=12, sphere 12 great-circle r=50=3769.91; LLM tools `brep_total_edge_length` + `brep_edge_length_by_kind`; 20 hermetic tests | вң… shipped |
| **`boolean.py`** | Tolerant pure-Python solid booleans (regularised cut/fuse/common) over the primitive matrix, 2-manifold result | вң… shipped |
| **`fillet_solid.py` / `chamfer.py`** | G1/G2 surface blend + edge fillet + variable chamfer | вң… shipped |
| **`geom/auto_chamfer.py`** | Auto-chamfer recommendation (ISO 13715): dihedral-angle classification вҶ’ safety / manufacturing / cosmetic / no-chamfer; `brep_recommend_chamfers` + `brep_apply_chamfer_recommendations` LLM tools | вң… shipped |
| **`geom/auto_fillet.py`** | Auto-fillet recommendation engine (Peterson 1974 + Boothroyd-Dewhurst 2002) вҖ” classifies interior/exterior corners, sizes radii per design intent, estimates Kt reduction; LLM tools `brep_recommend_fillets` + `brep_apply_fillet_recommendations` | вң… shipped |
| **`geom/fillet_recommend_radius.py`** | BREP-FILLET-RECOMMEND-RADIUS вҖ” per-edge radius recommendation combining 4 criteria: (1) face-size cap rвүӨface_min/4 (Boothroyd-Dewhurst В§4), (2) Peterson 1974 В§2.3 notch Kt formula r=0.1Г—notch_depth (tension+bending, analytic only, NOT FEA), (3) material stress-relief floor rвүҘfactorГ—wall_thickness (steel 0.05, cast_iron 0.08, etc.), (4) tool constraint rвүҘtool_radius_mm + sharp-edge preservation; `RadiusRecommendation` dataclass with criteria_radii transparency dict; LLM tool `brep_recommend_fillet_radius`; 21 hermetic oracle tests | вң… shipped |
| **`fillet_recommend_radius.py`** | Per-edge fillet radius recommendation (Peterson 1974 В§2.3; Boothroyd-Dewhurst 2002 В§4) вҖ” LLM tool `brep_recommend_fillet_radius` | вң… shipped |
| **`chamfer_recommend_size.py`** | Per-edge chamfer size recommendation (Drozda-Wick В§3-7; DIN 74:1974 Form A/B; ISO 13715:2017 В§5) вҖ” deburring 0.5mmГ—45В°; countersink; cosmetic; manufacturing вҖ” LLM tool `brep_recommend_chamfer_size` | вң… shipped |

| **`geom/face_area_exact.py`** | **BREP-FACE-AREA-EXACT**: compute the exact area of a B-rep Face whose underlying surface is a NurbsSurface, using the first fundamental form A = вҲ«вҲ« sqrt(EGвҲ’FВІ) du dv (do Carmo В§2.5; Piegl & Tiller В§10.3; Farin В§11.2). Reuses `compute_exact_surface_area` (5Г—5 GL per knot-span cell) for the NurbsSurface fast path; generic path uses NГ—N GL per cell with adaptive subdivision (default: `gauss_order=8`, `adaptive_subdivisions=4`). `FaceAreaResult` dataclass: `area_mm2`, `num_quadrature_points`, `relative_error_estimate`, `honest_caveat`. Also handles analytic surfaces (Plane/Cylinder/Sphere/Torus) via finite-difference partials. LLM tool `brep_compute_face_area_exact` registered in `plugin.py`. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 34 hermetic tests green (NurbsSurface flat 10Г—10вҶ’100mmВІ within 1e-9; sphere R=1вҶ’4ПҖ within 0.01%; sphere R=2вҶ’16ПҖ within 0.01%; cylinder R=2 h=5вҶ’62.83 within 0.01%; torus R=2 r=0.5вҶ’39.48 within 0.1%; FaceAreaResult contract; trim-caveat; gauss_order consistency; re-export). HONEST: trimmed faces (faces with inner loops) use bounding-rectangle approximation вҖ” trim curves NOT honoured in v1; `honest_caveat` field explicitly reports this. Polynomial NURBS approximations of curved surfaces (cylinder, torus) under-report area by the chord error of the spline (~2вҖ“8%) compared to the exact analytic surface. | вң… shipped |
| **`geom/principal_curvature_viz.py`** | **BREP-FACE-PRINCIPAL-CURVATURE-VIZ**: sample ОәвӮҒ, ОәвӮӮ (principal curvatures) over a B-rep Face on a UГ—V grid + SVG/PNG false-colour heatmap. `PrincipalCurvatureSample` dataclass (u, v, kappa_1, kappa_2, gauss_K, mean_H, is_degenerate); `PrincipalCurvatureVizResult` (samples list, svg_heatmap str, png_bytes bytes\|None, honest_caveat str); `sample_principal_curvatures(face, nu=20, nv=20, export_svg=True, export_png=False)`. Algorithm: exact analytic derivatives via `surface_derivatives` (Piegl-Tiller Alg. A3.6) for NurbsSurface; finite-difference fallback for other surfaces with `evaluate(u,v)`. Shape-operator characteristic equation (do Carmo В§3.4): ОәвӮҒ = H + вҲҡ(HВІвҲ’K), ОәвӮӮ = H вҲ’ вҲҡ(HВІвҲ’K); K = (LNвҲ’MВІ)/(EGвҲ’FВІ); H = (ENвҲ’2FM+GL)/(2(EGвҲ’FВІ)). SVG heatmap: viridis false-colour of |ОәвӮҒ| per UV cell; PNG via pure-Python encoder (no Pillow). LLM tool `brep_face_principal_curvature_viz`. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 33 hermetic tests green (plane Оә=0 exact; exact rational sphere |Оә|=1/R Вұ5e-3; exact rational cylinder |ОәвӮӮ|=1/R Вұ1e-3; torus K sign-change; SVG/PNG validity; K=ОәвӮҒВ·ОәвӮӮ identity; H=(ОәвӮҒ+ОәвӮӮ)/2 identity; grid clamping). HONEST: uniform UV-parameter grid only вҖ” high-curvature pockets between grid points are missed (lower bound on max|Оә|); not adaptive; polar/degenerate points (|S_uГ—S_v|<1e-14) set is_degenerate=True with NaN curvatures; heatmap maps |ОәвӮҒ|, not signed ОәвӮҒ. Refs: do Carmo В§3.4; Mortenson В§6.5; Pottmann-Wallner В§4. | вң… shipped |
| **`geom/surface_curvature_map.py`** | **NURBS-SURFACE-CURVATURE-MAP**: sample a *scalar* curvature field (Gaussian K, mean H, \|ОәвӮҒ\|, or \|ОәвӮӮ\|) over a NurbsSurface UV grid and export a coloured SVG/PNG heatmap. Distinct from `principal_curvature_viz` (per-sample ОәвӮҒ/ОәвӮӮ objects); this module collapses to a single user-chosen scalar for zone-colour mould analysis, fairness QC, or topology inspection. `CurvatureMapSpec` dataclass: `nu_samples=30, nv_samples=30, scalar_to_map` ("gauss"\|"mean"\|"abs_max"\|"abs_min"), `colormap` ("viridis"\|"rdbu"\|"" auto), `export_png=False`. `CurvatureMapResult` dataclass: `curvature_grid list[list[float]]`, `min_value, max_value, mean_value`, `svg_heatmap str`, `png_bytes bytes\|None`, `honest_caveat str`. `sample_surface_curvature_map(surface, spec)`. Colourmaps: viridis (sequential, default for abs_max/abs_min); RdBu diverging centred on 0 (default for gauss/mean); caller-overridable. SVG/PNG via pure-Python encoder (no Pillow). LLM tool `nurbs_sample_surface_curvature_map` registered in `plugin.py`. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 35 hermetic tests green (sphere R=1 KвүҲ1; sphere HвүҲВұ1; cylinder K=0 within 1e-6; cylinder \|H\|=0.25; cylinder \|ОәвӮӮ\|=0.5; saddle K<0 on вүҘ70% samples; plane K=H=0 exact; SVG/PNG validity; RdBu auto for gauss/mean; viridis auto for abs_max; spec validation errors; grid clamping; statistics invariants; face .surface resolution). HONEST: scalar export only вҖ” not ОәвӮҒ/ОәвӮӮ vectors; uniform UV-parameter grid; degenerate poles return NaN; colourmap is 5-anchor LUT. Refs: do Carmo В§3.3; Mortenson В§6.5; Piegl-Tiller Alg. A3.6. | вң… shipped |

**GK-P23: In-process isotropic remesh fallback** вң… вҖ” `mesh_isotropic_remesh.py` вҖ” Botsch-Kobbelt (2004) iterative pipeline: (1) split edges > 4/3В·L, (2) collapse interior edges < 4/5В·L, (3) flip edges to equalise vertex valence toward 6, (4) tangential Laplacian smoothing. Dataclasses: `TriangleMesh` (vertices_xyz_mm, faces), `IsotropicRemeshSpec` (mesh, target_edge_length_mm, num_iterations=5, tangential_smoothing=True, preserve_boundary=True), `IsotropicRemeshReport` (output_mesh, edge_length_min/max/mean/stdev_mm, num_splits/collapses/flips/smooths_total, valence_variance, honest_caveat). `isotropic_remesh(spec)` function. LLM tool `mesh_isotropic_remesh` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core/__init__.py`. 24 hermetic tests green (dataclass structure; square plane 2-tri вҶ’ many uniform triangles; stdev decreases vs coarse input; boundary corners preserved; tetrahedron subdivided; empty/invalid/zero-iter edge cases; operation counters; valence variance; package re-export). HONEST CAVEATS: pure-Python + NumPy; slower than instant_meshes binary for > 50k triangles (O(N) per pass edge-map rebuild); output is triangle-only вҖ” quad remesh stays in `quad_remesh.py`; not as feature-complete as instantmeshes for anisotropic or feature-aligned remeshing.

**GK-P50: NURBS arc-length inversion** вң… вҖ” `invert_arc_length` (NewtonвҖ“Raphson + bisection fall-back; Piegl & Tiller В§11.2 + Sederberg CAGD В§6.4). Returns `ArcLengthInvertResult{t_param, residual_mm, iterations, honest_caveat}`. Used for chord-length parameterisation, even-spaced CAM toolpaths, rebar layout. Wired as `nurbs_invert_arc_length` LLM tool. 19 tests green. Caveat: highly non-uniform knot vectors may trigger bisection fall-back (still converges, just slower).

- **SUBD-CAGE-EDGE-FLIP** вң… вҖ” `flip_edge(cage_mesh, edge_idx)` returns `EdgeFlipResult(new_cage_faces, num_edges_flipped, flipped_edge_indices, honest_caveat)`; topological flip of shared edge (v_a,v_b) in two adjacent triangles вҶ’ T1'=(v_a,v_c,v_d) + T2'=(v_b,v_d,v_c); ABC+BCD flip вҶ’ {A,B,D}+{A,C,D} вң“; double flip restores original topology вң“; boundary edge вҶ’ ValueError; non-manifold edge вҶ’ ValueError; quad face вҶ’ ValueError; LLM tool `subd_flip_edge`; honest: topological only вҖ” NO Delaunay in-circle test; triangles only; 14 tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/edge_flip.py`. - **SUBD-CAGE-AREA** вң… вҖ” `compute_cage_area(cage)` returns `CageAreaReport(total_cage_area_mm2, estimated_limit_surface_area_mm2, per_face_areas, min_face_area_mm2, max_face_area_mm2, degenerate_face_indices, num_quads, num_tris, num_ngons, honest_caveat)`; unit cube вҶ’ 6 mmВІ cage, 5.64 mmВІ limit estimate вң“; degenerate triangle flagged вң“; pyramid 1 quad+4 tris area oracle вң“; pentagon n-gon exact вң“; hexagon n-gon вң“; area scales kВІ вң“; LLM tool `subd_compute_cage_area`; 23 tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/cage_area.py`. HONEST: limit-surface estimate is empirical Г—0.94 вҖ” NOT exact eigenanalysis; error can exceed 5% for extraordinary-vertex-heavy cages. Refs: Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD В§10(6); Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH В§2; Zorin-SchrГ¶der (2000) В§3.
- **SUBD-CAGE-DUAL-MESH** вң… вҖ” `compute_dual_mesh(cage_mesh)` returns `DualMeshResult(dual_vertices, dual_faces, num_irregular_dual_faces, honest_caveat)`; dual vertices = one face centroid per primal face; dual faces = CCW-ordered ring of neighboring face centroids per primal vertex (atan2 angular sort on tangent plane); cube oracle: 8 verts + 6 quads вҶ’ 6 dual verts + 8 triangular dual faces (combinatorial octahedron), 0 irregular; 4Г—4 torus (all valence-4) вҶ’ 16 dual verts + 16 quad dual faces, 0 irregular; 2Г—2 plane grid вҶ’ 4 dual verts + 9 dual faces, boundary vertices counted irregular; cylinder barrel (open) вҶ’ correct dual vertex/face count, boundary rings flagged irregular; all dual face indices valid; LLM tool `subd_compute_dual_mesh`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; 28 oracle-asserted tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/dual_mesh.py`. HONEST: closed manifold meshes only for complete dual faces вҖ” boundary primal edges produce INCOMPLETE (open) dual faces; angular sort (atan2) works on convex vertex stars but may mis-order concave or nearly co-planar stars; dual vertices are primal face centroids, NOT CC limit-surface points; non-manifold vertices produce topologically undefined dual faces. Refs: Bossen-Heckbert (1996) В§3.1; Bommes-LГ©vy-Pietroni (2013) В§3.2.
