- **3D PMI + GD&T annotation UI** вң… вҖ” ISO 1101 GD&T toolbar (DrawingToolbar + GdntToolbar) with all 14 characteristics; datum A/B/C placement; FCF click-to-place modal with tolerance value, diameter zone, material-condition modifier, datum refs; SVG FCF glyphs (FcfGlyph/DatumGlyph) rendered inline per standard; 3D PMI overlay (Pmi3DOverlay) projects FCF labels into the three.js viewport; annotations persist via addFcf/addDatumLabel in the drawing data model.
- **Auto-dim ISO 129-1:2018** вң… вҖ” chain / baseline / mixed dimensioning (В§5.1); extension-line gap + overshoot (В§5.4); 10 mm line spacing; leader lines at preferred 15В° angles (В§10); symmetric / unilateral / limit tolerance formats (В§8); compliance validator; 2 LLM tools (`drawing_auto_dimension_iso`, `drawing_validate_iso`).
- **Auto 6-view + iso projection (ISO 128-30 / Bertoline 5e)** вң… вҖ” `drawings/projections.py`: `generate_six_view_drawing` (front/back/top/bottom/left/right + iso); third-angle (ANSI/ASME Y14.3) and first-angle (ISO/DIN) layout; hidden-line removal per view via ray-cast depth test; `compute_projection_silhouette`; `drawing_auto_views` LLM tool; standard isometric 120В° axis property validated (ISO 5456-3).
- **Section view auto-cutaway + ISO 128-30 hatch** вң… вҖ” `cut_body_with_plane` + `hatch_cross_section` + `section_view_for_drawing`; marching-triangles half-body clipping; iron/concrete/plastic material hatch patterns; cutting-plane marker + Bertoline В§11 arrow indicators; LLM tool `brep_section_view`.
- **Measurement chain auto-extraction (ASME Y14.5 + ISO 129)** вң… вҖ” `extract_measurement_chain` generates a complete inspection dimension chain for a B-rep body: A/B/C datum-frame inference (В§3.4), per-feature DOF coverage (holes: diameter + depth + 2 position dims), redundancy detection (ISO 129-1 В§6 no-closed-chain rule), `generate_inspection_report` in ISO129 or ASME14.5 format; LLM tools `drawing_measurement_chain` + `drawing_inspection_report` wired.
- **2D drawings** вң… вҖ” multi-sheet, dimensions, GD&T frames, section hatching, leaders/balloons, centerlines. NURBS silhouette projection to plane (Hertzmann 2000) вң… вҖ” sign-change grid locus, NURBS curve fit, visible/hidden layer output.
- **NURBS surfacing (Phase 4)** вң… вҖ” sweep1/2/network/blend/loft + `surface_continuity` (C0вҖ“C2/G0вҖ“G2); surface-direct boolean; trim-by-curve; curvature-comb viz; zebra/reflection-line viewport toggle. G3 *enforcement* on the OCCT side is structurally impossible (absent from OCCT's type system); pure-Python is the G3 path.
- **NURBS surfacing (Phase 4a вҖ” jewelry priority)** вң… вҖ” `opSweep2` (two-rail sweep via `BRepFill_PipeShell`-style RMF midline, `sweep2_to_body` in `brep_build.py`), `opNetworkSrf` (Gordon/Coons-Gordon four-curve network, `network_srf_to_body`), `opBlendSrf` (G1/G2 Bezier blend strip, `blend_srf_to_body`); all three registered as LLM tools (`feature_sweep2`, `feature_network_srf`, `feature_blend_srf` in `surfacing.py`); 33 hermetic `validate_body`-clean tests in `test_phase4a_jewelry_surfacing.py`; scenario fixtures in `tests/fixtures/`.
- **Trim-loop auto-heal (T-junctions, dead loops, orientation)** вң… вҖ” UV-domain repair pass: T-junction vertex merge (Sederberg-Zheng-Bakenov-Nasri 2003), dead-loop removal, CCW/CW orientation fix (Eberly shoelace), self-intersection detection; `nurbs_trim_loop_heal` LLM tool; 11 analytic-oracle tests.
- **NURBS seam control for periodic surfaces** вң… вҖ” `detect_seam` / `shift_seam` / `align_seam_to_curve` in `geom/seam_control.py`; `nurbs_shift_seam` LLM tool registered; Piegl-Tiller В§5.2 cyclic CP-net rotation with uniform knot rebuild; 16 analytic-oracle tests green.
- **Far-offset numerical conditioning** вң… вҖ” `offset_far_correction.py` (Maekawa 1999 В§6; Hoschek-Lasser 1993 В§17): curvature-aware safety-distance computation (`safe_offset_distance`), adaptive local-refinement clamp (`offset_with_local_refinement`), graceful degradation with flagged unsafe parametric regions (`graceful_offset`); LLM tool `nurbs_surface_offset_robust` registered.
- **Variable-section extrude / morphing sweep** вң… вҖ” `extrude_variable_section` (profile morphs per path parameter; linear / cubic-Hermite / C2 interpolation; Wang 2008 RMF frames) + `extrude_with_scaling_curve` (1-D scale taper along path) + `extrude_morph_via_rail_pair` (rail-guided profile morph); `nurbs_extrude_variable` LLM tool registered; 17 analytic-oracle tests green (constant-section degenerate, circleвҶ’square morph, conical-surface oracle, C2 smoothness).
- **NURBS curve/surface split at parameter** вң… вҖ” `split_curve_at`, `split_curve_at_multiple`, `split_surface_at_u/v`; PieglвҖ“Tiller В§5.3 full-multiplicity knot insertion; rational-NURBS correct; LLM tools `nurbs_split_curve` + `nurbs_split_surface` registered (GK-P06).
- **Rhino parity** вң… вҖ” 3DM I/O, SubD (Catmull-Clark), quad remesh, mesh tools, layers/display, parametric `.graph`, render output.
- **Persistent face naming** вң… вҖ” sketch-anchored + topo-hash (frontend T1вҖ“T7) plus kernel-side `feature_id::role::fingerprint` selector in the pure-Python DAG.
- **Assembly interference detection (MГ¶ller 1997)** вң… вҖ” `detect_interference_pair` / `detect_interference_assembly` / `compute_assembly_aabb`; AABB broad-phase + MГ¶ller 1997 triangle-triangle narrow phase + GK-18 boolean intersection volume; severity classification (none/touch/overlap/major_overlap); LLM tools `brep_assembly_interference` + `brep_check_clearance` вҖ” `kerf_cad_core/geom/assembly_interference.py`.

### Simulation / manufacturing

- **FEM** вң… вҖ” FEniCSx + CalculiX: linear-static + modal + steady thermal + bonded contact; linear eigenvalue buckling + harmonic frequency response + random-vibration PSD; MITC4 plate/shell; acoustics FEM/BEM; high-frequency EM; electrostatics + magnetostatics; multi-axial fatigue; 2-D projection NS solver. Reference-value suite with Roark/Blevins/Incropera oracles (42 of 43 green).
- **CFD foundation** вң… вҖ” 2-D laminar: potential flow (`Cp(Оё)=1вҲ’4sinВІОё` oracle) + lid-driven cavity (Ghia Re=100 reference); 61 hermetic tests.
- **Topology optimization** вң… вҖ” SIMP via FEniCSx; NURBS surface fit; multi-body.
- **CAM** вң… вҖ” 2.5D + 3D parallel/waterline + lathe + 5-axis constant-tilt + 3+2 indexed; tool DB; LinuxCNC/GRBL/Fanuc posts.
- **CAM toolpath collision verifier** вң… вҖ” `cam_toolpath_collision.py`: segment-by-segment holder/spindle capsule-vs-AABB (Ericson 2005 В§5.5) + capsule-vs-triangle-mesh (MГ¶ller 1997 В§6) minimum-distance checks at 1 mm sampling resolution; configurable safety margin; fixture mesh support; `cam_verify_toolpath_collision` LLM tool. Known limit: worst-case missed gap вүӨ step_mm Г— вҲҡ2 вүҲ 1.41 mm at default 1 mm step.
- **CAM feedrate lookahead optimizer** вң… вҖ” `cam_feedrate_lookahead.py`: two-pass corner lookahead (Erkorkmaz-Altintas 2001 / Altintas 2012 В§5.7); V_corner = sqrt(a_max Г— r_blend / sin(Оё/2)); forward-pass acceleration + backward-pass deceleration; per-waypoint feedrate schedule + corner angles + cycle time. `cam_optimize_feedrate_lookahead` LLM tool. Supports two profile types: `"trapezoid"` (constant-accel, default, backward-compatible) and `"s-curve"` (jerk-limited, opt-in). S-curve scheduling вң… вҖ” `schedule_s_curve()` implements the full 7-segment constant-jerk profile (Lambrechts-Boerlage-Steinbuch 2005 IEEE TCST / Erkorkmaz-Altintas В§3.3): jerk-on accel вҶ’ constant accel вҶ’ jerk-off accel вҶ’ constant velocity вҶ’ jerk-on decel вҶ’ constant decel вҶ’ jerk-off decel; triangular fallback when distance too short; `SCurveProfile` dataclass; `profile_type="s-curve"` param on `optimize_feedrate` produces jerk-accurate cycle times (10вҖ“30% longer than trapezoidal at same A_max). 16 new hermetic tests.
- **5-axis CAM UI** вң… вҖ” `CAMView.jsx` mode switch (3-axis / 5-axis-indexed / 5-axis-continuous); tilt axis (A/B/C) + angle; strategy (swarf / contour-on-tilted-plane / indexed-rough); spindle vector preview; dispatches `cam_run` backend tool (`operation=5axis_finish` or `3plus2`).
- **Feed-rate optimizer** вң… вҖ” Altintas 2012 chip-load model + machine acceleration cap (В§3.6) + tool deflection (Euler-Bernoulli); per-material/tool Vc+fz database (9 materials Г— 5 tool classes); forwardвҖ“backward feed smoothing; MRR + cycle-time estimator. LLM tools: `manufacturing_optimize_feed`, `manufacturing_cycle_time`. (Altintas reference data вҖ” NOT cutting-tool-manufacturer-certified.)
- **MANUFACTURING-TOLERANCE-COST** вң… вҖ” Tolerance-cost estimation (Boothroyd-Dewhurst В§11.2 / Figure 11.4 exponential curve): `compute_tolerance_cost(tolerance_mm, process, base_cost_usd, dimension_mm)` вҶ’ `ToleranceCostResult`; multiplier = exp(k Г— log10(t_max/t)); processes: turning (k=1.80, Вұ0.012вҖ“0.5 mm), milling (k=1.60, Вұ0.025вҖ“0.5 mm), grinding (k=2.50, Вұ0.002вҖ“0.02 mm), lapping (k=3.20, Вұ0.0005вҖ“0.005 mm); auto-upgrade chain (turningвҶ’grindingвҶ’lapping) when tolerance tightens beyond process capability; ISO 286-1:2010 IT-grade mapping (`tolerance_to_IT_grade`) for IT1вҖ“IT16; `manufacturing_tolerance_cost` LLM tool registered; 46 hermetic tests covering 4 tolerance bands Г— 2 processes, process-upgrade chain, IT-grade monotonicity, oracle B-D Fig 11.4 ratios, near-limit advisories, and LLM tool error paths. Honest-flag: simplified exponential fit; real cost depends on shop equipment, batch size, material hardness, and feature geometry вҖ” treat as Вұ30% estimate. References: Boothroyd-Dewhurst В§11.2 + Fig 11.4 (2010); ASME B89.1.5-1998; ISO 286-1:2010 В§4.
- **MANUFACTURING-MATERIAL-COST-ROLLUP** вң… вҖ” Multi-cavity BOM material cost roll-up: `compute_material_cost_rollup(parts, material_db, waste_factor)` вҶ’ `MaterialCostReport`; mass = volume_mmВі Г— density Г— 1e-6 [kg]; gross_mass = net Г— (1 + waste_factor); cost = gross_mass Г— price_per_kg; aggregation by material type, finishing operation, and cavity supplier; 2025 H1 spot-price baseline DB (LME + Plastics News) for 17 materials (ABS/PP/PC/PA66/PEEK/PLA/Al6061/Al7075/Steel304/316/1018/4140/Cu/Ti6Al4V/GrayIron/CFRP/GFRP); honest advisory: prices fluctuate вҖ” treat as H1 2025 baseline only; unknown materials zero-costed + flagged; `manufacturing_compute_material_cost_rollup` LLM tool; 26 oracle-asserted tests including Boothroyd-Dewhurst В§8.3 depth-bar oracle (1000Г—ABS@100cmВі вҶ’ $286.00 USD) and Al6061 cross-check вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/costing/material_cost_rollup.py` + `material_prices_2025.py`. References: Boothroyd-Dewhurst В§8.3 (2010); ASME Y14.5-2018 В§1.3; Tappi T 220 SP-08 (advisory).
- **3-2-1 Auto-fixture layout** вң… вҖ” Asada-By (1985) В§5 form-closure rank analysis; 6-locator placement (P1-P3 primary, P4-P5 secondary, P6 tertiary) on AABB workpiece; constraint matrix rank-6 validation; clamp-force estimates (material Г— operation); ASME B5.18-2018 compliant. `manufacturing_auto_fixture_layout` LLM tool.
- **CAM G-code emitter** вң… вҖ” `cam_gcode_emit.py`: emit Fanuc-compatible RS-274 G-code from a waypoint toolpath (G00 rapid / G01 linear / G02 CW arc / G03 CCW arc / M03 spindle-on / M05 spindle-off / M06 tool change; I/J centre offsets; F feedrate modal; S spindle modal); `GcodeProgram` dataclass; `emit_gcode()` pure-Python function; `cam_emit_gcode` LLM tool. Round-trips through `parse_gcode`. Dialect: Fanuc 0i/18i/Haas/GRBL вүҘ 1.1. Honest limit: XY-plane arcs only (G17); LinuxCNC %, Heidenhain TCPM, Siemens TRAORI out of scope. References: NIST RS-274/NGC (Kramer et al. 2000) В§3.4вҖ“3.8; Smid CNC Programming Handbook (2008) В§3. 44 tests.
- **CAM lathe profile G-code emitter** вң… вҖ” `cam_lathe_profile.py`: emit complete Fanuc RS-274 lathe program from a 2-D axis-symmetric profile (XZ polyline); G71 rough turning cycle (P/Q/U/W/D/F/S words), G70 finish turning cycle, G96 constant surface speed, G97 constant RPM, M03/M05 spindle on/off, M06 tool change; `LatheProgram` dataclass; `emit_lathe_gcode(profile, stock, tool_id, sfm=600, ipr=0.25)` pure-Python; `cam_emit_lathe_gcode` LLM tool registered. Depth bar: cylinder Гҳ20вҶ’Гҳ10 step + tapered profile emit valid G71+G70 with stock allowance, 600 SFM steel, 0.25 mm/rev IPR; diameter programming (X = 2Г—radius); G18 ZX-plane preamble. Honest flag: Fanuc 0i-TF/30i dialect ONLY вҖ” Heidenhain TURN PLUS, Siemens ShopTurn CYCLE95, Mazak SmoothTurn, Okuma OSP lathe codes out of scope; G71 Type I only (monotone-decreasing X; concave features warned). References: NIST RS-274/NGC (Kramer et al. 2000) В§3.4вҖ“3.9; Smid CNC Programming Handbook (2008) В§6; Fanuc 0i-TF OM В§14.2/14.3. 47 tests.
- **CAM wire-EDM path** вң… вҖ” `cam_wire_edm_path.py`: Fanuc wire-EDM G-code from a 2-D profile (line + arc segments); G41/G42 cutter compensation (D-register = wire_radius + spark_gap; typical 0.135вҖ“0.150 mm); M50/M51 wire feed on/off; G01/G02/G03 with I/J; straight lead-in for safe compensation activation; `WireEDMProgram` dataclass; `square_profile` + `circle_profile` convenience builders; `cam_emit_wire_edm_gcode` LLM tool. Depth bar: 50Г—50 mm square вҶ’ D=0.1500 mm (wire 0.25 mm, gap 0.025 mm); circle вҶ’ G03 I/J=-25./I/J=+25.; all 46 tests green. Honest limits: 2-axis (XY) only вҖ” no wire taper (4-axis U/V), no threading hole automation, no skim passes, no variable-feed corners. Refs: Tlusty 2000 В§13; Fanuc B-59064EN/01; Rajurkar et al. CIRP Annals 62(2):779-801.
- **CAM lead-in / lead-out arc segments** вң… вҖ” `lead_in_out.py`: tangent-arc, line, and perpendicular lead-in/lead-out G-code segments for 2D contour milling; eliminates witness marks at cutter entry/exit (MH 31e В§1131); `LeadSpec` + `LeadResult` dataclasses; `generate_lead_in_out(spec, cutter_comp)` вҖ” arc type: G02/G03 with I/J offsets (Fanuc incremental arc-centre convention), lead-in angle Оұ (1вҖ“90В°, 90В° = classic perpendicular tangent entry), lead-in length = RВ·Оұ_rad; line type: G01 approach along contour tangent; perpendicular type: G01 from normal offset; G41/G42 cutter compensation activated in lead-in block, G40 cancel in lead-out; `cam_generate_lead_in_out` LLM tool registered; 54 tests green. Honest limits: **2D contours only (XY plane, constant Z)** вҖ” 3D ramp entry and helical entry are NOT implemented; no gouge/collision checking (use `cam_verify_toolpath_collision`); I/J offsets are incremental/Fanuc convention (verify if using absolute arc-centre mode). Refs: MH 31e В§1131; Fanuc Operator Manual В§G41/G42.
- **CAM 3D parallel-offset surface milling** вң… вҖ” `offset_3d_path.py`: `Offset3DSpec` + `Offset3DResult` + `generate_offset_3d_path(spec)` вҖ” raster (zig-zag parallel passes) toolpath at constant tool_radius Z-offset above a sampled z(x,y) surface grid; scallop height h = R вҲ’ sqrt(RВІ вҲ’ (ae/2)ВІ) (Chuang & Yang 1995; Held & Klingenstein 1991 В§3.1); bilinear z(x,y) interpolation; G21/G90/G94/M03/G00/G01/M05/M30 NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.5 G-code; `cam_generate_offset_3d_path` LLM tool registered; 71 tests green. **Honest limits: 3-axis Z-axis-aligned only** (spindle always +Z vertical вҖ” no 5-axis tool-axis tilt; steep walls >45В° receive slightly less than one tool_radius offset вҶ’ potential micro-gouge on steep flanks per MH 31e В§1139); **no gouge checking** (use `cam_verify_toolpath_collision`); **no z-level contouring / waterline passes** (raster only); no arc-fitting post-processor (all G01 linear segments); scallop formula is flat-surface approximation only (curved surface deviation not modelled). Time estimate constant-feed only (add 5вҖ“15 % per MH 31e В§1109). Refs: MH 31e В§1139 (3-axis surface offset); Held & Klingenstein (1991) Computers & Graphics 15(3):333вҖ“341; Chuang & Yang (1995) Intl J Mach Tools 35(2):261вҖ“267; NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.5.
- **CAM-DRESS-CYCLE-WHEEL** вң… вҖ” `dress_cycle.py`: `DressSpec` + `DressCycleResult` + `generate_dress_cycle(spec)` вҖ” open-loop grinding wheel dressing cycle G-code generator (traverse dressing); num_passes = ceil(total_dress_amount / depth_per_pass); per pass: G01 infeed X by depth_per_pass вҶ’ G01 traverse Z across wheel_width at traverse_rate вҶ’ G00 rapid-retract Z to start; G28 G91 Z0.0 reference return after final pass; G21/G90/G94/M05/M30 NIST RS-274/NGC preamble; `cam_generate_dress_cycle` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; 58 tests green. Dresser types: "single_point_diamond" (traverse 50вҖ“300 mm/min, depth 0.002вҖ“0.025 mm/pass) + "rotary_diamond" (traverse 100вҖ“800 mm/min, depth 0.005вҖ“0.050 mm/pass). HONEST: **open-loop only** вҖ” no in-process wheel diameter measurement or closed-loop correction (AE sensor, power monitoring, roundness gauging NOT implemented); uni-directional traverse only (+Z per pass, bi-directional oscillation NOT generated); no wheel-spindle synchronisation G-code for rotary roll speed; time estimate constant traverse + 3000 mm/min rapid Z retract only (acceleration ramps excluded, add 10вҖ“20%); G-code is RS-274/NGC / Fanuc 0i-PD compatible вҖ” controller-specific dress cycles (Siemens CYCLE12x, ANCA DressPro) NOT emitted; out-of-band advisory if traverse rate or depth outside MH 31e В§1145 safe bands. Refs: MH 31e В§1145 (Wheel dressing); Sandvik Coromant CoroGrind Grinding Handbook В§5 (Wheel conditioning) вҖ” `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/dress_cycle.py`.
- **CAM-MILLING-DWELL-CHECK** вң… вҖ” `dwell_audit.py`: `DwellAuditSpec` + `DwellAuditReport` + `audit_milling_dwells(spec)` вҖ” G-code G04 dwell analysis for milling programs; parses every `G04 X<seconds>` (NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.5) and `G04 P<ms>` (Fanuc/Haas) command; estimates G01 cutting time from line-by-line distance / modal feed rate (G94 mm/min); `total_dwell_time_ms`, `num_dwells`, `dwell_per_op_ms`, `total_program_time_estimate_s`, `dwell_ratio_pct`, `excessive` flag (ratio > `max_total_dwell_ratio_pct`, default 5 %), `suspicious_long_dwells` (> `max_recommended_dwell_per_op_ms`, default 500 ms); modal G20/G21, G90/G91, G94/G95 state tracked; `cam_audit_milling_dwells` LLM tool registered; 45 tests green. HONEST: heuristic only вҖ” some dwells are deliberate (G89 boring spindle-settle, machine warm-up, coolant-pressure build); `excessive=True` is NOT proof of a programming error; G02/G03 arc moves excluded from cutting-time estimate (inflates dwell_ratio_pct for arc-heavy programs); G95 feed-per-rev blocks contribute 0 to cutting time; rapid rate assumed 10 000 mm/min (generic constant); acceleration ramps add 15вҖ“30 % to wall-clock time (Altintas 2012 В§5.7). Refs: MH 31e В§1140 (Dwell commands); NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.5 вҖ” `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/dwell_audit.py`.
- **CAM-G-CODE-ARC-LINEARIZE** вң… вҖ” `arc_linearize.py`: `ArcLinearizeSpec` + `ArcLinearizeResult` + `linearize_arcs(spec)` вҖ” converts G02/G03 arc commands to G01 linear segments for legacy CNC controllers that do not support circular interpolation (older Mach3 setups, plasma tables, laser cutters, some wire EDM). Supports both I/J centre-offset format and R radius format (R > 0 minor arc, R < 0 major arc per RS-274/NGC В§3.5.3); full-circle I/J arcs detected and handled; helical arcs (Z travel on G02/G03) linearised with linear Z interpolation. Segment angle О”Оё = 2В·acos(1 вҲ’ Оө/R) per MH 31e В§1130; N = ceil(Оё_arc / О”Оё); minimum-segment-length floor (default 0.05 mm) prevents degenerate micro-moves on tiny arcs. Returns `linearized_gcode`, `num_arcs_processed`, `total_segments_emitted`, `max_actual_chord_error_mm`, `expansion_ratio`; `cam_linearize_arcs` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; 42 tests green. HONEST: **modal G-codes not preserved** вҖ” each emitted segment carries an explicit `G01`; downstream code must not assume modal state after a linearised arc block; **XY-plane (G17) arcs only** вҖ” G18/G19 plane selection is passed through but arc maths does NOT adapt (G18/G19 arcs will linearise incorrectly); **full-circle R-format arcs** (start == end) are ambiguous per RS-274/NGC В§3.5.3 and are passed through unchanged with a warning comment; feed rate F is copied from the original arc line to every G01 segment (no arc-length-proportional feed correction); helical arcs linearised with linear Z interpolation (geometrically correct for uniform-pitch helices only). Refs: NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.5.3; MH 31e В§1130 вҖ” `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/arc_linearize.py`.
- **CAM-MILL-PROFILE-ROUGHING** вң… вҖ” `profile_roughing.py`: `ProfileMillSpec` + `ProfileRoughingResult` + `generate_profile_roughing(spec)` вҖ” multi-pass 2D profile roughing toolpath that progressively removes material from a closed CCW polygon boundary with adjustable stock offset, leaving a finish allowance for the final pass. Strategy: `num_axial = ceil(total_depth / depth_per_pass)` axial levels; per level, successive radial inward passes from `stock_offset_mm` down to `finish_allowance_mm` (step = cutter_radius = D/2 per pass, outermost вҶ’ finish-spring pass); polygon offset via vertex bisector / Minkowski-sum approximation (Preparata & Shamos 1985 В§8.4); G21/G90/G94/M03/G00/G01/M05/M30 NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.5 G-code; `cam_generate_profile_roughing` LLM tool registered; 76 tests green. HONEST: **2D polygon profile only** вҖ” no pocket-with-islands (island/internal boundaries not supported); no climb/conventional milling differentiation (all passes use same direction); no helical or ramping entry (plunges at feed rate); no cutter compensation G41/G42 (offsets pre-computed in software); polygon offset is bisector approximation вҖ” exact for convex profiles, may self-intersect on highly non-convex geometries (use Clipper library for production); time estimate constant-feed only (add 5вҖ“15 % per MH 31e В§1109). MRR = (stock_polygon_area вҲ’ finish_polygon_area) Г— total_depth. Refs: MH 31e В§1131 (profile milling); Sandvik CoroPlus Contour Roughing (2024); NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.5 вҖ” `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/profile_roughing.py`.
- **CAM-DRY-MACHINING-CHECK** вң… вҖ” `dry_machining_check.py`: `DryMachiningSpec` + `DryMachiningReport` + `check_dry_machining(spec)` вҖ” dry-machining feasibility checker per Sandvik Coromant Dry/Near-Dry Machining Application Guide (2024) and ISO 8688-1 tool-wear standards. Inputs: `workpiece_material` (8 classes: steel-low-carbon, steel-medium-carbon, steel-stainless-austenitic, cast-iron-grey, aluminum-wrought, aluminum-cast, titanium-Ti6Al4V, nickel-inconel-718), `tool_coating` (uncoated | TiN | TiAlN | AlCrN | diamond-CVD), `vc_m_per_min`, `fz_mm_per_tooth`, `ae_mm`, `ap_mm`, `tool_diameter_mm`, `operation` (milling-roughing | milling-finishing | drilling | turning). Returns: `feasible` (bool), `recommendation` (str), `tool_life_reduction_factor` (1.0 = same as flood; 0.5 = half вҖ” Sandvik mid-range Taylor-model values), `min_coating_required` (str), `max_vc_dry_m_per_min` (Sandvik catalogue absolute upper limit), `warnings` (list), `honest_caveat`. Rules (Sandvik Coromant 2024 + ISO 8688-1 + Klocke & EisenblГӨtter CIRP 1997): cast-iron-grey + carbide вҶ’ FEASIBLE (factor 0.90вҖ“1.00; graphite solid lubrication; uncoated acceptable; TiAlN preferred); steel-low-carbon + TiAlN/AlCrN вҶ’ CONDITIONAL (factor 0.70вҖ“0.85; max vc 180 m/min dry); steel-medium-carbon вҶ’ CONDITIONAL (factor 0.65вҖ“0.80; max vc 150 m/min; AlCrN preferred for hot hardness >900 В°C); steel-stainless-austenitic + AlCrN/TiAlN вҶ’ CONDITIONAL (factor 0.50вҖ“0.65; max vc 120 m/min; uncoated/TiN NOT acceptable вҖ” BUE + crater wear); aluminum-wrought / aluminum-cast вҶ’ NOT FEASIBLE (BUE / chip welding; flood or MQL + diamond-CVD); titanium-Ti6Al4V вҶ’ CHALLENGING (factor 0.30вҖ“0.50; MQL minimum required; combustion risk above 60 m/min fully dry per Biermann 2020 В§4); nickel-inconel-718 вҶ’ NOT FEASIBLE (extreme work-hardening; flood mandatory). Coating adequacy matrix (coating Г— material, 40 entries). `cam_check_dry_machining` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_cam/__init__.py`; 59 tests green. HONEST: rules are heuristic averages from Sandvik catalogue + CIRP literature вҖ” NOT a substitute for chip-form testing; tool_life_reduction_factor uses mid-range Sandvik Taylor-model values, uncertainty Вұ40 %; actual feasibility depends on machine rigidity, spindle thermal compensation, chip-air evacuation, insert geometry, exact alloy composition, BUE tendency, and surface finish requirement вҖ” verify against Sandvik CoroPlus ToolGuide before production. Ti6Al4V tool combustion risk above 60 m/min flagged but NOT modelled (physical testing required). Grey cast iron dust/fume hazard requires machine enclosure and extraction. Module does NOT model thermal FEA, chip-evacuation dynamics, or machine-specific spindle temperature behaviour. Refs: Sandvik Coromant Dry/Near-Dry Machining Application Guide (2024); ISO 8688-1:1989; Klocke F. & EisenblГӨtter G. CIRP Ann. 46(2) 1997; Biermann D. et al. "Dry and Near-Dry Machining" Springer 2020 В§4 вҖ” `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/dry_machining_check.py`.
- **CAM-COOLANT-FLOW-CHECK** вң… вҖ” `coolant_flow_check.py`: `MachiningOpForCoolant` + `CoolantFlowReport` + `check_coolant_flow(spec)` вҖ” recommends minimum coolant flow rate [L/min] and pressure [bar] for a CNC machining operation; verifies whether the spindle/through-tool coolant system can deliver them. Flow heuristic: `required_flow = flow_factor Г— MRR`; material factors (Sandvik CoroPlus В§3): steel=0.50, stainless=0.60, aluminum=0.30, titanium=0.50, composite=0.20 L/min per cmВі/min. Pressure thresholds (Sandvik CoroPlus В§3): titanium any coolant вүҘ70 bar; through-tool d>8mm вүҘ20 bar; through-tool dвүӨ8mm вүҘ10 bar; flood вүҘ2 bar; mist вүҘ4 bar; MQL вүҘ5 bar. Material-specific recommended coolant type: titanium вҶ’ through_tool (mandatory high-pressure); stainless вҶ’ through_tool (chip-breaking + heat); steel вҶ’ flood; aluminum вҶ’ flood; composite вҶ’ MQL. `cam_check_coolant_flow` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; 41 tests green. HONEST: flow factors are heuristic averages вҖ” actual requirements depend on ae/ap ratio, specific alloy thermal conductivity, insert grade, and chip volume; coolant chemistry (concentration, pH, biocide), chip-evacuation effectiveness, and nozzle positioning are NOT modelled; high-pressure through-tool channels require spindle + toolholder physically rated for that pressure (seal integrity not checked); MQL/mist flow is lubricant volumetric flow, not flood coolant; composite CFRP/GFRP may require dry or MQL-only machining regardless of flow rate. Refs: Sandvik CoroPlus Coolant Application Guide В§3 (2024); MH 31e В§1140 (Coolant application) вҖ” `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/coolant_flow_check.py`.
- **CAM chip-load + chip-thinning calculator** вң… вҖ” `chip_load_calc.py`: `MillingOpSpec` + `ChipLoadReport` + `compute_chip_load(spec)` вҖ” fz = Vf/(nГ—z) (MH 31e В§1136); radial chip-thinning Krad = D/(2В·sqrt(DВ·ae вҲ’ aeВІ)) when ae < D/2 else 1.0 (Sandvik CoroPlus 2024; Stephenson-Agapiou В§6); actual_chip_load = fz Г— Krad; MRR = ae Г— ap Г— Vf / 1000 cmВі/min; Sandvik CoroPlus 2024 recommended fz ranges (carbide/aluminium 0.05вҖ“0.15, carbide/steel 0.05вҖ“0.20, HSS/aluminium 0.03вҖ“0.10, HSS/steel 0.03вҖ“0.12, ceramic 0.10вҖ“0.30 mm/tooth); compliant flag; work_material lookup supports aluminium/aluminum/steel/stainless_303/aluminum_6061; `cam_compute_chip_load` LLM tool registered; 32 tests green. Honest caveats: thinning formula assumes circular arc-of-engagement (flat workpiece, peripheral end-mill only) вҖ” ball-nose tools, curved workpieces, profiling passes change engagement geometry; no climb/conventional distinction (both use same Krad); tool deflection NOT modelled (see Altintas 2012 В§3.6); recommended ranges are material-class averages вҖ” verify against CoroPlus ToolGuide for production. References: MH 31e В§1136; Sandvik CoroPlus Milling/feed-per-tooth (2024); Stephenson-Agapiou В§6.
- **CAM-CHIP-LOAD-VALIDATE** вң… вҖ” `chip_load_validate.py`: `ChipLoadSpec` + `ChipLoadReport` + `validate_chip_load(spec)` вҖ” validates programmed fz against published Sandvik Coromant / Kennametal / Harvey Tool catalog ranges for 7 specific workpiece materials (steel-1018, steel-4140-soft, stainless-304, aluminum-6061, titanium-Ti6Al4V, cast-iron-grey, plastic-acetal) Г— 5 diameter buckets (xs вүӨ3 mm, sm 3вҖ“6 mm, md 6вҖ“12 mm, lg 12вҖ“20 mm, xl >20 mm). Chip-thinning using Sandvik simplified formula fz_eff = fz_nom Г— D/(2В·ae) when ae < D/2 else 1.0. Derived spindle speed n = vcГ—1000/(ПҖГ—D) and table feed = fzГ—flutesГ—n. Warnings: chip-thinning active (factor + effective value), OVER-FEED (effective_fz > fz_max вҶ’ tool fracture risk), RUBBING/WORK-HARDENING (effective_fz < 60% fz_min), under-feed, high-engagement-at-upper-fz. `cam_validate_chip_load` LLM tool registered; 46 tests green. HONEST: ranges are catalog mid-field averages (Sandvik 2024 + Kennametal 2024 + Harvey Tool 2024) for carbide end-mills with TiAlN coating вҖ” actual limits depend on insert grade, edge prep, alloy hardness, machine rigidity, holder runout (<5 Ојm), and coolant strategy; chip-thinning formula is simplified linear Sandvik approximation (not exact trigonometric form); tool deflection, regenerative chatter, and harmonic excitation NOT modelled (see Altintas 2012 В§3); runout >5 Ојm effectively halves per-tooth chip load but is NOT corrected for; ranges apply to peripheral end-milling only (slot-drill, ball-nose, chamfer-mill require manufacturer-specific tables) вҖ” verify against CoroPlus ToolGuide for production. References: Sandvik CoroPlus Milling Technical Guide (2024); Kennametal Milling Application Guide (2024); Harvey Tool Speeds & Feeds (2024); MH 31e В§1136 вҖ” `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/chip_load_validate.py`.
- **CAM-DEEP-PECK-LIVE-TIME** вң… вҖ” `peck_live_time.py`: `PeckCycleParams` + `PeckLiveTimeReport` + `compute_peck_live_time(params)` вҖ” G83 peck-drill cycle live-time analytics: num_pecks = ceil(depth/peck_depth); per-peck model: rapid-down from R-plane to current bore top + feed drilling stroke + rapid-up to R-plane + optional dwell; live_time_fraction = cutting_s / total_cycle_s; adequate flag (threshold 0.50 per Sandvik CoroPlus 2024); separates cutting / retract / dwell times; `cam_compute_peck_live_time` LLM tool registered; 52 tests green. Use: chip-evacuation analysis (low live fraction вҶ’ heat cycling вҶ’ accelerated tool wear); tool-life budgeting (cutting-second accounting). Honest caveats: **ideal rigid rapid assumed** вҖ” no acceleration ramps at peck reversal (real machines add 5вҖ“20 % retract overhead per Sandvik CoroPlus 2024 В§Annex C servo dynamics); full-retract G83 per NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.8.4 вҖ” partial-retract G73/Haas-chip-break controllers will yield higher actual live fractions; dwell reported separately (not charged to cutting or retract). References: MH 31e В§1132; Sandvik CoroPlus Drill Cycle Analytics (2024); NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.8.4.
- **CAM** вң… вҖ” 2.5D + 3D parallel/waterline + lathe + 5-axis constant-tilt + 3+2 indexed; tool DB; LinuxCNC/GRBL/Fanuc posts; G83 peck-drilling canned cycle (NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.8.4); G84/G74 rigid tapping canned cycle (NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.8.4 + MH 31e В§1934; `cam_generate_tap_cycle` LLM tool; honest caveat: rigid tap timing only вҖ” floating tap holders not modelled); G85/G86/G89 boring canned cycles (NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.8.4 + MH 31e В§1162; `cam_generate_boring_cycle` LLM tool; G85=feed-out Ra 0.8 Ојm, G86=spindle-stop-out Ra 1.6 Ојm, G89=dwell-out Ra 0.4 Ојm; honest caveat: single-point boring bar only вҖ” no roughing/finishing pass differentiation; G89 P-word in Ојs per NIST vs ms Fanuc); **zig-zag face-mill toolpath** (`face_mill_path.py`): `FaceMillSpec` + `FaceMillResult` + `generate_face_mill_path(spec, climb_milling=True)` вҖ” rectangular pocket bbox + tool diameter + 70 % stepover (MH 31e В§1136) вҶ’ full G21/G90/G94/M03/G00/G01/M30 NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.5 G-code; climb vs conventional milling; `cam_generate_face_mill_path` LLM tool; 71 tests. Honest limits: 2.5D only (single flat depth); no helical entry; no cutter comp G41/G42; no high-feed (HFC) strategies; no corner arcs at pass reversal; time estimate excludes acceleration ramps (add 5вҖ“15 %, MH 31e В§1109). **Rigid-tap pre-run check** (`rigid_tapping_check.py`): `RigidTapSpec` + `RigidTapReport` + `check_rigid_tap(spec)` вҖ” validates a rigid-tap operation against machine spindle synchronisation capability and tap-strength limits; torque T = KВ·DВі (Sandvik CoroPlus 2024 + MH 31e В§1934 empirical K coefficients: HSS-steel=0.35, cobalt-steel=0.30, carbide-steel=0.25, HSS-aluminum=0.10; 4 materials Г— 3 tool classes); feed F = pitch Г— rpm; sync_compliant = rpm вүӨ machine_max_sync_rpm; tap_breakage_risk (low/medium/high) heuristic: deep hole (>3Г—D), rpm above material/tool limit, stainless+small+HSS combo; recommended_feed_override_pct; metric (M6x1.0, M10x1.5) + inch UNC/UNF (1/4-20, 3/8-16) thread parser; `cam_check_rigid_tap` LLM tool registered; 58 tests green. Honest caveat: K coefficients Вұ35 % вҖ” coolant effects, tap geometry (spiral-flute vs spiral-point), thread-fit class, and worn tool state NOT modelled. References: Sandvik CoroPlus Technical Guide 2024; MH 31e В§1934; NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.8.4.
- **CAM-G-CODE-ARC-LINEARIZE** вң… вҖ” `arc_linearize.py`: `ArcLinearizeSpec` + `ArcLinearizeResult` + `linearize_arcs(spec)` вҖ” converts G02/G03 arc commands to G01 linear segments for legacy CNC controllers that do not support circular interpolation. Supports I/J centre-offset + R radius formats; full-circle I/J arcs handled; helical arcs linearised with linear Z interpolation. О”Оё = 2В·acos(1 вҲ’ Оө/R) per MH 31e В§1130; min_segment_length_mm floor prevents micro-moves; `cam_linearize_arcs` LLM tool registered; 42 tests green. HONEST: modal G-codes not preserved (explicit G01 each segment); XY-plane (G17) arcs only; full-circle R-format arcs ambiguous вҖ” passed through with warning comment. Refs: NIST RS-274/NGC В§3.5.3; MH 31e В§1130 вҖ” `packages/kerf-cam/src/kerf_cam/arc_linearize.py`.
- **Slicing** вң… вҖ” plane-section, CNC layered, 3D-print G-code (Cura, Tier 1).
- **HVAC duct pressure loss вҖ” ASHRAE В§35 fittings** вң… вҖ” ASHRAE Handbook of Fundamentals 2021 В§35 (Ch. 21) Table 21-1 fitting loss coefficients: 10 fitting kinds (smooth/segmented elbows, 45В° elbow, tee branch/through, gradual/abrupt transitions, butterfly damper, gradual reducer/expander); `fitting_pressure_loss()` + `compute_duct_run_pressure_drop()` (straight-duct + fittings combined); `build_loss_table()` with full ASHRAE citations; 2 new LLM tools (`hvac.fitting_pressure_loss`, `hvac.compute_run_pressure_drop`).
- **Slicing** вң… вҖ” plane-section, CNC layered, 3D-print G-code (Cura, Tier 1); infill pattern library (gyroid TPMS, honeycomb, triangular grid, concentric) вң….
- **1D system simulation (kerf-1dsim)** вң… вҖ” Modelica-compatible equation-based DAE solver (BDF-1); R/L/C/MassSpring/Damper/ThermalConductor/FluidResistor components; **Modelica .mo import** вң… вҖ” recursive-descent subset parser: `model/end`, `parameter Real`, `Real`, `equation`, `der()`, `connect()`, `package` wrapping; `modelica_to_kerf_components` mapper; `load_modelica_library` directory scan; `sim_import_modelica` LLM tool registered. *Modelica subset support вҖ” NOT certified Modelica compliance.*
- **1DSim** вң… вҖ” Modelica-compatible equation-based DAE solver (BDF-1); Modelica import; FMI export; **SPICE 3F5 netlist import + MNA DC analysis** (R/C/L/V/I/Q/M parsing, `sim_import_spice` + `sim_dc_analysis` LLM tools; SPICE subset вҖ” NOT SPICE-certified, BSIM models out of scope).

- **KiCad-class PCB design** вң… вҖ” ERC, hier-schematic, buses/diff-pairs, net classes/rules, length tuning, via stitching/teardrops, shove router, copper pour, DRC, netlist-vs-layout consistency DRC (IPC-7351B) вң….

- **Wiring/harness** вң… вҖ” WireViz YAMLвҶ’SVG (2D) + 3D polyline harness routing + formboard-flatten 2D manufacturing output (T-37, P1-7 complete).
- **PLC** вң… вҖ” MATIEC lint Tier 1.

T-225..T-230.
- **FIRMWARE-PERIPHERAL-MAP-VERIFY** вң… вҖ” peripheral pin-mapping verifier against MCU hardware alt-function tables; detects: bad alt-function, pin conflict, missing required, peripheral pin-mux conflict, voltage incompatibility (5V tolerant check); embedded STM32F411 LQFP64 alt-function table (RM0383 В§7.3, PA0..PC15) + ATmega328P PDIP-28 (datasheet В§13, all 23 GPIOs); `firmware_verify_peripheral_map` LLM tool; `chip_specs.py` + `peripheral_map_verify.py`; 59 tests. NOT a substitute for ST CubeMX / Atmel Start.
- **Silicon / IC layout** вң… вҖ” VHDL + Verilog parsers; GHDL + Yosys + ngspice bridges; GDS II / OASIS I/O; SKY130 PDK; LEF/Liberty readers; OpenROAD place-and-route; DRC + LVS + parasitic extraction; mask fracturing; SPICE waveform viewer UI вң…. T-231..T-248.
- **Silicon / IBIS 7.1 signal integrity** вң… вҖ” IBIS 7.1 model import + eye-diagram estimation (`silicon_import_ibis`, `silicon_eye_diagram`); [Component]/[Pin]/[Model]/[Pulldown]/[Pullup]/[GND_clamp]/[POWER_clamp]/[Ramp]/[Voltage Range]; IV-curve interpolation; analytical eye opening height/width/jitter at arbitrary bit-rate + load. NOT IBIS-certified.
- **Firmware / embedded** вң… вҖ” board catalogue (Arduino/ESP32/STM32/RP2040/AVR); library cache; direct-gcc orchestrator (`avr-gcc`/`arm-none-eabi-gcc`/`xtensa-esp32-elf`); upload wrappers; serial monitor panel; LLM tools. T-225..T-230.
- **FIRMWARE-PERIPHERAL-MAP-VERIFY** вң… вҖ” peripheral pin-mapping verifier; detects bad alt-function, pin conflict, missing required, peripheral mux conflict, voltage incompatibility; embedded STM32F411 LQFP64 (RM0383 В§7.3) + ATmega328P PDIP-28 tables; `firmware_verify_peripheral_map` LLM tool; 59 tests.
- **FIRMWARE-CLOCK-TREE-VERIFY** вң… вҖ” STM32 clock-tree verifier; real PLL arithmetic (VCO = HSE/PLLM Г— PLLN; SYSCLK = VCO/PLLP; USB = VCO/PLLQ); detects VCO out of range, SYSCLK exceeded (100 MHz F411 / 168 MHz F407), APB1 > 42 MHz, APB2 > 84 MHz, USB вү  48 MHz (Вұ500 ppm), ADC > 36 MHz; embedded RM0383 В§6 (STM32F411) + RM0090 В§6 (STM32F407) tables; `firmware_verify_clock_tree` LLM tool; `clock_tree_specs.py` + `clock_tree_verify.py`; 71 tests. LOOKUP-TABLE ONLY вҖ” no jitter/phase-noise model.
- **FIRMWARE-DMA-CHANNEL-CONFLICT** вң… вҖ” STM32 DMA controller channel-assignment verifier; detects: INVALID_ASSIGNMENT (peripheral not legal on stream/channel, with alternatives), STREAM_CONFLICT (two peripherals on same stream), UNKNOWN_CONTROLLER; embedded RM0383 В§10.3.3 Tables 27вҖ“28 (STM32F411) + RM0090 В§10.3.3 Tables 42вҖ“43 (STM32F407) stream-channel-peripheral matrices; `firmware_verify_dma_assignments` LLM tool; `dma_specs.py` + `dma_channel_conflict.py`; 64 tests. STATIC CONFLICT DETECTION ONLY вҖ” no DMA throughput/priority/FIFO model.
- **FIRMWARE-INTERRUPT-PRIORITY-VERIFY** вң… вҖ” Cortex-M NVIC interrupt priority verifier; detects: OUT_OF_RANGE (priority outside [0,15] for STM32F4xx 4-bit field), SAME_PREEMPT_PRIORITY (two peripherals share a preemption level вҖ” non-deterministic tie-break by IRQ number, ARM Cortex-M Generic UG В§B3.3), RT_IN_LOW_BAND (TIM/EXTI in LOW band, pre-empted by NORMAL), NON_RT_IN_RT_BAND (USB/ADC/RTC in RT band), UNKNOWN_PERIPHERAL, BASEPRI_MISCONFIGURED (BASEPRI=0 disables masking, В§B1.5.4); PRIGROUP-aware preemption-level extraction (CMSIS NVIC_EncodePriority formula); embedded RM0383 Rev 3 В§10 STM32F411 + RM0090 Rev 19 В§10 STM32F407 IRQ tables; `firmware_verify_interrupt_priorities` LLM tool; `interrupt_specs.py` + `interrupt_priority_verify.py`; 93 tests. STATIC CHECKS ONLY вҖ” no WCET, RTOS priority-inheritance, or runtime latency model.
- **FIRMWARE-MEMORY-MAP-VERIFY** вң… вҖ” Cortex-M linker memory-layout verifier; detects: FLASH_OVERFLOW (sections exceed chip Flash capacity, RM0383 В§3), SRAM_OVERFLOW (runtime sections exceed chip SRAM capacity), STACK_OVERFLOW_INTO_BSS (stack + .data + .bss > SRAM; conservative static check), VECTOR_TABLE_MISPLACED (vector table base not at Flash start and not in SRAM for VTOR remap, ARM Cortex-M Generic UG В§B3.2.4), ISR_COUNT_MISMATCH (vector table entry count != chip NVIC count, RM0383 В§10); embedded memory maps for STM32F411 (512 KB Flash / 128 KB SRAM, RM0383 В§3) + STM32F407 (1 MB Flash / 128 KB SRAM, RM0090 В§3); `firmware_verify_memory_map` LLM tool; `memory_map_verify.py`; 63 tests. STATIC SECTION-SIZE CHECK ONLY вҖ” does not run the linker; use arm-none-eabi-size + map-file for production audits.
- **FIRMWARE-SPI-TIMING-VERIFY** вң… вҖ” SPI master/slave timing compatibility verifier; checks: master clock_hz вүӨ slave max_clk_hz, master setup_ns вүҘ slave min_setup_ns, master hold_ns вүҘ slave min_hold_ns, CPOL exact match, CPHA exact match (Motorola SPI spec canonical CPOL/CPHA definition + ARM Cortex-M Generic UG В§SPI Timing); reports clock_margin_pct, setup_margin_ns, hold_margin_ns, violation list; violation codes: CLOCK_TOO_FAST, SETUP_VIOLATION, HOLD_VIOLATION, CPOL_MISMATCH, CPHA_MISMATCH; edge case: MCP3008 ADC at 1.35 MHz max (DS21295D В§1.0 Table 1-1) verified against STM32F411 SPI1 @ 1 MHz; `firmware_verify_spi_timing` LLM tool; `spi_timing_verify.py`; 41 tests. HONEST: assumes ideal square-wave signals; ignores PCB trace propagation delay and crosstalk; use a logic analyser on real hardware.
- **FIRMWARE-I2C-CLOCK-STRETCH-CHECK** вң… вҖ” IВІC clock-stretch worst-case effective speed analyser; computes effective IВІC bus frequency when slaves exercise SCL clock stretching and verifies SCL low-timeout compliance; algorithm per NXP UM10204 Rev 7 В§3.1.9: t_byte_effective = (9/f_nom) + stretch_us/1e6; f_effective = 9/t_byte_effective; timeout_compliant = (worst_stretch_us Г— bytes_per_txn) < scl_low_timeout_msГ—1000; reports effective_clock_hz, worst_case_stretch_per_byte_us, timeout_compliant, slowest_slave, throughput_degradation_pct; `firmware_check_i2c_clock_stretch` LLM tool; `i2c_clock_stretch_check.py`; 36 tests. HONEST: assumes synchronous single-master bus вҖ” multi-master arbitration NOT modelled; stretch accumulated conservatively on every byte; rise/fall derating and t_BUF overhead not included; verify on target hardware with a logic analyser. Refs: NXP UM10204 Rev 7 В§3.1.9; STM32F411 RM0383 В§26.6 TIMEOUTB register.
- **FIRMWARE-UART-BAUD-DRIFT-CHECK** вң… вҖ” UART baud-rate drift analyser; given MCU clock (Hz) and UBRR divisor register value, computes actual baud rate and percent drift vs nominal; flags unreliable links (|drift| вүҘ 2%, per RS-232 / IEEE Std 488 baud-rate tolerance); recommends closest standard baud + UBRR combinations that achieve < 0.5% drift with the same clock; ATmega normal mode: baud = clock / (16Г—(UBRR+1)); double_speed (U2X): baud = clock / (8Г—(UBRR+1)); standard bauds: [9600, 19200, 38400, 57600, 115200, 230400, 460800, 921600]; `UartConfigSpec` + `BaudDriftReport` dataclasses; `check_uart_baud_drift` function; `firmware_check_uart_baud_drift` LLM tool; `uart_baud_drift_check.py`; 24 tests. HONEST: ATmega integer-divisor model is exact for AVR; for STM32 (fractional BRR register, RM0383 В§19) this model OVER-ESTIMATES drift вҖ” the STM32 fractional generator typically achieves < 0.1% on standard bauds whereas this integer model reports ~0.94% at 80 MHz / 115200; clock-source tolerance (crystal Вұ100 ppm, resonator Вұ0.5%) not modelled; verify on target hardware with oscilloscope or logic analyser. Refs: ATmega328P В§19 (USART); STM32F411 RM0383 В§19; IEEE Std 488.
- **FIRMWARE-FLASH-WEAR-LEVEL** вң… вҖ” MCU flash endurance and time-to-failure estimator for EEPROM-like wear-leveling; given sector layout, write rate, and N-sector wear-leveling pool: total_writes = writes_per_second Г— 31,557,600 s/yr Г— lifetime_years; sector_erase_events = ceil(total_writes / ceil(sector_size / bytes_per_write)); cycles_per_sector = sector_erase_events / N; adequate = cycles_per_sector вүӨ endurance_cycles; time_to_failure_years = endurance Г— N Г— WA / writes_per_sec / sec_per_yr; recommended_sectors = ceil(sector_erases / endurance); depth-bar: STM32F411 128 KB sector (RM0383 В§3, 10k cycles), 1 write/s, 10 yr, 1 sector вҶ’ 3.15e8 cycles (31,558Г— over limit, need ~31,558 sectors); same with 100 sectors вҶ’ 3.15e6 (still 316Г— over limit); ATmega328P EEPROM (В§11, 100k cycles), 0.0001 write/s, 10 yr вҶ’ 31,558 cycles вҶ’ adequate; `FlashSpec` + `WriteWorkload` + `FlashWearReport` dataclasses; `compute_flash_wear` function; `firmware_compute_flash_wear` LLM tool; `flash_wear_level.py`; 26 tests. HONEST: assumes perfect uniform wear distribution вҖ” real algorithms (NuttX MTD, Zephyr NVS, ST EEPROM emulation AN2594) achieve ~80вҖ“90% of ideal; divide time_to_failure_years by 0.85 for conservative estimate; write amplification is worst-case (one sector erase per logical write); streaming / buffered writes achieve lower WA; temperature derating not modelled (STM32F411 endurance halves at Tj = 125В°C per RM0383 В§3 Table 6). Refs: STM32F411 RM0383 В§3; ATmega328P В§11; JEDEC JESD47 В§9.
- **FIRMWARE-FLASH-WEAR-LEVEL** вң… вҖ” MCU flash endurance and time-to-failure estimator for EEPROM-like wear-leveling; total_writes = writes_per_second Г— 31,557,600 s/yr Г— lifetime_years; cycles_per_sector = ceil(total_writes / WA) / N; adequate = cycles_per_sector вүӨ endurance_cycles; recommended_sectors = ceil(sector_erases / endurance); depth-bar: STM32F411 128 KB sector (RM0383 В§3, 10k cycles), 1 write/s, 10 yr, 1 sector вҶ’ 3.15e8 cycles (inadequate); ATmega328P EEPROM (В§11, 100k cycles), 0.0001 write/s, 10 yr вҶ’ 31,558 cycles (adequate); `FlashSpec` + `WriteWorkload` + `FlashWearReport` dataclasses; `compute_flash_wear` function; `firmware_compute_flash_wear` LLM tool; `flash_wear_level.py`; 26 tests. HONEST: assumes perfect uniform wear distribution вҖ” real algorithms (NuttX MTD, Zephyr NVS, ST AN2594) achieve ~80вҖ“90% of ideal; WA model is worst-case; temperature derating not modelled. Refs: STM32F411 RM0383 В§3; ATmega328P В§11; JEDEC JESD47 В§9.
- **FIRMWARE-RAM-USAGE-AUDIT** вң… вҖ” MCU RAM utilisation auditor; given .data (initialised globals), .bss (zero-inited globals), heap_max_bytes (worst-case dynamic allocation estimate), stack_max_bytes (worst-case stack depth estimate), and total_ram_bytes: static_alloc = data + bss; dynamic_alloc = heap + stack; total_used = static_alloc + dynamic_alloc; free_bytes = max(0, total_ram вҲ’ total_used); utilization_pct = total_used / total_ram Г— 100; within_budget = total_used вүӨ 80% of total_ram (10% safety guard for interrupt frames + malloc metadata); recommendation identifies largest contributor when over budget; depth-bar: STM32F411 128 KB (RM0383 В§2) data=8KB/bss=16KB/heap=24KB/stack=8KB вҶ’ 56 KB used, 72 KB free, 43.75% util вҶ’ adequate; ATmega328P 2 KB (В§8) data=500B/bss=1200B/heap=200B/stack=100B вҶ’ 2000 B used, 48 B free, 97.66% вҶ’ over budget; `MemorySectionSizes` + `RamUsageReport` dataclasses; `audit_ram_usage` function; `firmware_audit_ram_usage` LLM tool; `ram_usage_audit.py`; 46 tests. HONEST: static estimate only вҖ” does not account for malloc fragmentation (budget 20вҖ“30% overhead for general-purpose allocators) or interrupt-driven stack growth (each Cortex-M interrupt frame = 32 B; nested ISRs multiply this); RTOS task stacks not counted unless included in heap_max_bytes / stack_max_bytes; validate stack peak with stack-painting or RTOS uxTaskGetStackHighWaterMark(). Refs: RM0383 Rev 3 В§2 (STM32F411 SRAM map); ATmega328P В§8 (SRAM organisation).
- **FIRMWARE-STACK-DEPTH-ESTIMATE** вң… вҖ” static worst-case stack depth estimator for Cortex-M / ATmega firmware; DFS through the function call graph accumulating per-function frame sizes; detects recursive cycles (back-edges); adds ISR preemption overhead once (default 32 B = Cortex-M3/M4/M7 exception frame: 8 registers Г— 4 B, ARM Cortex-M Generic UG В§B1.5.6); depth-bar: main(100 B) вҶ’ A(200 B) вҶ’ B(50 B) + ISR 32 B = 382 B total; cycle AвҶ’BвҶ’A flagged as has_cycles=True; ATmega variant passes isr_overhead_bytes=3 (PC save only); multiple-callee branching takes deepest path; `FunctionFrame` + `StackDepthReport` dataclasses; `estimate_stack_depth` function; `firmware_estimate_stack_depth` LLM tool; `stack_depth_estimate.py`; 38 tests. HONEST: STATIC ESTIMATE ONLY вҖ” does not account for VLA (variable-length arrays; makes exact depth undecidable), alloca(), longjmp/setjmp, or indirect calls (function pointers, callbacks); frame sizes must come from arm-none-eabi-gcc / avr-gcc -fstack-usage (*.su files), not guesses; RTOS tasks each have their own stack вҖ” analyse each task independently; recursive cycles report a per-iteration lower bound only. Refs: ARM IHI 0042F AAPCS В§5.2/В§6.1; ARM Cortex-M Generic UG В§B1.5.6; Greenwood (2011) "Static Stack Analysis for Embedded Systems" В§3; Brylow et al. (2001) LCTES/OM.
- **FIRMWARE-RTOS-PRIORITY-CHECK** вң… вҖ” FreeRTOS / Zephyr / ChibiOS task priority assignment verifier; Liu-Layland (1973) rate-monotonic schedulability bound: U = ОЈ Cбөў/Tбөў вүӨ nВ·(2^(1/n)вҲ’1); also evaluates Bini-Buttazzo (2001) tighter hyperbolic bound О (Uбөў+1) вүӨ 2; verifies RM priority assignment (shorter period вҶ’ higher priority integer, FreeRTOS/Zephyr/ChibiOS convention); depth-bar: 2 tasks T1 period=10ms WCET=4ms (P2), T2 period=20ms WCET=8ms (P1) вҶ’ U=80%, bound=82.84%, schedulable, assignment correct; overload detection with recommendation to reduce WCET or lengthen periods; high-utilisation (>90%) headroom warning; largest contributor advisory; `RtosTaskSpec` + `RtosPriorityReport` dataclasses; `check_rtos_priorities` function; `firmware_check_rtos_priorities` LLM tool; `rtos_priority_check.py`; 43 tests. HONEST: sufficient condition only for independent periodic tasks вҖ” does NOT model shared resources (PCP/PIP, requires Sha-Rajkumar-Lehoczky 1990 blocking-time response-time analysis), aperiodic/sporadic tasks (Deferrable/Sporadic Server algorithms), interrupt latency, context-switch overhead, or deadlines вү  periods (use EDF/DM for Dбөў вү  Tбөў). Refs: Liu-Layland (1973) J. ACM 20(1); Bini-Buttazzo (2001) ECRTS; ARM FreeRTOS Kernel Developer Docs; Renesas R01AN5545; Zephyr Scheduling Docs.
- **FIRMWARE-CRC-COMPUTE** вң… вҖ” table-driven CRC checksum engine for embedded protocol verification; 5 algorithms: CRC-8 (poly 0x07, init 0x00), CRC-16/CCITT-FALSE (poly 0x1021, init 0xFFFF, no reflection вҖ” ITU-T V.41), CRC-16/MODBUS (reflected poly 0xA001, init 0xFFFF вҖ” Modbus RTU spec В§2.5.1), CRC-32/ISO-HDLC (reflected poly 0xEDB88320, init 0xFFFFFFFF, XOR-out 0xFFFFFFFF вҖ” IEEE 802.3 Ethernet FCS), CRC-32C/Castagnoli (reflected poly 0x82F63B78, init 0xFFFFFFFF, XOR-out 0xFFFFFFFF вҖ” iSCSI RFC 3720 / SCTP RFC 4960); official check-vector "123456789" verified: CRC-16/CCITT=0x29B1, CRC-32=0xCBF43926, CRC-32C=0xE3069283; returns crc_hex + crc_int + crc_binary (zero-padded bit-string) + polynomial_hex + honest_caveat; `CRCSpec` + `CRCResult` dataclasses; `compute_crc` function; `firmware_compute_crc` LLM tool; `crc_compute.py`; 66 tests. HONEST: 5 standard algorithms only вҖ” CRC-64 (ECMA-182, XZ), CRC-16/CCITT-TRUE (init=0), CRC-32/BZIP2 (big-endian), CRC-32/JAMCRC (no output XOR), and bitwise-reflection variants require a separate tool; Modbus CRC register value uses Williams LSB-first convention (low byte transmitted first on wire). Refs: Koopman (2002) FTCS-32; Koopman & Chakravarty (2004) DSN; ITU-T V.41; IEEE 802.3-2018 В§3.2.8; IETF RFC 3720 В§B.4; Williams (1993) "A Painless Guide to CRC Error Detection Algorithms."
- **FIRMWARE-PWM-RESOLUTION** вң… вҖ” MCU PWM resolution and frequency-error analyser; given timer clock (Hz), desired PWM frequency (Hz), and counter bit-width (8/10/16/32), searches integer prescaler P вҲҲ [1..65536] to find (P, ARR) that maximises achievable resolution_bits = log2(ARR+1) while keeping |freq_error| < 1%; algorithm: ARR = round(clock/(PГ—freq)вҲ’1) clamped to [1, 2^bitsвҲ’1]; f_actual = clock/(PГ—(ARR+1)); freq_error_pct = (actualвҲ’target)/targetГ—100; oracle: 16 MHz / 1 kHz / 16-bit вҶ’ P=1, ARR=15999, 13.97 bits; 16 MHz / 20 kHz / 16-bit вҶ’ P=1, ARR=799, 9.64 bits; STM32F411 100 MHz / 20 kHz / 16-bit вҶ’ P=1, ARR=4999, 12.29 bits; 100 MHz / 50 Hz / 32-bit вҶ’ >20 bits; `PWMConfigSpec` + `PWMResolutionReport` dataclasses; `check_pwm_resolution` function; `firmware_check_pwm_resolution` LLM tool; `pwm_resolution_check.py`; 25 tests. HONEST: integer-prescaler model is exact for STM32F411 (PSC вҲҲ [0..65535], RM0383 В§13) вҖ” ATmega328P Timer1 prescaler is discrete {1,8,64,256,1024} (В§15), so only those 5 values are legal on ATmega; interrupt latency, dead-time insertion (TIM1/TIM8 BDTR), complementary PWM, and centre-aligned ARR alignment constraints NOT modelled. Refs: STM32F411 RM0383 В§13 (TIM2вҖ“TIM5); ATmega328P В§15 (Timer/Counter1 Fast PWM, ICR1 mode).
- **FIRMWARE-ADC-EFFECTIVE-BITS** вң… вҖ” ADC Effective Number of Bits (ENOB) calculator with oversampling improvement; base ENOB from SINAD: ENOB = (SINAD_dB вҲ’ 1.76) / 6.02 (ADI MT-003 Rev. B Eq. 1); or from directly-specified datasheet ENOB; oversampling gain: ENOB_after = ENOB + log2(OSR)/2 (TI SBAA221 В§2.1 вҖ” each 4Г— OSR adds 1 bit via вҲҡOSR noise reduction); voltage resolution: signal_full_scale_V / 2^ENOB_after; recommended OSR for target bits: 4^(target вҲ’ ENOB) rounded up to next power-of-4; SNR estimate: 6.02 Г— ENOB_after + 1.76 (inverse ADI MT-003); depth-bars: SINAD=68 dB вҶ’ ENOB = (68вҲ’1.76)/6.02 вүҲ 11.00 bits; OSR=16 вҶ’ gain=2.0 bits вҶ’ 13.00 bits; target 14 bits from ENOB 11 вҶ’ recommend OSR=64; `ADCSpec` + `OversamplingSpec` + `ADCEffectiveBitsReport` dataclasses; `compute_adc_enob` function; `firmware_compute_adc_enob` LLM tool; `adc_effective_bits.py`; 58 tests. HONEST: oversampling gain assumes white (uncorrelated) noise ONLY вҖ” correlated noise sources (50/60 Hz mains hum, PSU switching ripple, reference noise, quantisation plateaux on slowly-varying DC signals) DO NOT average out; real-world improvement is typically 0.5вҖ“1.5 bits per decade of OSR, not the full theoretical log2(OSR)/2; thermal (kT/C) noise of the sample-and-hold capacitor sets an absolute floor; dither injection (low-level white noise added before the ADC) can partially recover theoretical gain by breaking quantisation plateaux. Refs: ADI MT-003 Rev. B; TI SBAA221; Maxim AN2861.
- **FIRMWARE-CONST-ALLOCATION** вң… вҖ” Flash (.rodata, .text) vs RAM (.data initialised constants) allocation analyser for tight MCUs (STM32F411, ATmega328P); input: GCC linker-map symbol list (name, section, size_bytes); Flash sections: .text + .rodata + .init_array + .ARM.exidx; RAM sections: .data + .bss; key metrics: rodata_bytes (Flash constants вҖ” correct placement), data_init_bytes (RAM-stored constants вҖ” wasteful, both Flash LMA + RAM VMA consumed); suspect_data_consts: top-10 .data symbols matching ALL_CAPS naming convention (^_*[A-Z][A-Z0-9_]*$) and >= 4 bytes, sorted by size вҖ” heuristic for likely-constant arrays misplaced in RAM; top_rodata_consumers: top-10 .rodata symbols by size; flash_utilization_pct + ram_utilization_pct; recommendations: data_init_bytes > 1 KB вҶ’ "move large const arrays from RAM to flash via const-qualifier / section attribute"; flash > 80% вҶ’ "enable -Os"; depth-bar: STM32F411 (512 KB Flash / 128 KB RAM) LOOKUP_TABLE 2 KB in .data вҶ’ suspect flagged + const-migration recommendation; 4 KB .rodata on 4 KiB MCU вҶ’ -Os triggered; `SymbolEntry` + `ConstAllocationReport` dataclasses; `analyze_const_allocation` function; `firmware_analyze_const_allocation` LLM tool; `const_allocation.py`; 41 tests. HONEST: HEURISTIC ANALYSIS ONLY вҖ” detection based on ELF section placement and ALL_CAPS naming convention, NOT on C/C++ source AST or DWARF type info; a mutable global named 'MAX_SPEED' will be flagged; a const array named 'lookup' will not; .data LMA Flash cost is not separately reported from the symbol map; ARM Thumb literal pools in .text are not included in rodata_bytes. Refs: GCC Internals В§18; ARM IHI 0044F AAPCS В§5.4; RM0383 Rev 3 В§3 (STM32F411 512 KB Flash / 128 KB SRAM); ATmega328P В§8 (SRAM) + В§28 (Flash).
- **FIRMWARE-WATCHDOG-CHECK** вң… вҖ” firmware watchdog-kick gap analyser; given a task schedule (list of FirmwareTask with period_ms, wcet_ms, priority, kicks_watchdog) and a WatchdogSpec (IWDG or WWDG, timeout_ms, optional window_min_ms), verifies that the independent watchdog is kicked frequently enough across ALL execution paths to never time out вҖ” even under worst-case latency; algorithm: (1) find slowest kicker (max period), (2) add WCET of all higher-priority non-kicker tasks (blocking time), (3) max_gap = slowest_kicker.period_ms + blocking_time_ms, (4) is_safe = max_gap < timeout_ms; WWDG: also flags kicks earlier than window_min_ms (early-kick reset risk, RM0383 В§20); depth-bar: kicker period=100 ms + blocker WCET=0 ms vs IWDG 250 ms вҶ’ max_gap=100 ms, margin=150 ms, safe; kicker period=1000 ms vs IWDG 500 ms вҶ’ violated; WWDG kick=50 ms in window 60вҖ“100 ms вҶ’ window violation; `FirmwareTask` + `WatchdogSpec` + `WatchdogCheckReport` dataclasses; `check_watchdog` function; `firmware_check_watchdog` LLM tool; `watchdog_check.py`; 29 tests. HONEST: STATIC SCHEDULE ONLY вҖ” no IRQ latency, DMA burst, or scheduling-jitter model; assumes ideal fixed-priority preemptive scheduler; shared-resource blocking (PCP/PIP) NOT modelled; WWDG window-minimum uses kicker period as proxy вҖ” verify on hardware with logic analyser; IEC 61508 SIL-2+ requires challenge-response watchdog in addition to this check. Refs: STM32F4 RM0383 В§19 (IWDG), В§20 (WWDG); IEC 61508:2010 Part 2 В§7.4.3.7; ARM Keil AN259.

### Aerospace / composites

- **Applied aerodynamics** вң… вҖ” ISA atmosphere, VLM/thin-airfoil, flight mechanics, propulsion, Breguet range/endurance; 6-DOF; orbital mechanics (Kepler/Lambert/Hohmann); rocket propulsion (CEA-lite); ADCS (quaternion + reaction wheels + magnetorquers); spacecraft thermal network.
- **Composites (CLT)** вң… вҖ” ABD matrix, per-ply stress/strain, Tsai-Wu/max-stress/Hashin failure indices, first-ply-failure, laminate moduli.
- **Composites manufacturing UI** вң… вҖ” `LaminateStackup` (drag-to-reorder ply table, balance/symmetry check, areal-weight + cost rollup, CLT stiffness matrix preview); `AFPToolpathView` (AFP 2D tape-path canvas, cure cycle plot, path-plan dispatch, **Export CNC dropdown вҶ’ G-code / APT**); `FiberOrientationContour` (HSL contour heatmap, angle tooltip, exploded ply stack, drape sim dispatch). File kinds: `.layup` / `.afp_plan` / `.fiber_map`. Backend routes: `POST /api/composites/clt`, `POST /api/composites/afp` (+ `?format=gcode|apt`), `POST /api/composites/fiber_map`; auth-gated. **AFP CNC export вң…** вҖ” `afp_export.py` (`afp_to_gcode` 5-axis G-code with M200/M201/M202/M203/M204/M205 fibre M-codes; `afp_to_apt` APT/CL ISO 3592 GOTO/FEDRAT/AUXFUN); `composites_afp_export` LLM tool; Fibersim + VeriFiber AFP rows вҶ’ yes; 79 tests green.
- **Layup angle optimizer (Tsai-Hahn 1980 + Daniel-Ishai 2006)** вң… вҖ” minimize weight subject to Tsai-Wu FPF margin constraint; simulated-annealing search over discrete angles; symmetric + balanced constraint enforced.
- **Aeroelasticity** вң… вҖ” flutter boundary (Theodorsen + p-k method), doublet-lattice.

| GK-P20 | **UV-unwrap hardening вҖ” seam-cut + chart pack + distortion stats** вҖ” post-processes raw LSCM/ARAP UV layouts: cuts the mesh at marked seam edges into connected UV islands (charts) via BFS face-adjacency flood-fill; translates each chart bbox to origin; tries 0В°/90В°/180В°/270В° rotations to minimise bbox area; shelf-first-fit bin-packs charts into a unit square; reports per-chart and global angle/area distortion (Sander et al. 2003 Multi-Chart В§3 + LГ©vy et al. 2002 LSCM В§5). Dataclasses: `UVUnwrapHardeningSpec` (mesh_vertices_xyz, mesh_faces, initial_uv, seam_edges), `UVChart` (face_indices, uv_min, uv_max, chart_area_uv, chart_area_3d_mm2, scale_factor), `HardenedUVResult` (packed_uv per-corner indexed face*3+k, charts, num_charts, num_seam_cuts, packing_efficiency, max_distortion, mean_distortion, honest_caveat); `harden_uv_unwrap(spec)` entry point; `nurbs_harden_uv_unwrap` LLM tool wired via gated import; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py`. 21 hermetic tests. HONEST CAVEATS: shelf packing only (not optimal guillotine / VLSI); rotation at 90В° increments only (no fractional-angle SAT minimisation); distortion = per-face Jacobian residual (sampling-based lower bound, NOT continuous LSCM energy). Refs: P. Sander, S. Gortler, J. Snyder, H. Hoppe вҖ” "Multi-Chart Geometry Images", SGP 2003; B. LГ©vy, S. Petitjean, N. Ray, J. Maillot вҖ” "Least Squares Conformal Maps for Automatic Texture Atlas Generation", SIGGRAPH 2002; Kenyon (1996) shelf-first-fit; Sleator (1980) shelf algorithm. | Blender UV Unwrap / RizomUV | вң… shipped вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/uv_unwrap_hardening.py` |
| GK-P21 | **Displacement layer stack вҖ” multi-layer ordered displacement maps** вҖ” `DisplacementLayer` (name, displacement_values, mode add/subtract/multiply/replace, mask, strength, enabled) + `DisplacementStackSpec` (base_vertices_xyz, base_normals_xyz, layers) + `DisplacementStackResult` (output_vertices_xyz, layer_contributions, num_layers_applied, max_displacement_mm, mean_displacement_mm, honest_caveat); `apply_displacement_stack(spec)` accumulates d_total per-vertex across layers in order; final P' = P + d_totalВ·NМӮ; `mesh_apply_displacement_stack` LLM tool wired via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py`. Refs: Pixologic ZBrush Docs 2024 (layer blend modes); Aumann-McNamara (2009) Layered Displacement Maps (SIGGRAPH course notes); Lee-Moreton-Hoppe 2000 Displaced Subdivision Surfaces (SIGGRAPH 2000). HONEST CAVEATS: per-vertex displacement only вҖ” no fractional indexing across face barycentric coordinates; caller must supply unit-length normals (not renormalised); multiply on zero accumulator yields zero вҖ” prepend add/replace layer first; pure-Python O(VГ—L) loop. 23 hermetic tests. | ZBrush layer stack / Mudbox layer displacement | вң… shipped вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/mesh_displacement_stack.py` |
| GK-P22 | **Sculpt brushes for SubD cages + triangle meshes** вҖ” 4 brushes: Inflate (along vertex normal), Crease (inverted inflate / pull inward), Smooth (one-ring centroid relaxation), Pinch (attract to stroke centre); Wendland C2 falloff kernel w(t)=(1-tВІ)ВІ (Wendland 1995); auto-normals via area-weighted one-ring averaging; `SculptStroke` + `MeshSculptResult` dataclasses; `apply_sculpt_brush` core API; `mesh_sculpt_brush` LLM tool wired. Refs: Botsch-Sorkine 2008 В§3; Sculptris/ZBrush brush math (Pixologic 2024). Honest (v1): single-stroke stateless вҖ” no undo stack, no stroke history, no dyntopo; smooth = unweighted first-order centroid only (no cotangent Taubin); crease = mesh-level inward inflate (not CC subdivision sharpness propagation); 35 tests. | Blender Sculpt / ZBrush | вң… shipped вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/mesh_sculpt_brushes.py` |
| G-5 | **Kernel G3 / class-A leading** вҖ” wired G3 blends + curvature-comb + imprint | Alias / ICEM Surf | рҹҡ§ in flight |
| G-6 | **SubD authoring with creases + edit workflow** | Rhino 8 SubD | вң… shipped вҖ” cage creation/extrude/bevel/loop-cut/slide/crease/bevel-weight + Catmull-Clark evaluation вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_authoring.py`; SubD boundaryвҶ’curve snap вң… вҖ” `geom/subd_boundary_replace.py` |
| G-6b | **SubD mirror symmetry detect + enforce** | Rhino 8 / Maya / Blender SubD symmetry | вң… shipped вҖ” `detect_mirror_symmetry` (score-based, Podolak 2006), `enforce_mirror_symmetry`, `mirror_edit`; 2 LLM tools (`subd_detect_symmetry`, `subd_enforce_symmetry`) вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_symmetry.py` |
| GK-P | **Per-face SubD variation** (subdivision scheme + crease + features per face) | вҖ” | вң… shipped вҖ” `FaceVariation` dataclass + `apply_face_variations` (CC / Loop / Mod-Butterfly / Doo-Sabin per face, G0 at boundaries) + `extract_face_variation_map` round-trip + `subd_apply_face_variations` LLM tool вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_face_variation.py` |
| G-5 | **Kernel G3 / class-A leading** вҖ” wired G3 blends + curvature-comb + imprint | Alias / ICEM Surf | рҹҡ§ in flight |
| G-6 | **SubD authoring with creases + edit workflow** | Rhino 8 SubD | вң… shipped вҖ” cage creation/extrude/bevel/loop-cut/slide/crease/bevel-weight + Catmull-Clark evaluation вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_authoring.py`; **dense-meshвҶ’cage**: QEM (Garland-Heckbert 1997) + quad recovery (Bommes 2013) вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_decimate_to_cage.py`; **cageвҶ’primitive snap**: analytic closest-point projection onto sphere / cylinder / plane (`project_cage_to_sphere`, `project_cage_to_cylinder`, `project_cage_to_plane`; `ProjectionReport`; 3 LLM tools) вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_project_primitive.py` |
| G-6b | **SUBD-SYMMETRY-DETECT: mirror + rotational + spherical symmetry detection** | Rhino 8 SubD / Blender | вң… shipped вҖ” PCA-based mirror planes (Podolak 2006), n-fold rotational axes (Mitra-Guibas-Pauly 2006), spherical flag; `detect_symmetry(cage) -> SymmetryReport`; continuous-symmetry honest-flag via eigenvalue equality; `subd_detect_symmetry` + `subd_enforce_symmetry` LLM tools; 39 oracle tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/subd_symmetry.py`, `subd_symmetry_tools.py` |
| G-7 | **Render: caustics + dispersion** вҖ” in-browser path-tracer + Blender Cycles spectral | Cycles / V-Ray / KeyShot | рҹ”ҙ not started вҖ” Cycles translator stashes Sellmeier/Abbe coefficients for downstream use but no caustic solver is wired; in-browser path-tracer not started |
| G-8 | **Direct + parametric history coexistence** | Fusion / Inventor / Onshape | вң… shipped вҖ” history mode (direct edit promoted to DAG feature node, replays on upstream changes) + in-place mode; 30+ tests вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/direct_edit.py`, `geom/history/direct_edit.py` |
| G-9 | **Full joint system** вҖ” rigid/revolute/slider/cam/gear/pin-slot | Inventor / SolidWorks | вң… shipped вҖ” all six joint types with analytic kinematics and drive support вҖ” `kerf-mates/joints.py` |
| G-10 | **BIM parametric family authoring UX** | Revit | вң… shipped вҖ” `FamilyTemplate` schema + expression evaluator + cycle detection + `generate_body` вҖ” `kerf-bim/family_authoring.py` |

| G-15 | **BIM site / earthwork (toposolids)** | Revit / Civil 3D | вң… shipped вҖ” toposolid B-rep grading + IFC site export вҖ” `kerf-bim/tools/site_geometry.py`, `kerf-bim/site_ifc.py` |
| G-16 | **BIM material catalogue with render appearance** | Revit / Enscape | вң… shipped вҖ” 40+ materials with PBR properties (`base_color`, `metallic`, `roughness`, `ior`, `transmission`) wired to Cycles translator вҖ” `kerf-bim/material_catalogue.py` |

### Long-tail verticals

Everything committed, lowest priority. Ordered roughly by near-term readiness.

**Mechanical / product:** cams generators В· woodworking / furniture / joinery + cutlist В· power one-line / switchgear В· lighting / photometric В· interior / space-planning / FF&E *(IFC 4 export (ISO 16739-1:2018) вң… вҖ” subset export, NOT buildingSMART certified; `kerf-interior/ifc_export.py`)* В· kitchen / bath / cabinetry / millwork В· landscape В· scaffolding / formwork.

| Woodworking | Capability | Status |
|---|---|---|
| Joinery geometry validator (Hammer-Krenov) | Validate dovetail (7В°вҖ“14В° pin angle, вүҘ1/3 board pin width, вүҘ2 pins), mortise-and-tenon (1/3-rule, cheek check, tenon length), box joint (вүҘ3 fingers, equal widths, depth==thickness), finger joint (angle 15Вұ3В°); strength estimate via FPL Wood Handbook shear values Г— joint efficiency for oak/pine/cherry/maple/walnut in kN; `woodworking_validate_joinery` + `woodworking_joinery_strength` LLM tools | вң… shipped вҖ” `kerf-woodworking/joinery_validate.py` |
**Mechanical / product:** cams generators В· woodworking / furniture / joinery + cutlist В· power one-line / switchgear В· lighting / photometric В· interior / space-planning / FF&E В· kitchen / bath / cabinetry / millwork В· landscape (plant catalog with USDA + Dirr references, 101 species вң…) В· scaffolding / formwork.

**Vehicles:** composites ply/layup authoring (draping / fiber-steering / Fibersim class) В· hull fairing (NURBS-reachable) В· 3D harness routing.

**Civil / infrastructure (distinct engines):** plan-and-profile sheet engine В· IFC-4.3-infra I/O В· bridge/tunnel В· mining В· marine/dredging В· rail signaling. *(CRS engine, horizontal/vertical alignment, corridor, earthworks, geotechnical, LandXML 1.2 I/O, pressurized water-distribution networks (Todini GGA + Hazen-Williams/Darcy-Weisbach), gravity sewer (Manning), storm rational method + HDS-5 culverts already shipped; TINView / PipeNetworkView / GradingPlanView / LandscapeView UIs вң… 2026-05-29.)*

**Body-worn / medical / craft:** watchmaking / horology В· eyewear / frames В· footwear / last design В· dental CAD (crowns/aligners) В· orthopedic / prosthetics В· hearing aids.

**Soft goods (distinct 2D/developable engine):** apparel / pattern-making + drape В· technical textiles / sails / membrane / tensile В· upholstery / leather. *(ARAP/LSCM pattern flattening for non-developable surfaces (Bo-Wang 2007 / LГ©vy 2002) вң… вҖ” `kerf-apparel/pattern_flatten.py`, `apparel_flatten_pattern` LLM tool wired.)*
**Soft goods (distinct 2D/developable engine):** apparel / pattern-making + drape В· technical textiles / sails / membrane / tensile В· upholstery / leather. *(ASTM D5219 + ISO 8559 grading rules вң… вҖ” `GradingRule`, `build_grading_table`, `apply_grading`, `grade_check_iso_8559` shipped; `apparel_apply_grading` + `apparel_grade_check` LLM tools registered вҖ” `packages/kerf-apparel/src/kerf_apparel/grading.py`.)*

**Scientific / niche:** microfluidics / MEMS В· signage / large-format.

**Silicon next:** verification depth + post-silicon (cocotb testbench harness, power analysis, STA, clock-tree synthesis, formal equivalence, Tiny Tapeout / Efabless harnesses). T-249..T-258.

**Firmware next:** RTOS primitives, OTA, RTOS-aware debugger, power profiling, pin-map cross-check vs PCB, USB-class drivers. T-259..T-265. **T-274 вң…** вҖ” Build / Flash / Monitor UI wired: `FirmwareProjectPanel`, `BuildOutput`, `SerialMonitor` in `src/components/firmware/`; `firmware_project` kind renders in Editor; PlatformIO + Arduino IDE compare rows added.

**Aerospace next:** XFOIL-class viscous solver, aircraft conceptual sizing (Raymer/Roskam), stability derivatives, aero-acoustics (FW-H), heat-shield/ablation, aerospace fasteners. T-266..T-272.

**Platform (demand-gated post-launch):** fully-local / offline / no-account desktop app вҖ” committed but not a launch pillar. Portability + two-way sync + easy self-host is the launch answer.

### Strategic AI-native capabilities

These are roadmap-level moats that span every sector simultaneously and compound leverage instead of adding it linearly.
