## Genuinely outstanding

*Last verified: 2026-05-26 (status verify-pass against live codebase).* Items that are actually `рҹ”ҙ not started` or meaningfully incomplete after the pass above.

### Tractable soon (weeks, well-scoped)

- **G-7 caustics + in-browser path-tracer** вҖ” Cycles spectral dispersion data (Sellmeier/Abbe) is stashed by the translator but no caustic solver is wired; in-browser WebGPU path-tracer not started.
- ~~**P0-7 bulk import endpoint**~~ вҖ” вң… shipped `POST /api/projects/import` (ZIP archive upload; path-traversal guard + size/count caps + extвҶ’kind mapping).
- **P0-5 viewport integration** вҖ” LOD planner and lazy-load ordering are implemented in `assembly/perf.py` but not yet wired to the 3D viewport renderer.
- **P0-7 bulk import endpoint** вҖ” `POST /api/projects/import` (ZIP archive upload); workaround (file-by-file) exists; bulk path not yet implemented.
- **P0-5 real-part catalogue** вҖ” LOD planner heuristics use synthetic triangle / bbox estimates; wiring to real tessellated part geometry (via `mesh_url` pre-baked buffers) would sharpen tier boundaries for production DMU use.

### Multi-month epics

- **GK-P foundational kernel** вҖ” general solid boolean for NURBS-faced bodies; Stam limit-tangents вң… + G1 at extraordinary SubD points; fractional creases; MatchSrf G3; analytic surface derivatives.
- **GK-P foundational kernel** вҖ” вң… general solid boolean shipped (GK-P-A); remaining: Stam limit-tangents + G1 at extraordinary SubD points; fractional creases; MatchSrf G3; analytic surface derivatives.
- **GK-P Bezier extraction** вң… вҖ” B-spline вҶ’ multi-Bezier patch decomposition (Piegl & Tiller В§5.6); foundational for FEA tet-mesh handoff, GPU-friendly rendering, IGES export. (`bezier_extract.py`, LLM tool `bezier_extract` registered.)
- **NURBS-CONVERT-TO-IGES-144** вң… вҖ” full IGES 5.3 В§4.27 entity-144 (Trimmed Parametric Surface) writer + reader: `write_iges_trimmed_surface(srf, outer_loop, inner_loops) -> bytes` serialises entity 128 (В§4.26 NURBS surface) wrapped by entity 142 (В§4.23 Curve on Parametric Surface) outer + optional inner (hole) loops, each referencing entity-126 (В§4.22) UV-space B-spline curves. `read_iges_trimmed_surface` returns `TrimmedSurfaceRecord` with `outer_loop`, `inner_loops`, `has_3d_outer/inner` flags and `form` (Form 0). Field-count oracle verified against В§4.27 Table 1 (4 + N2 fields). Hausdorff round-trip oracle вүӨ 1e-6 for trimmed plane + circular-hole case. LLM tool `nurbs_export_iges_144` registered (`geom/io/iges_144_tool.py`); 32 tests green.
- **GK-P reparametrisation** вҖ” Reparametrization (chord-length + centripetal + Foley-Nielsen) вң… вҖ” `geom/reparam.py`; `fit_curve`/`fit_surface` accept `parameterisation` kwarg; LLM tool `nurbs_reparametrize` registered (Piegl-Tiller В§9.2.2).
- **GK-P non-manifold detection + repair** вң… вҖ” `detect_non_manifold` / `repair_non_manifold` for B-rep bodies (T-junction edges, touching-cone vertices, self-intersecting loops) and mesh equivalents; `brep_non_manifold_check` + `brep_non_manifold_repair` LLM tools; `heal_body(repair_non_manifold=True)` integration. (Weiler 1985 / Sheffer-Hart 2002.)
- **GK-P curve lifting** вҖ” Curve lifting (2D-loop вҶ’ 3D-on-surface + inverse) вң… вҖ” `geom/curve_lifting.py`: `lift_curve_to_surface`, `lift_curve_with_arc_length`, `project_3d_curve_to_surface_uv`; LLM tool `nurbs_curve_lift_to_surface`; 14 analytic-oracle tests (P&T В§10.3.1).
- **GK-P shell-offset operator** вң… вҖ” shell-offset operator (constant thickness + fillet propagation): `shell_offset_body`, `detect_shell_self_intersection`, `shell_with_open_face`; `brep_shell_body` LLM tool; 47 tests green.
- **GK-P curvature heatmap export** вң… вҖ” `render_curvature_heatmap` / `export_heatmap_png` / `export_heatmap_svg` / `generate_curvature_legend`; viridis + diverging_blue_red palettes; pure-Python PNG encoder (IHDR+IDAT+IEND, no Pillow); 2 LLM tools (`nurbs_export_curvature_png`, `nurbs_export_curvature_svg`) registered вҖ” `geom/curvature_heatmap.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-CURVATURE-PROFILE-EXPORT** вң… вҖ” Оә(t) sampled along a NurbsCurve at configurable resolution; exports (1) CSV (t, Оә, arc_length, x, y, z, high_kappa_risk), (2) SVG plot of Оә vs arc-length (inflection markers, high-risk bands), (3) PNG plot (pure-Python encoder, no Pillow); `CurvatureProfileResult` dataclass; `export_curvature_profile` / `export_curvature_profile_result`; LLM tool `nurbs_export_curvature_profile` registered; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; honest-flag `high_kappa_risk` per sample where |dОә/dt| > 5Г— mean; **adaptive curvature-weighted sampling** вң… вҖ” `export_curvature_profile_csv(curve, num_samples, adaptive=True, output_path)` implements de Boor В§VI / Hoschek-Lasser В§5 curvature-weighted resampling: seed NГ—10 uniform samples вҶ’ compute w(t)=|Оә(t)|В·вҖ–C'(t)вҖ– вҶ’ integrate W(t) cumulatively (trapz) вҶ’ invert at equal-spaced W targets вҶ’ dense samples in high-Оә regions; straight-line (ОәвүЎ0) falls back to arc-length uniform; CSV WARNING header suppressed when adaptive=True; 43 hermetic tests (35 original + 8 adaptive: straight-line uniform fallback, kappa-zero on line, denser corner samples, S-curve non-uniform t-spacing, exact count preservation, circle accuracy, no-WARNING header, adaptive max error < uniform) вҖ” Farin В§11.6, Sapidis В§3, de Boor В§VI, Hoschek-Lasser В§5 вҖ” `geom/curvature_profile_export.py`.
- **GK-P17 SHEET-METAL-FLAT-PATTERN** вң… вҖ” `compute_flat_pattern(part: SheetMetalPart) вҶ’ FlatPatternResult`; parametric sheet-metal flanges, bends, and unfold-to-flat-pattern with K-factor interpolation from r/t per DIN 6935 / Suchy "Handbook of Die Design" В§3 / ANSI Y14.5M. `SheetMetalPart` dataclass: `material` (steel-cold-rolled|stainless-304|aluminum-5052|copper + aliases), `thickness_mm`, `length_mm`, `width_mm`, `bend_radius_mm`, `bend_angle_deg`, `flange_lengths_mm` (ordered straight segments; bends = lenвҲ’1). `FlatPatternResult`: `flat_length_mm`, `flat_width_mm`, `bend_allowances_mm` (per-bend BA list), `k_factor`, `total_bend_deduction_mm`, `num_bends`, `honest_caveat`. K-factor interpolation: r/t < 1 вҶ’ K = k_min (0.33 steel / 0.31 SS / 0.40 Al/Cu); r/t вүҘ 3 вҶ’ K = k_max (0.44 steel / 0.38 SS / 0.50 Al/Cu); 1 вүӨ r/t < 3 вҶ’ linear. BA = (ПҖВ·Оё/180)В·(r + KВ·t); OSSB = (r+t)В·tan(Оё/2); BD = 2В·OSSB вҲ’ BA; flat_length = ОЈflange_lengths вҲ’ ОЈBD. LLM tool `sheetmetal_compute_flat_pattern` registered via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py`. 33 hermetic tests (K-factor at r/t<1/1/2/3/>3; material alias resolution; single 90В° L-bracket KвүҲ0.385; BA formula oracle; flat-length formula oracle; flat-width passthrough; 180В° hem fold no-raise; stainless thicker bend K; stainless K < mild steel; U-channel 2 bends; U-channel flat-length formula; zero bends single panel; aluminum K_max; copper alias; unknown material / zero thickness / negative radius / angle>180 / empty flanges вҶ’ ValueError; dataclass field types; honest caveat content; re-export from __init__). HONEST CAVEATS: K-factor is empirical (tabulated DIN 6935 interpolation) вҖ” measured press-brake data should be used when available; bend-deduction formula assumes inside-set air-bend geometry; bottoming/coining process shifts the neutral axis (see sheet_metal_bend_table.py); spring-back NOT modelled вҖ” apply overbend to compensate (typically 1вҖ“3В° for mild steel per DIN 6935 В§4); multi-bend interaction for closely-spaced bends (< 4Г—t apart) not captured; flat_width_mm passed through unchanged (no notch/relief geometry modelled). Refs: Suchy "Handbook of Die Design" В§3; DIN 6935:1990; ANSI Y14.5M-2018 вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/sheetmetal_features.py`.
- **GK-P16 NURBS-LOFT-WITH-GUIDE-RAILS** вң… вҖ” `loft_with_guide_rails(spec: GuideRailLoftSpec) вҶ’ GuideRailLoftReport`; skinning loft through cross-section curves while following N guide rail curves that constrain the surface's intermediate shape (Rhino/Fusion 360 guide-rail loft pattern). `GuideRailLoftSpec`: `cross_section_curves` (вүҘ 2 NurbsCurves), `guide_rail_curves` (вүҘ 1), `num_v_samples` (default 20), `degree_v` (default 3), `closed_v` вң…. `GuideRailLoftReport`: `loft_surface` (NurbsSurface), `num_cross_sections`, `num_guide_rails`, `max_guide_rail_deviation_mm`, `mean_guide_rail_deviation_mm`, `num_self_intersections`, `honest_caveat`. Algorithm: (1) sample v uniformly at `num_v_samples` stations; (2) interpolate cross-sections by lerp between bounding pair; (3) for each guide rail evaluate rail point at v, compute displacement from interpolated cross-section to guide; (4) blend displacement with Gaussian weight centred at the rail's U-parameter (Пғ = 1/(2В·n_rails)); (5) accumulate blended displacements; (6) fit interpolating NurbsSurface via row-then-column B-spline fitting (P&T В§9.4.5). **closed_v=True вң…** (P&T В§9.4.5 periodic skinning): samples num_v+1 stations with last==first, fits open surface on extended grid, clamps last degree_v CP columns to first degree_v columns (seam wrap), replaces knots_v with periodic open-uniform vector; warns if first/last cross-sections are not coincident (> 1e-3 mm). `_check_guide_endpoint_alignment` warns (UserWarning) when guide endpoints are > 0.5 mm from the first/last cross-section. LLM tool `nurbs_loft_with_guide_rails` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py`. 39 hermetic tests (all previous + torus/vase circle loop closed_v, periodic knot uniformity, seam CP wrap, mismatched seam warning, coincident seam no warn, vase shape, tilted ellipse loop). HONEST: **approximate** guide-rail constraint вҖ” Gaussian displacement blend, NOT an exact constrained-NURBS solver; `max_guide_rail_deviation_mm` and `mean_guide_rail_deviation_mm` are reported for QC; guide endpoints mismatched from cross-sections trigger UserWarning; exact isogeometric constrained fitting (P&T В§10.5) is out of scope. Refs: Piegl & Tiller В§10.3 (skinning) + В§10.4 (Gordon) + В§9.4.5 (periodic skinning); Rhino 8 guide-curve loft docs; Fusion 360 guide-rail loft help вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/loft_guide_rails.py`.
- **GK-P15 NURBS-SURFACE-ANALYTIC-DERIVATIVES** вң… вҖ” `compute_analytic_derivatives(surface, u, v) вҶ’ SurfaceDerivativeResult`; closed-form вҲӮS/вҲӮu, вҲӮS/вҲӮv, вҲӮВІS/вҲӮuВІ, вҲӮВІS/вҲӮuвҲӮv, вҲӮВІS/вҲӮvВІ via Piegl & Tiller Algorithm A3.6 (B-spline tensor-product derivative table) + rational quotient rule A4.4. `SurfaceDerivativeResult` dataclass: `dS_du`, `dS_dv`, `d2S_du2`, `d2S_dudv`, `d2S_dv2` (each a `tuple[float,float,float]`), `gauss_K` = (LNвҲ’MВІ)/(EGвҲ’FВІ), `mean_H` = (ENвҲ’2FM+GL)/(2(EGвҲ’FВІ)) (do Carmo В§3.2; Mortenson В§6.5), `honest_caveat`. `SSIHardenedMarcher` class: `march(surface_a, surface_b, seed_uv_a, seed_uv_b, step_mm=0.5, max_steps=1000)` вҖ” differential-geometry SSI marcher (Patrikalakis & Maekawa В§5) with bisection fallback when |nМӮ_AГ—nМӮ_B| < tangent_threshold (near-tangent robustness). LLM tool `nurbs_surface_derivatives_analytic` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py`. 19 hermetic tests (plane K=H=0, cylinder K=0/H=1/(2R), sphere K=1/RВІ/H=1/R, вҲӮВІS/вҲӮuВІ radially inward on cylinder, analytic vs Richardson FD < 1e-8 non-rational, analytic vs FD < 1e-6 rational cylinder, SSI two-cylinder Steinmetz curve, dataclass fields, rational/non-rational caveats, K=HВІ sphere identity, bilinear patch exact partials, parameter clamping, SSI cylinderГ—plane circle radius, near-tangent parallel-plane guard). HONEST: curvature NaN at degenerate points (poles, seams where |S_uГ—S_v| < 1e-12); rational NURBS uses the correct quotient rule (P&T A4.4) but may have large condition number for near-zero weights; SSI marcher traces one branch per seed вҖ” bifurcation points not handled; bisection fallback is O(stepВІ) accurate but uses more evaluations. Refs: Piegl & Tiller В§3.3 (A3.6/A4.4); Patrikalakis & Maekawa В§5; do Carmo В§3.2 вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/surface_analytic_derivatives.py`.
- **GK-P NURBS-DERIVATIVE-FIELD-VISUAL** вң… вҖ” 1st partial-derivative vector-field arrow-plot on NURBS surfaces: `render_derivative_field_png` / `render_derivative_field_svg`; real analytic derivatives at a u/v sample grid (default 12Г—12) via `surface_derivative`; two-colour encoding (red = вҲӮS/вҲӮu, blue = вҲӮS/вҲӮv); proper arrow scaling (longest arrow вүӨ cell size); pure-Python PNG encoder (IHDR+IDAT+IEND, no Pillow); 2 LLM tools (`nurbs_derivative_field_png`, `nurbs_derivative_field_svg`) registered; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 19 hermetic tests (flat-plane parallel, sphere tangent, PNG magic bytes, SVG structure, scale bound) вҖ” `geom/derivative_field_viz.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-FIT-G2** вң… вҖ” `fit_curve_g2(spec: G2FitSpec, degree=5) вҶ’ G2FitResult`; fit a degree-5 B-spline curve to a set of 3-D data points with G2 (curvature-continuous) end conditions. `G2FitSpec` dataclass: `data_points` (list of xyz), `start_tangent_xyz`, `start_curvature_xyz`, `end_tangent_xyz`, `end_curvature_xyz`. `G2FitResult`: `fitted_curve` (NurbsCurve), `max_residual_mm`, `mean_residual_mm`, `start_g2_residual`, `end_g2_residual`, `honest_caveat`. Algorithm (Piegl & Tiller В§9.4; Farin "CAGD" Ch 10): (1) chord-length parameterisation; (2) clamped knot vector via P&T В§9.2 averaging rule; (3) first three and last three control points fixed analytically from the G1/G2 endpoint formulas (P&T Eqs 9.26вҖ“9.29: C'(0)=pВ·(P_1вҲ’P_0)/Оҫ_{p+1}, C''(0)=p(p-1)В·[(P_2вҲ’P_1)/Оҫ_{p+2}вҲ’(P_1вҲ’P_0)/Оҫ_{p+1}]/Оҫ_{p+1}; symmetrically at t=1); (4) interior CPs solved by least-squares collocation. Degree вүҘ 2 required for G2; default degree=5. LLM tool `nurbs_fit_curve_g2` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 22 hermetic analytic-oracle tests (straight line residual < 1e-9, circle arc residual < 1e-6, G2 start/end constraints < 1e-9, G1 start/end constraints < 1e-9, 8-point freeform, 12-point 3D, degree-2/3/5, knot clamping, endpoint interpolation, residual non-negativity, residual field parity). HONEST: chord-length parameterisation used throughout вҖ” centripetal parameterisation (Lee 1989; Foley-Nielsen 1989) may give smaller oscillations for high-aspect-ratio data with large spacing variation and is NOT implemented here. Curvature vectors are *parametric* second derivatives C''(t), NOT the Frenet curvature Оә(s)В·nМӮ вҖ” for surface-blending use cases, pass the adjacent curve's C''(t) evaluated at the join parameter вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_fit_g2.py`. Refs: Piegl & Tiller В§9.4; Farin "CAGD" Ch 10; Lee (1989) CAD 21(6).
- **NURBS-SURFACE-SHEAR-OFFSET** вң… вҖ” `apply_shear_offset(surface, shear: ShearMatrix) вҶ’ SurfaceShearOffsetResult`; apply a global linear shear-transform (I+S) to all control points of a NurbsSurface: P'_x = x + s_xyВ·y + s_xzВ·z, P'_y = y + s_yxВ·x + s_yzВ·z, P'_z = z + s_zxВ·x + s_zyВ·y (Mortenson В§4.8; Piegl & Tiller В§6.1 Theorem 6.1). `ShearMatrix` dataclass: six off-diagonal shear coefficients (s_xy, s_xz, s_yx, s_yz, s_zx, s_zy; all default 0.0). `SurfaceShearOffsetResult`: sheared_surface, max_displacement_mm, mean_displacement_mm, honest_caveat. Knots and weights preserved exactly. LLM tool `nurbs_apply_surface_shear_offset` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 20 hermetic tests (identity unchanged, zero displacement, single-axis oracles for all 6 coefficients, combined superposition, knot/weight preservation, rational weight copy, max/mean displacement formulas, maxвүҘmean invariant, ValueError for non-3D CPs, ShearMatrix defaults, input not mutated, honest caveat content). HONEST: global linear shear only вҖ” non-uniform warp (thermal distortion, springback, gravity sag) requires per-point deformation field, not a single ShearMatrix; displacement stats are control-point displacements, not evaluated-surface deviations вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/surface_shear_offset.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-FOOTPRINT-ON-PLANE** вң… вҖ” `project_curve_to_plane(curve, plane_point, plane_normal) вҶ’ FootprintResult`; orthographic projection of a 3-D NurbsCurve onto an arbitrary plane, producing a planar 2-D NurbsCurve in plane-local UV coordinates. `FootprintResult` dataclass: `footprint_curve_2d`, `projection_axis`, `max_orig_depth`, `honest_caveat`. Each control point projected via P' = P вҲ’ ((PвҲ’O)В·nМӮ) nМӮ; degree, knot vector and weights preserved exactly (Piegl & Tiller В§6.1 Theorem 6.1). Degenerate flag when curve is perpendicular to the plane (footprint collapses to a point). `lift_footprint_to_3d` inverse helper. LLM tool `nurbs_curve_project_to_plane` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 17 hermetic analytic-oracle tests (helixвҶ’XY circle radius exact, already-planar identity, vertical-line degenerate, skewed-normal unit-axis, knot/weight/degree preservation, non-rational weights=None, max_orig_depth, projection-formula depth, 45В°-tilt analytic, make_circle_nurbs round-trip, lift round-trip, ValueError zero-normal, multi-turn helix, YZ-plane analytic). HONEST: orthographic (linear) projection only вҖ” no perspective; for rational NURBS the footprint is a correct rational NURBS but the Euclidean evaluated curve may differ from a naive point-by-point projection. Refs: Piegl & Tiller В§6.1; Mortenson В§4.4 вҖ” `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_footprint_on_plane.py`.

- **NURBS-NORMAL-CURVATURE-AT-POINT** вң… вҖ” normal curvature Оә_n = II(t,t)/I(t,t) via Meusnier's theorem (do Carmo В§3.2 / Mortenson В§10.4); `normal_curvature_at(srf, u, v, direction_uv) вҶ’ NormalCurvatureReport` (Оә_n, Оә_1, Оә_2, K, H, principal_dirs, is_umbilic, is_degenerate); principal curvatures from characteristic equation of shape operator; Euler's formula Оә_n(Оё)=Оә_1cosВІ(Оё-ПҶ)+Оә_2sinВІ(Оё-ПҶ) verified; umbilic honest-flag (Оә_1=Оә_2 вҶ’ principal_dirs=None); LLM tool `nurbs_normal_curvature_at_point` registered; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 32 hermetic analytic-oracle tests вҖ” sphere K=1/|Оә_n|=1 in 12 dirs, cylinder Оә_along=0/|Оә_across|=1/R/K=0, saddle K<0/mixed-sign principals, Euler formula bounded in all dirs вҖ” `geom/normal_curvature.py`.
- **NURBS-FAIR-COMPOSITE-CURVE** вң… вҖ” `composite_fair.py`: `fair_composite(curves, max_iter=50, lambda_smoothness=1.0)` вҖ” global curvature-variance fairing for poly-NURBS chains; minimises ОЈвҖ–DВІPвҖ–ВІ (discrete bending energy, Greiner-Hormann 1996 В§3.2) over all segments with per-iteration G1 seam re-imposition (Klass 1980 В§3 bisector) and hard-pinned global endpoints (вүӨ1e-6); honest `converged=False` flag for anti-parallel seams or stalled descent; returns `CompositeFairResult` (faired_curves, curvature_variance_before/after, iterations, converged, endpoint_error); `nurbs_fair_composite` LLM tool; 10 hermetic tests вҖ” 3-segment kink вүҘ50% variance reduction, smooth arc not degraded, endpoints within 1e-6.

- **GK-P50** вң… вҖ” NURBS surface optimal reparametrization: LSCM (angle-preserving, LГ©vy 2002) + ARAP (shape-preserving, Liu 2008); distortion metrics; `nurbs_reparametrize_optimal` LLM tool; 21 tests.
- **GK-P SubD / mesh** вҖ” multires displacement; SDF CSG + marching-cubes; sculpt brush engine; LSCM UV unwrap (module exists, wiring incomplete). **SubD automatic LOD chain + progressive mesh (Hoppe 1996) вң…** вҖ” `geom/subd_automatic_lod.py`; `subd_generate_lod_chain` LLM tool; cage = LOD 0, each CC step = next level, QEM progressive mesh, screen-space LOD picker.
- **GK-P SubD / mesh** вҖ” multires displacement; SDF CSG + marching-cubes; sculpt brush engine; LSCM UV unwrap (module exists, wiring incomplete); **SubD wire intersection + feature curve embedding вң…** (`geom/subd_wire_intersect.py` вҖ” `intersect_subd_with_wires`, `extract_wire_from_subd_intersection`, `embed_wire_as_feature_curve`; LLM tool `subd_intersect_wires` registered).
- **GK-P SubD / mesh** вҖ” multires displacement; SDF CSG + marching-cubes; sculpt brush engine; LSCM UV unwrap (module exists, wiring incomplete). NURBSвҶ”Mesh reconciliation with fidelity tracking (LГ©vy 2009) вң… вҖ” `geom/mesh_reconciliation.py`; two-sided Hausdorff deviation metric, extras detection, round-trip pipeline, feature-line-guided fit; LLM tools `brep_reconcile_nurbs_mesh` + `brep_round_trip_with_fidelity`.
- **GK-P SubD / mesh** вҖ” multires displacement; SDF CSG + marching-cubes; sculpt brush engine; LSCM UV unwrap (module exists, wiring incomplete); SubD cage derivation from dense mesh (Lee-Moreton-Hoppe 2000) вң….
- **GK-P SubD / mesh** вҖ” multires displacement; SDF CSG + marching-cubes; sculpt brush engine; LSCM UV unwrap (module exists, wiring incomplete). **SubD edge flow optimization (Bommes 2009) вң…** вҖ” `geom/subd_edge_flow.py`; `subd_optimize_edge_flow` LLM tool registered.

- **GK-P SubD / mesh** вҖ” multires displacement; SDF CSG + marching-cubes; sculpt brush engine; LSCM UV unwrap (module exists, wiring incomplete). OpenSubdiv-compatible SubD export (Pixar OSD 3.5) вң… вҖ” `subd_opensubdiv_export.py`; OBJ/JSON/binary formats + compatibility checker + subdivision pyramid. SubD USD export (USDA ASCII, catmullClark, creases) вң… вҖ” `subd_export_usd.py`; `export_subd_to_usda` + `parse_usda_subd` round-trip; LLM tool `subd_export_to_usd`; targets HdStorm/Houdini/Maya USD workflows; USDC binary out of scope. **SUBD-LIMIT-MESH-EXPORT-OBJ** вң… вҖ” `subd_export_obj.py`; `export_limit_to_obj(cage, levels=2, include_normals=True) -> str` + `parse_obj` round-trip; LLM tool `subd_export_limit_to_obj`; cube cage 2 levels вҶ’ 96 quads; face count scales 4Г— per level; bounding-box convergence verified. Geometry only вҖ” no MTL; vertex normals via area-weighted cross-product (not Stam exact eigenbasis); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`.
- **GK-P SubD / mesh** вҖ” multires displacement; SDF CSG + marching-cubes; sculpt brush engine; LSCM UV unwrap (module exists, wiring incomplete). **SUBD-EXPORT-PLY** вң… вҖ” `subd_export_ply.py`; `export_limit_to_ply(cage, levels=2, format="ascii") -> bytes` + `parse_ply` round-trip; LLM tool `subd_export_limit_to_ply`; ASCII and binary_little_endian; valid PLY header (ply, format, element vertex N, property float x/y/z, element face F, property list uchar int vertex_indices, end_header); cube cage 2 levels вҶ’ 96 faces; binary body compact vs ASCII; sphere cage bounding-box convergence. Honest (v1): geometry only вҖ” no colour, normals, texture coords; no big-endian; pure-Python struct module. 36 tests. Ref: Turk (1994) Stanford PLY spec. **SUBD-EXPORT-GLTF** вң… вҖ” `subd_export_gltf.py`; `export_limit_to_gltf(cage, levels=2, format="gltf") -> bytes` + `parse_gltf` round-trip; both `.gltf` (JSON + base64 buffer) and `.glb` (binary GLB container) formats; valid `asset.version="2.0"`; POSITION (VEC3 FLOAT) + SCALAR UNSIGNED_INT indices; quads fan-triangulated; GLB magic b"glTF" + version 2; cube cage 2 levels вҶ’ 192 triangles; vertex/face counts round-trip; sphere cage bounding-box convergence. Honest (v1): geometry only вҖ” no materials, normals attribute, textures, animations, skinning; no Draco compression; pure-Python (json + struct). 39 tests. LLM tool `subd_export_limit_to_gltf`. Ref: Khronos glTF 2.0 https://www.khronos.org/gltf/ **SUBD-EXPORT-STEP** вң… вҖ” `subd_export_step.py`; `export_limit_to_step(cage, levels=2) -> str` + `parse_step_subd` round-trip; valid ISO 10303-21 STEP AP242 ASCII file; FILE_DESCRIPTION + FILE_NAME + FILE_SCHEMA + DATA section; CARTESIAN_POINT / VERTEX_POINT / EDGE_CURVE / EDGE_LOOP / FACE_OUTER_BOUND / ADVANCED_FACE on PLANE surfaces / OPEN_SHELL / SHELL_BASED_SURFACE_MODEL / SHAPE_REPRESENTATION; minimal SI unit context (millimetres); cube cage 2 levels вҶ’ 96 ADVANCED_FACEs; face count scales 4Г— per level; sphere cage bounding-box convergence; structural validity verified (header + DATA + ENDSEC). Honest: faceted B-rep вҖ” each subdivided polygon is a flat PLANE face (STEP has no native SubD primitive); not smooth NURBS. Pure-Python. 38 tests. LLM tool `subd_export_limit_to_step`. Ref: ISO 10303-242:2020, ISO 10303-42:2022, ISO 10303-21:2016.
- **GK-P architectural geometry** вҖ” B-repвҶ’2D tessellate; roof/curtain-wall/corridor generators; wall compound-layer offset; hatch/section-fill.
- **GK-P sketcher** вҖ” collinear constraint; ellipse solver entity; G2 continuity. **Parametric sketch constraint solver (Sutherland 1963 / Hoffmann 2001) вң…** вҖ” Newton-Raphson DOF solver with Jacobian numerical differentiation, 10 constraint kinds (coincident/horizontal/vertical/parallel/perpendicular/tangent/distance/angle/equal/on_curve), `check_consistency` (over/under detection via rank), `drag_entity` interactive re-solve, 2 LLM tools (`nurbs_sketch_solver`, `nurbs_sketch_drag`) вҖ” `geom/sketch_solver.py`.
- **GK-P interop** вҖ” 3DM write with Hausdorff readвҶ’writeвҶ’read oracle.
- **T-100 FEM depth** вҖ” explicit dynamics вң… shipped (`kerf_fem/explicit_dynamics.py`); full nonlinear static (only 1-D bar/truss shipped); k-Оө turbulence CFD; coupled FEA-based variation analysis. (Acoustics FEM, EM, harmonic, buckling, PSD, multi-axial fatigue, explicit dynamics are now all shipped.)
- **T-100 FEM depth** вң… EPIC CLOSED вҖ” all sub-tasks shipped: explicit dynamics, full nonlinear static (geometric + material + contact + arc-length), k-Оө turbulence CFD, coupled-field probabilistic FEA (LHS + Karhunen-LoГЁve), plus acoustics FEM, EM, harmonic, buckling, PSD, multi-axial fatigue.
- **Composite curve G2 audit + upgrade** вң… вҖ” `composite_g2.py`: `audit_composite_g2` (per-joint G0/G1/G2 residuals), `upgrade_to_g2` (cubic Hermite / quintic Bezier blend insertion), `composite_curvature_profile` (Оә(s) statistics + jump detection); LLM tools `nurbs_composite_g2_audit` + `nurbs_composite_g2_upgrade` registered; 4 validation test classes (27 tests green).
- **GK-P rational conic detection** вң… вҖ” `detect_conic` / `extract_canonical_circle` / `simplify_curve`; Lee 1987 algebraic LS fit + Piegl-Tiller В§7.2 classification; returns `ConicInfo` (center, axes, radii, eccentricity, focus, plane_normal) for circle / ellipse / parabola / hyperbola; 2 LLM tools (`nurbs_detect_conic`, `nurbs_simplify_conic`); 24 hermetic analytic-oracle tests вҖ” `geom/conic_detect.py`.
- **GK-P NURBSвҶ”mesh max deviation** вҖ” NURBS surface вҶ” triangle mesh Hausdorff distance + per-region max + RMS (Aspert-Santa-Cruz-Ebrahimi 2002 / Cignoni-Rocchini-Scopigno 1998); critical for class-A reverse-engineering acceptance (point cloud вҶ’ NURBS fit). LLM tool: `nurbs_max_deviation_to_mesh`. вң…
- **GK-P auto-lightweight** вҖ” Auto-lightweight body (Lyche-MГёrken knot removal + rational simplification) вң… вҖ” `geom/auto_lightweight.py`; `brep_auto_lightweight` LLM tool; 4 hermetic oracle tests.
- **NURBS-CURVE-CIRCLE-FIT** вң… вҖ” fit a circle to a 2D NurbsCurve by least-squares (Kasa 1976 + Taubin 1991); reports center, radius, RMS and max residual; `nurbs_fit_circle_to_curve` LLM tool wired. Caveats: 2D only вҖ” for 3D space curves project onto a plane first; short arcs (< 30В°) prefer Taubin. Ref: Taubin (1991) IEEE TPAMI 13(11):1115вҖ“1138; Kasa (1976) IEEE TIM 25(1):8вҖ“14.
- **NURBS-CURVE-LINE-FIT** вң… вҖ” fit a straight line to a 2D NurbsCurve via total-least-squares (TLS) / SVD; `LineFitResult(origin_xy, direction_xy, rms_residual_mm, max_residual_mm, is_planar_line, honest_caveat)`; `fit_line_to_curve` + `nurbs_fit_line_to_curve` LLM tool wired; 35 hermetic tests. Algorithm: centroid subtraction + thin SVD; principal right-singular vector = least-squares line direction; perpendicular residuals computed orthogonally. Use cases: linear-segment detection in imported STEP/IGES profiles, snap-to-line in 2D sketcher, near-straight edge classification. HONEST: 2D only вҖ” for 3D space curves project onto a plane first; for 3D principal-axis fit use 3D SVD separately; direction is undirected (unit vector, sign-canonicalised); sampling is parameter-uniform, not arc-length-uniform. Refs: Press В§15.7 (TLS); Lawson-Hanson В§6 (SVD geometric fitting). `geom/curve_line_fit.py`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-CONIC-DETECT** вң… вҖ” `detect_conic_type(curve_or_points, num_samples=100, residual_threshold_mm=0.01)` returns `ConicDetectResult(conic_type, conic_coefficients, eccentricity, rms_residual_mm, honest_caveat)`; classifies a 2-D NurbsCurve or raw point set as one of: `circle` | `ellipse` | `parabola` | `hyperbola` | `line` | `free_form`. Algorithm: (1) sample `num_samples` 2-D points; (2) line gate вҖ” if TLS perpendicular-distance RMS < `residual_threshold_mm` вҶ’ `"line"`; (3) fit the general conic AxВІ+Bxy+CyВІ+Dx+Ey+F=0 via SVD null-space (smallest right-singular vector), normalised so Frobenius norm of the quadratic block [[A, B/2],[B/2, C]] = 1; (4) if RMS pseudo-geometric residual > `residual_threshold_mm` вҶ’ `"free_form"`; (5) classify by discriminant О” = BВІвҲ’4AC: О” < вҲ’Оө вҶ’ ellipse-family (circle if additionally |B| < Оө_c and |AвҲ’C| < Оө_cВ·max(|A|,|C|)), |О”| вүӨ Оө вҶ’ parabola, О” > Оө вҶ’ hyperbola. Eccentricity: 0 for circle, sqrt(1вҲ’bВІ/aВІ) for ellipse, 1 for parabola, sqrt(1+bВІ/aВІ) for hyperbola (axes extracted from 3Г—3 homogeneous conic matrix eigendecomposition). LLM tool `nurbs_detect_conic_type` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 32 hermetic tests (circle r=1, circle r=5, ellipse a=3/b=1 eвүҲ0.9428, parabola y=xВІ/2, horizontal line, tilted line, sinusoid free_form, random free_form, rectangular hyperbola xy=1, coefficient round-trip, raw-point array, threshold gate, degenerate < 5 points). **HONEST CAVEATS**: (1) Algebraic least-squares fit is biased by gradient magnitude вҖ” for production-quality circle detection use Pratt (1987) or Taubin (1991) in `curve_circle_fit.py`. (2) Parabola detection via discriminant thresholding is fragile near the parabolic boundary for noisy data вҖ” the О”=0 locus is a measure-zero set. (3) The `rms_residual_mm` is a *pseudo-geometric* residual (algebraic value / gradient magnitude), not the true Euclidean distance to the conic. (4) Line detection uses TLS perpendicular RMS exclusively (degenerate conic Bxy+Dx+Ey+F=0 has nonzero quadratic-block norm, so a separate geometric test is needed). Refs: Pratt, V. (1987) "Direct least-squares fitting of algebraic surfaces." SIGGRAPH В§3; Fitzgibbon, A., Pilu, M., & Fisher, R.B. (1999) "Direct least-square fitting of ellipses." IEEE TPAMI 21(5):476вҖ“480. `geom/curve_conic_detect.py`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`.
- **BREP-EDGE-FACE-NORMAL-FLIP** вң… вҖ” detect and fix B-rep faces whose outward normals are inconsistently oriented (some inverted) via iterative neighbour-consensus BFS voting. `FaceNormalFlipResult` dataclass: `face_normals_after`, `num_faces_flipped`, `flipped_face_indices`, `consensus_score`, `honest_caveat`. `detect_and_flip_face_normals(faces_with_normals, max_iter=10, threshold=0.15)`: for each BFS edge (AвҶ’B), if dot(n_A, n_B) < -threshold (anti-parallel, indicating face B is inverted relative to the expected co-oriented outward direction of a convex surface) вҶ’ flip face B. Iterates until convergence. LLM tool `brep_detect_and_flip_face_normals` registered in `plugin.py`. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 16 hermetic tests. **Honest caveats**: (1) PERPENDICULAR-FACE LIMITATION вҖ” adjacent faces with orthogonal normals (|dot|вүӨthreshold, e.g. unit cube) produce no flip signal; a cube cannot be corrected from normals alone. (2) Algorithm assumes CONVEX surface convention (adjacent outward normals co-oriented, dot>0); NOT valid for concave surfaces or open flat meshes where inversion produces co-oriented pairs. (3) Isolated faces (no neighbour_face_indices) are returned unchanged. (4) Absolute orientation is seeded from the first face per connected component вҖ” all-inward input is internally consistent but absolutely wrong. (5) Not a geometric B-rep heal: does not recompute normals from surface derivatives; for production use OCCT BRepLib::OrientClosedSolid. Refs: Mantyla В§6.4; Hoffmann В§3; Weiler 1985 В§3. `geom/face_normal_flip.py`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`.
- **T-100 FEM depth** вҖ” explicit dynamics (module exists, not yet imported/registered); full nonlinear static (only 1-D bar/truss shipped); k-Оө turbulence CFD; coupled FEA-based variation analysis. (Acoustics FEM, EM, harmonic, buckling, PSD, multi-axial fatigue are now shipped.)
- **T-101 CFD depth** вҖ” RANS turbulence models; 3-D unstructured meshing; OpenFOAM bridge.
- ~~**AFR topology ordering**~~ вҖ” вң… shipped: `afr_to_dag` + `.feature` emitter + `afr_to_parametric` LLM tool in `kerf-cad-core/afr/dag.py`.
- **T-101 CFD depth** вҖ” k-Оө RANS shipped (T-101-A вң…); 3-D unstructured meshing (T-101-B, 4L); OpenFOAM bridge depth (T-101-C, 4M).
- **T-100 FEM depth** вҖ” explicit dynamics (module exists, not yet imported/registered); full nonlinear static (only 1-D bar/truss shipped); k-Оө turbulence CFD; coupled FEA-based variation analysis. (Acoustics FEM, EM, harmonic, buckling, PSD, multi-axial fatigue are now shipped.)

- **T-100 FEM depth** вҖ” explicit dynamics (module exists, not yet imported/registered); full nonlinear static (only 1-D bar/truss shipped); k-Оө turbulence CFD; coupled FEA-based variation analysis. (Acoustics FEM, EM, harmonic, buckling, PSD, multi-axial fatigue are now shipped.)

## Deliberately not building

This list is only AI-redundant *authoring/UX interaction paradigms* вҖ” not skipped domains or correctness features.

| Not building | Why |
|---|---|
| Visual node programming (Grasshopper / Dynamo / Sverchok) | The LLM writing a parametric script *is* the graph. `.script.py` + SDKs + JSCAD + `.graph` cover the value. |
| Ribbon / toolbar maximalism | The LLM is the command palette вҖ” discovery is a chat sentence, not a menu hunt. |
| Macro recorders / scripting-GUI builders | The LLM is the macro author; it writes `.script.py` directly. |
| Gumball / direct-modeling maximalism | Keep a basic gumball; the LLM edits the feature tree. |
| In-app wizards / tutorials / onboarding tours | The chat is the wizard вҖ” context-specific guidance on demand. |

---

## How to contribute

Pick a task from [`tasks.md`](./tasks.md) (sized for a single isolated agent run), or open an issue proposing a new long-tail sector line. The roadmap states *why* and *in what order*; `tasks.md` is the *how*. Keep them in sync: when a priority moves here, move the corresponding tasks there.
